niṣphalāya vai pṛ  ataḥ arhatva prāpnuvanto yathā śrāvakayāninaḥ  dīpo yathā nirvṛtimabhyupeto naivāvani gacchati nāntarikṣam diśa na kācid vidiśa na kācit snehakṣayāt kevalameti śāntim eva kṛtī nirvṛtimabhyupeto naivāvani gaccati nāntarikṣam diśa na cācid vidiśa na kācit kleśakṣayāt kevalameti śāntim saundarananda ma itthantatparamaśāntanirodhāvasthā manyantemahāyāninaśca tanneārthamāmananti yathā ca saddharmapuṇḍarīke  tathaiva śrāvakāḥ sarve prāptanirvāṇasajñitaḥ jinotha deśayettasmai viśrāmoya na nirvṛtiḥ  upāya eṣa buddhānā vadanti yadima nayam sarvajñatvamṛte nāsti nirvāṇa tatsamārabha  eva śrāvakayānibhiryat paramapadamavagamyate taccarama lakṣya nāstiviśrāmasthitimātram atastathāgatena tannirodhādupari mahābodhaye preryate punastatraivokta yat sarvajñatājñānaṣaṭpāramitāśūnyatānimittatāpraṇidhānādīni tvayā sādhagīyāni punastatraiva  tryadhvajñānamananta ca ṣaṭ ca pāramitāḥ śubhāḥ śūnyatāmanimitta ca praṇidhānavivarjitam  ataḥ śrāvakāḥ arhataḥ nirodhasamāpatyā jñānakāyasyaavidyāvāsanāyā anāsravakarmaṇaḥ mṛtyusakramaṇasya ca balena nava janma gṛhītvā mahāyāna praviśya buddhatva labhante mahāyāne kena pathā praveṣṭavyamasmin viṣaye taibbatācāryāṇā matāni nimnāni   sabhāramārgeṇa praveṣṭumuktiḥ keṣācid viduṣām teṣāmāśayaḥ  buddhatvāvāptyai mahāyānasya sabhārādipañcamārgānugamanamāvaśyakam  apare ācāryā vadanti  arhaddvārā kleśāvaraṇasya samūlanāśena sasāre punarjanma na grahītavya bhavati ataḥ sukhāvatīprabhṛtibuddhakṣetre sabhūya tata eva kramaśaḥ bodhisattvasādhanāmanuśīlya buddhatva labhyeta   aparairācāryairarhaddvārā kleśāvarasya kṣayena mahāyāne prathamapramuditābhūmi praviśya bhāvanāmārgeṇa jñeyāvaraṇānā kramaśaḥ kṣayena  buddhatvāvāptiḥ svīkriyate   anye ācāryāḥ bodhisattveṣu saptamabhūmiparyanta kleśāvaraṇasya sūkṣmavāsanayāarhadbhibhasteṣā samūlanāśena bodhisattvānā saptamabhūmitaḥ praveśamāmananti etanmatamatāntarāṇā vistāro bhoṭavidvadbhirmadhyamakāvatāraprathamaparicchede vyadhāyiyatra ca dūragamābhūmeḥ prāptyanantara bodhisattvaiḥ prajñayā śrāvakāṇāmākarṣakatvaprasaṅgaḥ carcitosti mahāyāniṣvapi keṣācid viduṣā matamidam  pāramitānayenāpi ante mantranayaḥ vajrayānamāśrayaṇīyo bhavatinānyathāālokālokābhāsālokopalabdhisamāvaraṇāni pariśudhyanti samyaksambodhiprāptirapyaśakyā yadyapi etannayadvaya mahāyāne eva sammilitam yathā cādvayavajrasagrahe  mahāyāna ca dvividha pāramitānayo mantranayaśceti pṛ adhunāvalokanīya pāramitānayamantranayayoścāntara kim ki ca tattatvam yadabhāve pāramitāyānibhiścāpi mantrayānavajrayānayorāśrayamādāyaiva lakṣyaprāptirvidhīyate etadvicāravimarśena nayadvayasya sādhanāpakṣaḥ kīdṛśaḥ tadapi suspaṣṭa bhaviṣyati  ubhayanayāntara spaṣṭayatā bhoṭadeśasya mahāsiddhācāryasumatikīrticoṅkhāpāmahodayena mahāmantrakrame pratyapādi   nayadvayasya caramalakṣya ataḥ abhisamayālaṅkārasya  etaduktimanusṛtya ubhaya prāṇimātrahitāya bodhitattvabhīpsati ato bodhicittadvasya bhedarekhā svīkartumaśakyā  sarvadharmāṇā nisvabhāvatāyāḥ svīkṛtyā śūnyatāyāmapi bhedāsattvena śūnyatāpi tadubhayasya bhedarekhā bhavitumaśakyā  ubhayanaye ṣaṭpāramitānā caryānuśīlanenāpi sīmārekhā kartumaśakyā  pātreṣu mṛdumadhyādhimātrakramamādhārīkṛtya bhedaḥ kartumaśakyaḥ yato hīmau bhedāvubhayanaye sambhāvyete   pāramitānayo rāgarahitānā tantranayaśca rāgayuktānā pātrāṇāmanugrahāyopadiṣṭaḥ ityapi mantumaśakya yato hi pāramitānayepi eva niyamosti yathā ca bodhicaryāvatāraḥ  eva buddhvā parārtheṣu bhavet satatamutthitaḥ niṣiddhamapyanujñāta kṛpālorarthadarśinaḥ  etadatiricya pāramitānayānupālakā bahavo gṛhasthā api bhavitu śaknuvanti naitadevabrāhmaṇaputro bhikṣunakṣatropi upāyakauśalena prāṇikalyāṇāya maithunamakārṣīt eva vidhā naikā kathāḥ sūtragrantheṣūpalabhyante tatraiva mantranayepi īdṛśā aneke mahāpuruṣāḥ ye bhikṣavaḥ eva nāpi tu siddhapuruṣā apyāsan atra vicāraṇīya hi tantre rāgamārgīkaraṇa vivecita para pāramitānaye rāgādīni prāṇinā hitāyoktāni etannayadvaye mahadidamantara vidyateyacca vicāraṇīyamāste  mahāsukha sacāryya viṣayaśūnyatāyā dāḍhyārpteḥ sīmā rekhāpi svīkartumaśakyāyataśca pāramitānayepi śamathe dārḍhyaprāptyā prāṇavāyurniyamyateyataḥ kāyapraśrabdhi prāpya kāye sukha sacarate sa ca yatheccha cittaprasrabdhisamāpatyā svaviṣayesthairyya labdhumarhati ata ubhayatra sukhānubhūtyā sīmārekhāṅkana kiyatsabhavamida vicāraṇīya vartate kecit tantre avikāritāyāḥ anakṣarasukhasya ca viṣaye kathayanti pāramitānaye tu sthitiriya praśrabdhikāliko prayāsādinirbharā ca tiṣṭhati  punaścātra mahāsukhābhiprāyaḥ raktaśvetabodhicittasyārdrībhāvatayā nāḍīvāyutilakādīnā prakriyayā samutpannasukhena gṛhyeta tarhi kevalamanuttaratantrasya  vaiśiṣṭyamida syāt kriyādyanyasāmānyatantrāṇā tu na syāt  ittha nayadvayena prāpte lakṣye lopi bhedo nāstitatprāptau mārge ca śūnyatādarśanacittotpādapāramitāsambharaṇādīnā bhedenāntara na kartu pāryate niṣkarṣaḥ para cātra vicāraṇīyamidam  ubhayanayasya mukhyoddeśya parārthavidhānamyadā ca parārthaviṣaye vicintyate tadeda kārya rūpakāyena sabhāvyate dharmakāyena cāsambhāvyam śāstreṣu dharmakāyaprāptiḥ svārthasampatyā rūpakāyasya ca prāptiḥ parārthasampatyābhihitā idamapi satya yat ekasyābhāveparasya prāptirasambhavā śrāvakayānivaibhāṣikasautrāntikāstu buddhasya rūpakāya karmavipāka manyante nirvāṇamapi bhāgadvaye vibhajanti buddhatvaprāptyanantaramapi skandhasantateḥ avicchinnarūpeṇa vidyamānatāvasthā sopadhiśeṣanirvāṇatvena skandhasantateḥ pañcaskandhānānirodhāvasthā nirupadhiśeṣanirvāṇatvena cocyate eva rūpakāyanirodhamanu prāṇinā sākṣāt kalyāṇa na sambhāvyate para mahāyānamate tadāpi te buddhāḥkalyāṇannivṛttāḥ syuratha vā tatparārthasampattiḥ kṣīyeta ityapi nābhimatam śrāvakayānamate buddhopadeśa eva dharmakāyatvena manyate yo hi tannirūpadhiśeṣanirvāṇānantara parārtha sampādayate  yathā ca mahāparinirvāṇāvasthāyām ānandādiśiṣyairmahāparinirvāṇaprāptāvatyantaduḥkhānubhūtau prakaṭitāyā satyā buddhena svīyāntimopadeśarūpeṇāvoci   mayā eva kimapi tathya svajīvane tava  sammukha na gopitam  mattannirāvaraṇacaritrameva tava śāstṛpathapradarśaka cāsti tadeva dharmakāyaḥ tadācaryya svayamātmani jñānadīpa jvālaya bhagavato buddhasya sa upadeśaḥ adya pañcāśaduttarasahasradvayavarṣāntaramapi janasya hṛdayāni satyāhisābodhitattvāni prati prerayati bauddhadharmadarśanādhyayanādhyāpanayoryāvichinnā paramparāsaiva ca tat buddhasyapuṇyasya pariṇāmo vidyate  ittha śrāvakayānimatānusāra buddhena manuṣyarūpeṇa avatīryya prāṇinā pratyakṣakalyāṇavidhāna na sambhāvyate tathāpi pravacanarūpidharmakāyenādyāpi  sa duḥkhamuktyai janān sanmārgamārohayati  śrāvakayāninaḥ rūpakāyena lakṣyaprāpti na manyante buddhasya rūpakāya ca duḥkhasatya manyante  yadyapi śrāvakayānino buddhakāya duḥkhaskandhamāsrava ca svīkurvanti tathāpi tat dvātriśallaṣaṇaiścaturaśītianuvyañjanaiḥ suśobhitamabhimatam hetumārge etat puṇyasabhārasya sacayaphalamabhimanyante yathā sāmānyaprāṇinā surūpatā tatpuṇyakarmaphala manyate sa eva kramo buddhena sahāpi para ca mahāyāninā sthitau vaiparītyamavalokyate  gotravyākhyāprasaṅge vārteya suspaṣṭā yadasminnaye buddho mahāparinirvāṇānantaramapi nirmāṇakāyasabhogakāyayoḥ rūpeṇāvirbhūya satata sattvahita  vidadhāti  atastat prāptiḥ kathaṅkāra śakyeti vicāraṇīyam  idandṛsyate yat prajñāpakṣasya pūrṇataḥ pratipādana pāramitāyānepyasti para ca vineyajanādhyāśayānurūpa yāvad bhavaḥ sthāsyati tāvat prāṇimātrahitena  vidyamānarūpakāyasyopādānakāraka ki syāt  yad dvātriśallakṣaṇaiścaturaśītyanuvyañjanaiśca suśobhitaḥ nirmāṇakāyaḥ akaniṣṭhabhuvane ca sthitaḥ sabhogakāyo vidyate  yathā ca vaya śūnyatājñāpikā prajñā dharmakāyasyopādānakāraṇa mattvā vicāryya tad bhāvayāmaḥ tathaiva rūpakāyasya hetubhūtadevakāyasya  bhāvanāvidhiḥ pāramitānayepi nākathyata  arthāt parārthasiddhidāyakarūpakāyasya mārgīkaraṇavidherbhavanam abhavanam vānayadvayasya sīmārekhāṅkana bhavatu śakyate ittha svīkṛtau satyā punaḥ praśnaḥ  yatphala prāptavyamastikintat sadṛśaphala bhāvyeta yadi bhāvanīyantarhi ki manuṣyajanmane manuṣyarūpa bhāvayitavya tathaiva paśupakṣiparyanta etadvyāptiḥ svīkāryā naivam yataḥ pāramitānayena dānādipuṇyārjanādapi lakṣaṇānuvyañjanāni siddhyanti paramatra cirakālopekṣyate vajrayāne tu phalabhāvanayā rūpakāyaḥ śīghra siddhyati sūtrālaṅkāre sambhogakāyasyaikarūpatva pacasu viniyatatvamupabhogairyuktatva cāmanyata āśrayeṇāśayenāpi karmaṇā te samā matāḥ prakṛtyāsasranenāpi prabandhenaiṣu nityatā  itthamavacchinnatayā sattvānā sammukha prakaṭānāya rūpakāyasyaikovicchinnaḥ āśrayaḥ upādāna ca nūnamapekṣyate atastadarthantatsvarūpabhāvanāyā āvaśyakatva sambhāvyate pāramitānaye dharmakāyaheturhi prajñā rūpakāyahetustu puṇyam yathā āryanāgārjuno ratnāvalyām  buddhānā rūpakāyastu puṇyasabhārato bhavet dharmakāyaḥsamāsena jñānasabhārajo nṛpa  etadanusāreṇa dharmakāyasya hetuḥ jñānasabhāraḥ rūpakāyasya ca hetuḥ puṇyasabhāro vartate prāyaśassvarvepi matamidamāmanantitathāpi pāramitānaye jñānasabhāraḥ avikalarūpeṇa pratipādyate yathā copari nirdiṣṭa darśana catuṣkoṭiniṣprapañcād nānyad sambhavam para ca rūpakāyahetusambhandhaḥ pāramitānaye  yasya yasyātra yo heturlakṣaṇasya prasādhakaḥ tasya tasya prapūryāya samudāgamalakṣaṇaḥ abhisamayālaṅkāraḥ gurūṇāmanuyānādirdṛḍhatā savara prati sagrahasevana dāna praṇītasya ca vastunaḥ abhisamayālaṅkāraḥ eva dvātriśallakṣaṇacaturaśītyaguvyañjanānā heturūpeṇa gurvāgamanapratyudgamanavidhānadānādipāramitānuśīlanañcetyādi varṇitam tatopyagre utkṛṣṭāvasthā prāptu buddhakṣetrasya pariśuddhivyavasthā vyadhīyata yathā cābhisamayālañkāre  sarvasattvamanojñānamabhijñākrīḍana śubhā buddhakṣetrasya niṣpattirbuddhasevāparīkṣaṇe  akṣayajñāna jinakṣetraśuddhirmāyopamā sthitiḥ sañcintya ca bhavādānamida karmāṣṭadhoditam  etad vyākhyāyamāno haribhadrobravīt  eva viśuddhakṣetrasya rūpabhūmiḥ svarṇanirmitā tarupallavādīni ratnajaṭitāni jalādīnyapi aṣṭaguṇairyuktāni atra bodhisattvā devadevīnā rūpeṇa bhāvyante tathā ca sarve dharmā māyopamā manyante  para ca vajrayānimate yāvat sādhako maṇḍalayuktavimānasya trayodaśabhirupabhogavastubhistathā lakṣaṇānulakṣaṇairyuktaphalarūpisambhogakāyasya  mārgāvasthāyāmeva bhāvanā na kurute tāvat dānaśīlādimātreṇa rūpakāyaprāptiraśakyā  prekṣaṇīyamadhunā yad vajrayānasya svarūpakāyasya mārgīkaraṇaprakriyā kā pāramitānayamantranayayorbhedavicārāraṇāyāmida suspaṣṭa devakāyasya prāptyai rūpakāyasya viśiṣṭamupādāna bhavet  yathā hi dharmakāyasyopādānahetubhūtā śūnyatā bhāvyate tathaiva rūpakāyasyopādānāyāpi sūkṣmamantrayānasyārambhaḥ o svabhāvaśuddhāḥ sarvadharmāḥ  svabhāvaśuddhoham tathā ca o śūnyatājñānavajrasvabhāvātmakoham ityetābhyā jāyate   arthāt sarvadharmasvabhāvaśūnyatā bhāvayitvā tacchūnyatābhāvanayā catuṣkoṭiniṣprapañcanijacitena sūkṣmaprāṇacittena vā sāmarasya niṣpadyate yathā dīpadīpālokayoḥ puṣpasya tadūgandhasya ca pārthakyamaśakyamtathaiva cittaprāṇavāyvorapi na pārthakyam parasparamekarasattvam sūkṣmavāyorapi tantreṣu pañcaprabhāmayaprāṇatva kathitam cittasya prabhāsvaratvamadvayasvarūpatva ca tasmādeva devarūpa prakāśate  atra svayam iṣṭadevaḥ saptāvayavayukto vajradharaḥ tadanu ca svabhāvataḥ niṣprapañcasvabhāvaśūnyatā bhāvayitavyā yaddhi vajrayāne utpattikramaniṣpannakramabhāvanayā  sajñitam  arthāt sakṣepataḥ vajrayāne kāyavākcittanāmakatrivajrakāyasvarūpasya samarasatā ekākāratā cittamasti cittameva kāyaḥ vāgeva cittam ityabhimatam guhyasamājatantre  kāyavākcittavajreṇa bhedyābhedyasvabhāvataḥ  nāmasagītāvapi anādinidhano buddha ādibuddho niranvayaḥ jñānaikacakṣuramalo jñānamūrtistathāgataḥ  yāvat buddhasya jñānamasīmita tāvadeva buddhasya rūpamapiyāvat paryanta buddhasya jñāna vyāpta tāvatparyanta kāyasyāpi vyāptiḥ sūkṣmaprāṇānā cittasyāthavā nijacittasya svīkṛti binā sarvasattvānā hitātmaka yaduddeśyamasmākantanna setsyati pāramitāyā sarvadharmasya niḥsvabhāvatvam asyaiva ca pratipādanantatra vidhīyate tasyāmavasthāyām na grāhyo na ca grāhakaḥ ityādivākhyānā sāhāyyena kimapi hastagata na bhavati evamanubhūyate yad vaya kvacit sarvaśūnyākāśe avasthitāḥ smaḥ pratikāryasya pratyayeṣu vicāreṇa itthamanubhūyate yad vaya kutracit śūnyākāśaparyanta prasṛtasya sikatāmayasthalasya registānasyamadhye vartāmahe kimasti  kutrāstikasmādāgataḥkutra gantavyamkva ca sthitaḥki vidheyakimvidheyamityeṣā praśnānā samādhānāni nopalabhyante yadyapi vijñānavādinaḥ advaye mādhyamikāścāpyadvaye viṣayaviṣayyekākāratārūpaśūnyatāyā sthitāḥ para ca vijñānavādinaścittasattāmabhiniveśena sāka svīkurvanti mādhyamikānā pratikṣaṇa tathāgataskandhagatiprabhṛtīnā parīkṣaṇe vyatyeti tathā hi mādhyamikakārikāgatāgataparīkṣāyām gata na gamyate tāvadagata naiva gamyate gatāgatavinirmukta gamyamāna na gamyate   ityetadanusārantu kimapi gamanāgamanādika na budhyate akarmaṇyatā cānubhūyate vā ato mahallakṣyabhūtaparārthahetave divyaśaktijñānacakṣuḥprabhṛtiprāptyartha  catuṣkoṭiniṣprapañca prāṇacitte nijacitte bodhicitte vā mahāmudrāyā sampannacitterthāt ābhāsaśūnyādvayarūpe samāhitirāvaśyikī pratīyate   atrābhāsaśūnyatārthe na jñānaśūnyatāmātram apitu caturthābhiṣekavelāyā saketitaḥ paramārthaprabhāsvaraḥ arthāt eva rūpaḥ saptāvayavairyukto  vajradharaḥ sabhogakāya eva mahāmudrāthavābhāsaśūnyo vartate  vajrayānasyaitadeva darśana sādhanāyāḥ pramukha tattva cāsti vajrayāne svaya devatvenotpādayitṛvidhiṣu bījalakṣaṇāyudhādyālambanāyā bhāvanāyā vibhinnavidhayo vartanteyasmāttantrāṇā kriyācaryāyogānuttarādayo vibhāgā jāyante etadbhāvanāvidhayaḥ paścād vakṣyante vajrayānoktamadvayasvarūpa yadatra vimṛṣṭa tadanuttaratantrasambaddhameva tantrāṇāmeteṣā bhedopadhedāḥ sādhanāpaddhatayaścāgre pratipādayiṣyante vajrayānasādhanāsvarūpam bodhisattvayānasya bhedadvayapāramitānayo guhyamantranayaścārthāt mahāyānasya dhārādvayī vartate advayavajrasagrahepītthameva pratyapādi mantranayasya svarūpābodhanāt pūrvamidamāvaśyaka yattattattvadarśana sādhanāpakṣaśca budhyeta prathamaparicchedetra tattvadarśanaviṣaye sakṣepeṇa varṇitam sādhanāsambandhe pāramitānayasya kiñcid mūlabhūtānyantarāṇi pratipādayiṣyantetra yataḥ sāmānyatantrasādhanāvidhirvivecitaḥ syāt viṣayaśūnyatāyā pāramitānayamantranayayośca kimapyantara nāsti tibbatīyamahāsiddhācāryeṇa śākyapaṇḍitena kathitamśūnyatā niṣprapañcā bhavitu śaknoti niṣprapañcato vyāvṛttā satī śūnyatā sadasatoḥ śāśvato ucchedapakṣe vā patiṣyati  atreda bodhya yatśūnyatā niṣprapañcā tvastyeva para ca yatra śūnyatā niṣprapañcamātra tatraiva mantranaye iya prajñopāyādvayamayī vartate hevajre yathā nāsti bhāvako na bhāvostimantra nāsti na devatā sasthitau mantradevau caniṣprapañcasvabhāvataḥ  sādhanānuśīlanenādvayatattvasthiti svabuddhyanusāra bhagavatyāḥ sādhakaḥ sākṣātkartumīpsati viṣayesmin vistareṇa tantracatuṣṭayasya sādhanāpaddhatau vicārayiṣyate tantracatuṣṭaye vārteyamabhimatā yat pāramitāyānasya caryā sādhanāheyopādeyatādika dhyātvā vidhīyatemantranaye tu viśuddhasamatābhāvanayā sarvadevadevīśca vīravīrāṅganāśca māyopamā matvā nānā pūjārcanā kriyate yatra pāramitānaye śrameṇa śamathaḥ vipaśyanā ca bhāvyate tatra mantranaye upāyakuśalatayā saha sanimittautpattikramaanimittautpannayogadvārā prāṇāyāmena vāyu niyantrya vajrajāpādeḥ saralo vidhiranuṣṭhīyate  pāramitānaye samādhiḥ pṛṣṭhalabdhasthitiśca kramaśaḥ bhāvyate yatra cātrādvayajñānena sarvadharmasamabhāvād yugapad bhāvanayā vividha puṇya  sacīyate   pāramitānaye sādhanādvārā sādhyāptiḥ kāmyate tadatra mantranaye upāyakauśalena sanimittanirnimittayogābhyā prāṇāyāmato vāyu niyantrya vajrajapādeḥ  saralavidhiḥ svīkriyate  pāramitānaye sādhayanā sādhyāptiḥ para ca mantranaye sādhyasvādhanayoradvayatattvataiva tasmādeveda phalayānamucyate pāramitānaye yatra anantakalpaparyanta duṣkara taponuṣṭhīyate tatraiva cāya sādhakaḥ ekāsane eva bodhiprāptimabhilaṣatiprāptumapi śaknoti sāmānyaprāṇinā hitāya pāramitānaye upāyānāmalpataiva mantranaye vṛṣṭividhānam rogaśamana śāntiraudrapuṣṭivaśīkaraṇaprabhṛtividhayaḥ aneke santi ata eva trinayapradīpe mantrayāna pāramitānayāpekṣayā caturvidhavaiśiṣṭyena viśiṣṭamabhihitam yathā   asamohaḥ  upāyabahulatā  aduṣkaracaryā  tīkṣṇendriyatā  asamohaḥ pāramitāsādhakaḥ prāṇikalyāṇāya hastapāda śarīrāṇi ca pradadāti para cāsakhyajanānā hita sādhayitumaśakyametena atra khaḍgājanavṛṣṭiprabhṛtayoneke upāyāssanti yaiśca prāṇihita vidhātu śakyam   upāyabahulatā yatra ca pāramitānaye samayasavaratapasyopavāsaprabhṛtayaḥ naike duṣkaraniyamāstatraivātra tantre nānāśayarucisāmarthyānusāra  śāntaraudrabībhatsabhayānakaprabhṛtyupāyānā sāhāyyamupādātu śakyate   aduṣkaracaryā yatra pāramitānaye kleśāstyājyāstatraiva tantre kleśān nāpahāya bodhaye tad mārgīkaraṇa kriyate yathā ca hevajratantre yena yena hi badhyante jantavo raudrakarmaṇā sopāyena tu tenaiva mucyante bhavabhandhanāt  pañcakramepi yena cittena bālāścasasāre bandhana gatāḥ yoginastena cittenasugatānā gati gatāḥ   tīkṣṇendriyatā advayatattva sa eva jñātu prabhavati yaśca pūrvasaskārayuktaḥ vastusthityavagamane tīvrabuddhiśca syāt yadyapi tīvrabuddheḥ naikeṣu kṣetreṣu svasvapṛthak svarūpa bhavati para cātra vastusatyatāvagamanatīvrataivottamā manyate pāramitāvādinaḥ samagratābhāvaboddhumasamarthāstenaiva naikamārgeṣu prajñopāyādvayatattvasya vivecana nopalabhyate  yatra ca pāramitāsādhakaḥ ṣaṭsu daśasu vā pāramitāsu ekaikā bhāvayati tatraiva tantrasādhakāya sampūrṇabrahmāṇḍamaṇḍala devatādvayabodhicittamāste  tacca sarvamātmasannihitamātmastha ca vidyate svakāya eva nijamaṇḍalamayameva tantrasya sādhanāvidhirasti anaṅgavajrobhidyatte śrīmatā vajrasattvena yepi cānye nidarśitāḥ adhimuktivaśāḥ kecit taiśca ki tattvavedinaḥ  kriyāditantracatuṣṭayasya svarūpam ka yaḥ sādhakaḥ bāhyaśārīrikamudrāvidhānena kāyasiddhi vāgdvārā mantrāvṛtyā vāksiddhi cittena ca devabhāvanāvidhānena cittaguṇāśca prāpnoti  eva cābhyantaradhyānabhāvanāpekṣayā bāhyaśuddhyādiśubhācaraṇāni prabalatayā kurute sa kriyātantravānucyate   seratogapāmahodayena tantracatuṣṭayasvarūpa kramaśaḥ spaṣṭayatoktam upalabhyadevī mudrā vā samālokya rāga samutpādya tadrāgamārgīkaraṇa  kurvat tattvadhyānasthiteḥ prakriyaiva kriyātantrasya svarūpam   kha upalabhyadevyā īkṣaṇena saha hāsādiprakriyā vidadhānaḥ sukhānubhūtyā niṣprapañcasvarūpasya sādhanā vyadadhat kāyavākcaryādiśuddherābhyantaracittayogasya  ca samānarūpeṇa anuśīlakaḥ sādhakaśca caryātantravān nigadyate   ga upalabhyadevyā pāṇigrahaṇa vidhāya sukha sacārayan sukharūpaviṣayajñānāt viṣayaśūnyatāyāḥ sākṣātkāre prayatnaśīlo yogī yogatantravān  ucyate   gha samāpattiyoge sthitvādvayatattva sākṣātkṛtya bāhyapeyāpeyagamyāgamyaśubhāśubhaprabhṛteḥ sampādana binā caryākārakaḥ sādhakonuttaratantravān  kathyate  prajñopāyaviniścayasiddhau anaṅgavajreṇocyate gamyāgamyādisakalpa nātra kuryāt kadācana māyopamādiyogena bhoktavya sarvameva hi  dharmadhātusamudbhūtā na kecit paripanthinaḥ prabhujīta yathākāma nirviśaṅkena cetasā  tibbatasya paravartipaṇḍitadharmaśrīmahodayenāpi nantracatuṣṭasya savara dīkṣā svarūpa pratipādayatāvocidarśanahāsyapāṇyāptiprabhṛtiṣvekasya sukhasya mārgīkaraṇa vidhāya tatsadṛśarāgasya pariśodhanāya viśiṣṭaprajñopāyajñāna  bhāvayitvā dvāratrayasya kāyavākcittarūpasya  vāsanāhetave vikalpabādhakasahetucittasya kriyācaryādikatantrāṇāmabhiṣekātprāptaḥ savaraḥ śīlañca kriyāditantrāṇā savarasvarūpa vartate caturṇāntantrāṇā maṇḍala likhan tathāgataḥ kathayāmāsakriyātantramaṇḍale dakṣiṇatastārādevī rāgamudrāyā vāmataśca dharmadānamudrāyā padmakulasyāmoghapāśa vilokya lekhanīyam kriyātantravajroṣṇīṣepi kathitapitṛdevo mātṛdevī prati mātṛdevī  ca pitṛdeva pratyavekṣate iti śvetavarṇeṣu likhet   vairocanābhisamayatantre caryātantravidhi spaṣṭayatā vyalekhidakṣiṇataḥ buddhaḥlocanasmitamudrāyāmavatiṣṭhate asya nikhila śarīra kāntimayam vāme ca sthitā śākyamuneriya bhāryā yogatantramaṇḍasambandhe vajraśekharaḥ prāvocatvajradevī vajraśabda kurvatī bhagavataḥ hastamāliṅgayantīti dṛṣṭvā likhet anuttaratantramaṇḍale pitara mātara ca yuganaddhasamāpattisvarūpa likhet yataśca samāpattiyogenaivādvayatattva sidhyati tathā ca guhyasamāje tathāgatamahābhāsā locanā vā vibhāvayet dvayendriyasamāpatyā buddhisiddhimavāpnuyāt  etena suspaṣṭa tantracatuṣṭaye sādhakaiḥ rāga mārgīkurvadbhiḥ advayatattva sāksātkartumiṣyate sampuṭatantrepi hāsadarśanapāṇyāptiḥ sa tu tantre vyavasthitaḥ rāgaścaiva virāgaścacarvayitvā ghuṇaḥ sthitaḥ  etadvyākhyāyamāno bustonaḥ lilekhakāmadhātau rāgasya catvāro bhedaḥ trāyastriśasyādhaḥ samāpattidvārāyāme āliṅganenatuṣite pāṇyāpti kṛtvānirmāṇaratau hāsena ca paranirmitavaśavartini mudrādarśanamātreṇa santoṣaḥ sukha cānubhūyate vineyajanaiḥ rūpadhātau kāmadhātoḥ rāgo na bhavati atasteṣā vineyajanānā rūpadhāturāgānmuktyai buddhena pāramitānaya upadiśyate ye sādhakā vairāgyamārgādadamitāstebhyastantramadiśyata etattathāvalokanena tantre ekasya niścitarāgasya mārgīkaraṇa bhavati  para cāsya kṛte niścitameva rūpavatīmudrā sasevya sādhanā nānivāryyā yataśca strīpuruṣayoḥ śukraśoṇitobhayarūpatvāt kāryakāraṇayoḥ santaterekatvācca tantraśāstresmin evam ityasya vyākhyayā suspaṣṭa vihitam anekaṣvartheṣu varṇitam para ca lalanā śoṇitavāhakanāḍī rasanā śukravāhakanāḍī melana madhyamānāḍī ca prajvālya śukrasravaṇa vidhātu śakyam yasya na naike viṣayāstantre samupavarṇitāḥ etasmācca kālpanikenaikena mārgeṇa rāgasya mārgīkaraṇamadvayatattva ca sākṣātkṛta bhavati prathamāvasthāyāmayameva sādhakasya mārgaḥ samucitaḥ pratibhāti  rūpavatīmudrā sasevya samāpatyādvayatattvasya sākṣātkārāyedamaparihārya yat prathama dharmaśūnyatā manomayarūpeṇa yāvad asaṅkucitaḥ san  antaḥ sūkṣmacetanayā jānīyāt śūnyatāyā ca yadā cittasyātmasātkaraṇa bhavet tadaivātisūkṣmaśūnyādvayatattvamahāsukhasya sādhanā vidadhyāt sādhakasyāparipakvatayā etadācaraṇa loke jugupsita bhavatietena ca samāje etatparamadivyamārgasyāvahelanā jāyate sādhakasya paripakvadaśāyā etadācarettu etatsatyatā tathya ca kopi nāvaroddhu śaknoti sādhakaścāścaryakāricamatkārān prakaṭayitumarhati camatkārapradarśanāya vineyajanānāmapātratvamiti kecidanadhikṛtā nigadanti uccapadastho gururapi na darśayati para ca ta eva mudrādika sasevya caryā vidadhati tarhi tepi truṭi vidadhati etattruṭyā tantra prati hīnabhāvo janeṣvajāyatayo hi dharmāvalambinā mahān doṣa iti  kulavicāraḥ sāmānyakulasya sambandhe bhārataratnabhūṣitaḥ pī vī kāṇe mahodayaḥ dharmaśāstrasyetihāse bauddhabauddhetarobhayakulayorvarṇanamakārṣīt bauddhaśāstreṣu mantrayānādatiriktānyamateṣu kulaśabdasya sthāne gotraśabdaḥ prāyujyata pāramitānayaśrāvakayānīyagrantheṣu gotraśadārthe eva tantre kulaśabdasya prayuktatvāt mahāyānottaratantre maitreyanāthaḥ akathayat gotra kula vā tacchaktiḥ yā hi samyaksambodhi prāpayati tenocyatesame jīvā ekasmin dine nūna nirvāṇa labhante sarvajīveṣu gotrasya vidyamānatvāt yathā sambuddhakāyaspharaṇāt tathatāvyatibhedataḥ gotrataśca sadā sarvebuddhagarbhāḥ śarīriṇaḥ ma  gotrāstitva eva jīvo buddho bhavitumarhati nānyathā gotrasya dvau pramukhau bhedau  prakṛtistha gotram paripuṣṭigotra ca yathā gotra tad dvividha jñeya nidhānaphalavṛkṣavat anādiprakṛtistha casamudānītamuttaram ma u  gotra nidhiphalābhyā paripūrṇa vṛkṣasamam prathamamanādiprakṛtitaḥ pariśuddha cāsti yacca gaganākāramāste cittasya yāsau prakṛtiḥ prabhāsvarā na jātu sā dyauriva yāti vikriyām āgantukaiḥ rāgamalādibhistvasā vupaiti sakleśamabhūtakalpajaiḥ ma u  nābhirnirvartayatyena karmakleśāmbusacayaḥ na nirdahatyudīrṇopi mṛtyuvyādhijarānalaḥ ma u  arthādida gotra karmakleśādyabhimukha na bhavatipara cāsya svarūpamāgantukaḥ hetuvikṛta na kartu pārayati idamādita eva gaganavat prabhāsvarasvarūpa yasya ca notpattirna nāśaśca etasminneva tathāgataguṇasthitiḥ pṛthivyā nirmalajalamiva śarīradhāriṣu sthitam nāgarjunaḥ pṛthivyantarhita toya yathā tiṣṭhati nirmalam kleśairantarhita jñāna tathā tiṣṭhati nirmalam prakṛtisthagotrasya prabhāsvarasya cābhimukhībhāva eva pariśuddhatāna tu kāryakāranahetubhya utpattiḥ yathā agniḥśauca yathā vastra malina vividhairmalaiḥ agnimadhye yathā kṣipta dagdha na vastratā se ṭī pṛ  jñānasādhanābhyā yathā yathā sādhakaḥ āgantukakleśān prajahāti tathā tathā tatra prabhāsvarabuṇo vikasati antataḥ sādhanāsādhayu caikībhūtau tathā bhavataḥ yathā śuklapakṣīyaścandraḥ kṛṣṇatvaśuddhyā pūrṇatā prāpnoti mārgagamanaparipuṣṭagotrayorayameva kramaḥ maitreyanāthenāpi śarīriṣu sthitagotrasya guṇān upamayā spaṣṭayatā etatsvarūpa vyāhṛtam jinagarbhavyavasthānamityeva daśadhoditam tatkleśakośagarbhatva punarjñeya nidarśanaiḥ buddhaḥ kupadme madhumakṣikāsu tuṣeṣu sārāṇyaśucau suvarṇam nidhiḥkṣitāvalpaphaleṅkurādi praklennavastreṣu jinātmabhāvaḥ jaghanyanārījaṭhare nṛpatva yathā bhavenmṛtsu ca ratnabimbam āgantukakleśamalāvṛteṣu sattveṣu tadvat sthta eṣa dhātuḥ ma u ta  yathā nirgandhapuṣpe madhumañjaryyantonna aśucau suvarṇam bhūmau nidhiḥ kukhādyena kṛṣiḥ praklinnavastrāveṣṭitamaṇirdevamūrtirvā strīgarbhe cakravartī rājā ca cavatiṣṭhate tathaiva  sattvānāmanādiprabhāsvaracitte tathāgatānā guṇo dhāturūpeṇa tiṣṭhati  sādhanayā tatprakaṭīkaraṇameva paripuṣṭagotramabhidhīyate buddhasyāyameva rūpakāyopi mahāyānottaratantre buddhakāyatrayāvāptirasmād gotradvayānmatā prathamāt prathamaḥ kāyo dvitīyād dvau tu paścimau ma u  prathamagotrāddharmaprāptiḥ dvitīyācca sabhogakāyanirmāṇakāyayośca jāyate kāraṇenānenaiva nirmāṇakāyopi dharmakāyāt prasphuṭita uktaḥ yataḥ sarvaguṇāḥ prathamagotre eva tu tiṣṭhanti prathamagotrasya gaganasamatvāt sarvajīvasyāpi samatvam yathā cākāśadharmadhātoranekatvamaśakyantathaiva prakṛtigotravaiṣamya na bhavati abhisamayālaṅkāre cāpi dharmadhātorasambhedād gotrabhedo na yujyate ādheyadharmabhedāttu tadbhedaḥ parigīyate  āśritadharmabhedena sattvabhedo vidhātu śakyaḥ  yathā suvarṇarajatalauhādīnā kalaśeṣu pārthakya tanmūlya sthāna cāpi pṛthak bhavitu śaknoti para ca tatra sthitākāśadhātau kopi bhedaḥ  na bhavitu śaknoti tathaiva sattvānā svabhāvabhirucīnā kāraṇena śrāvakayāninaḥ pratyekabuddhaḥ bodhisattvāśca kathyante svasāmarthyānurūpa  paramapada prāpyate  prakṛtisthabhedatvādaya bhedo nāstipara ca paripuṣṭagotrasya pūrṇatāpūrṇatābhedenājāyata vaibhāṣikasautrāntikavijñānavādibhiḥ śrāvakārhatvapratyekabuddhatvasamyaksambuddhatva ceti pṛthaksvatantrapadatraya svīkriyate kintu nedamucittam  mahāyāninastu arhatpratyekabuddhākhya viśrāmapadasthalatvena nirdhārayanti yāvat samyaksambodhirna labhyate tāvat nirvāṇa na kathayitu yataśca prathamagotra dvitīyagotra ca candracandrikāsadṛśa vidyate yathā cokta prajñā jñānavimuktīnā dīptispharaṇaśuddhitaḥ abhedataśca sādharmya prabhāraśmyarkamaṇḍalaiḥ ma u ta  gotrasya pariśuddhireva sādhaka sabhāraprayogadarśanabhāvanāśaikṣaṇikākhyapacamārgeṣu vibhajate yathā aśuddhośuddhaśuddhotha suviśuddho yathākramam sattvadhāturiti proktobodhisattvastathāgataḥ  ma u ta  etadaśuddhāvasthā hi sattvadhātuḥ aśuddhaśuddhāvasthā ca bodhisattvasya prathamabhūmito bhāvanāmārgaparyanta pariśuddhāvasthā  tu tathāgatatvam   asmābhiḥ kathayitu śakya yat kleśajñeyāvaraṇasamanvitaḥ pṛghatjanaḥ aśuddhaḥ kleśena sadgrāhyadhāraṇayā ca śuddhaḥ jñeyāvaraṇena aśuddhaḥ  eva ca darśanabhāvanāmārgau śuddhāśuddhau āvaraṇadvayena pūrṇaśuddhastathā bhavati sāratastu vaktu śakyate sādhakaḥ svasvayogatānurūpa sādhanāmanuṣṭhāya paramapada samavāpnoti sādhanāyāḥ śaktiḥ kula gotrañca kula yatra phalantatraiva mārgācaraṇe mārgo heturvāpi vidyate yathā loke kulasantaniragrimodhikārī bhavati tattvatastu kulamevameva yathā ca manuṣyaḥ para ca buddhisatarānusāreṇa naike bhedā vidhātu śakyāḥ  loke eva manuṣyasya buddhau varṇasasthānādibhedena naike bhedā dṛśyante tathaiva tantragrantheṣu vyāvṛttyanusāreṇānekakulavṛttāni carcitāni yathā hi ka sādhakeṣu kleśānā nyūnādhikavāsanayā tantragrantheṣu tattatkleśānā mārgīkaraṇavidhiḥ nyarūpi vajrapañjare buddhenāvocidveṣāmohāhaṅkārarāgamātsaryādigrastajanānanugrahītu dveṣapradhānasādhakāyokṣobhyakulasyamohapradhānāya vairocanakulasya ca rūpa dhārayitvā mayā tanmārgaḥ pratyapādi kha sādhakānā varṇānurūpa hevajratantre kuladevaḥ eva nyarūpyata yo hi yogī bhavet kṛṣṇaḥakṣobhyastasya devatā yo hi yogī mahāgauro vairocanaḥ kuladevatā yo hi yogī mahāśyāmaḥamoghastasya devatā yo hi yogī mahāpiṅgo ratneśaḥ kuladevatā raktagauro hi yo yogīamitābhaḥ kuladevatā śvetagauro hi yo yogī tasya vajrasattvakula bhavet  ga śarīravartilakṣaṇānusāramapi sādhakaḥ kena kulena sambaddhaḥ kīdṛksaskāranidhiḥida dṛśyate yathā ca hevajre anāmikāmūle yasyastriyā vā puruṣasya vā navaśūka bhaved vajramakṣobhyakulamuttamam vairocanasya bhavet cakramamitābhasya paṅkajam ratnasambhavo mahāratna khaḍga karmakulasya ca  buddhistarānusāramapi sādhakaḥ vibhinnakuliko manyate anekākārabuddhitvāt pudgalāḥ pañca samatāḥ ratnacandanapadmāśca puṇḍarīkastathotpalaḥ pradīpodyotanapaṭalam pṛ ghaeva sādhakānā vibhinnāśayasāmarthyānusāramapi kulasyāsakhyā bhedāḥ guhyasamāje cāpi tattva pañcakula proktatrikula guhyamucyate adhidevo rahasya ca parama śatadhā kulam  punaḥ pañcakulānā vistareṇa agaṇitā kulabhedā jāyante hevajratantre cāpi ekameva mahācitta pañcarūpeṇa sasthitam pañcakuleṣu sabhavastatrānekasahasraśaḥ tasmādekasvabhāvosau mahāsukha śaśvatparam pañcatā yāti bhedena rāgādipañcacetasā daśagaṅgānadībālukātulyā ekakuleṣu tathāgatasaṅghāḥ saṅghakuleṣu hyanekakulāniteṣu kuleṣu kulāni śatāni tāni ca lakṣakulāni mahāntikoṭikulāni bahūni bhavanti tatra kuleṣu cāsakhyakulāni paramānandakulodbhavāni  tattvataḥ ekasmin satyapyānantya vistareṇasakṣepatastu kāyavākcitteṣu antataḥ kāyasyaiva cittatvāt cittasyaiva kāyatvācca prabhāsvaro nijacitte mahācitte ca samāviśati idameva gotra kula cāpi sahajasiddhau kula sādhanāpakṣatvenāṅgīkṛtya varṇitam kulāni bhajate loke pañcasakhyākṛtālayam kulasevayā bhavetsiddhiḥsarvakāmapradā śubhā  akṣobhyaścāmitābhaśca ratnasambhavo vairocanaḥ amoghaśca tathā proktāḥ sattvānā siddhihetunā  akṣobhyaprabhṛtikulasādhanayā siddhiravāpyate punastatraivoktakulasevayā bhavetsiddhiḥ samyaksambuddhabhāṣitam phalaprāptyai svasvamārgānuśīlana kulasevārthāt kulācaraṇamucyate etasmād hetoḥ bodhicaryāvatāre bodhicittasya dīkṣāvāptyanantara sādhaka svātmāna buddhakulaprasūta manyateeva ca buddhasya bhāvyuttarādhikāriṇa matvā svadurlabha mānavajīvana dhanya manute yathā adya me saphala janma sulabdho mānuṣo bhavaḥ adya buddhakule jāto buddhaputrosmi sāmpratam   sampuṭodbhavatantre sādhakaḥ abhiṣeka samupalabhya saharṣa svodgārān prakaṭayan vakti prāptābhiṣeko manujaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ praharṣitaḥ vadet sumadhurā vāṇī jagadānandakāriṇīm adya me saphala janmasaphala jīvita ca me adya buddhakule jāto buddhaputrosmi sāmpratam  itthamatra tantrasāmānyasādhanā vicāryya mānavaprakṛtyanurūpa kula nirdhāryya sādhanā vidheyā etadagre adhikāribhedena kriyācaryāditantrasādhanāvidhayo nirūpayiṣyante  dvitīyaḥ paricchedaḥ kriyātantram kriyātantrābhyudayaḥ kriyātantrasya deśanāprasaṅge kathita bhagavāstathāgataḥ śrāvastyā māsatrayāya trāyastriśalloke  dharmopadeśena svamātaram anugrahītu jagāma tata eva yathāsamaya sumeruparvatādisthānamupagatyānekatantraśāstrāṇi dideśapunaśca jambūdvīpa parāvṛtya magadhaśrāvastyādivibhinnasthāneṣu nānāvidhābhirucivineyajanebhyaḥ tantramupadideśa eteṣu ca kriyātantra mañjuśrītantrāvalokiteśvaratantravajrapāṇitantrācalatantravidyādevītantroṣṇīṣatantrākhyeṣu ṣaṭsu bhāgeṣu vyabhāji kramesminneva kriyātantrasyābhyudayastat prādurbhāvaśca nirūpyate  mañjuśriyā sambaddhatantram mañjuśrīmūlakalpasya deśanā tathāgatena śuddhāvāsaloke kṛtāekasmin samaye bhagavān śuddhāvāsopari gaganapratiṣṭhite  acintyasāścaryādbhutabodhisattvasanipātamaṇḍalamāle viharati sma ityādiprakaraṇe vistṛtavivaraṇa draṣṭu śakyate  avalokiteśvaratantram avalokiteśvareṇa sambaddhānyanekāni tantrapustakāni santi teṣu āryāmoghapāśatantra bhagavāstathāgataḥ potalaparvate samupādiśatyaccāvalokiteśvarakṣetramudyate tatraiva cāsakhyabodhisattvaiḥ rūpalokasattvaiśca etadupadeśaḥ alābhi   āryāvalokiteśvarapadmajālamūlatantrarāja bhagavān himālayasya mahāvane āyuṣmadmahākaśyapagayākaśyapaānandakumāraśāriputramaudgalyāyanasubhūtiprabhṛtīn  naikāśca bhikṣūn śrāmaṇerān nāgadevāsurakinnaragandharvādīn samupādiśat   āryāparimitāyurjñānahṛdayanāmadhāraṇī buddho gaṅgātaṭe bhikṣusaghabodhisattvebhya upādiśat  āryāvalokiteśvaraguhyakośaasaṅgacintāmaṇicakrahṛdayanāmadhāraṇī bhagavān bodhisattvebhyaḥ ṛṣiparvate didiśe   āryamukhadeśakavidyāmantrahṛdayanāmadhāraṇī bhagavatā tathāgatena śrāvastyā veṇuvane bhikṣusaghena maitreyādibodhisattvaiśca sāka viharatāvalokiteśvarādiṛṣīṇā  vidyādharādīnā ca nivedanena samupādeśi    āryasamantabhadranāmadhāraṇī rājagirau bhagavatāṣṭasahasrabhikṣusaghenāsakhyabodhisattvaiḥ śuddhāvāsakulasya devaiśca paripūrṇāyā sabhāyā  pravacana vidadhatā avalokiteśvaraistaddhāraṇī deśayitu vinatau samupādiśyata   āryāmodhapāśakalpaḥ bhagavatā potalāparvate avalokiteśvarasya nivedanena deśitaḥ   āryāvalokiteśvaranāmadhāraṇī svayamavalokiteśvareṇa maitrīvaśāt padmacandrasūryāsane ekānanacaturbhujābhirāvirbhūya bodhisattvebhyaḥ samupadiṣṭā  bhagavān svayameva padmāvalokiteśvararūpeṇāvirbhūya vajrāsane vajrapāṇaye sihanādatantramupadidiśe   āryāvalokiteśvarāṣṭaśataka bhagavatā devanāgayakṣagandharvarākṣasāsurakinnaravineyaiśca sāka viharatā brahmādibodhisattvānā samakṣa  desita yatra vibhinnaparyāyeṣu avalokiteśvaraḥ praśasitaḥ  acalatantram  asyāpyaneke upavibhāgāḥ samupalabhyante  eteṣu cāryācalanāmadhāraṇī bhagavatā trāyastriśaloke daśamabhūmivāsibodhisattvasamantabhadrākāśagarbhasarvanīvaraṇaviṣkambhimañjuśrīpāṇyavalokiteśvaramaitreyaprabhṛtibodhisattvaiḥ  sama viharamāṇena maitreyasya nivedanena akāri   āryavighnavināyakadhāraṇī bhagavān śrāvastījetṛvane āyuṣmadratinivedanenopādiśat  śrīvajrabhairava svaya vajrabhairavodiśat  vajrapāṇitantram  bhagavāstathāgata āryavajrapāṇinīlāmbaradharavajrapālanāmakatantra pātālaloke nāgarājānandaupanandabodhisattvavajrapāṇiprabhṛtibhiḥ  saha viharannupādiśat    āryavajrapāṇinīlāmbaratrilokavijayanāmatantra sumeruparvatasya dakṣiṇapradeśe alakāvatyā vajrapāṇisahitānantadevāsurebhyo bodhisattvebhyaśca  tathāgatabhagavatā samupādeśi   nīlāmbaradharavajrapratyakṣatantratrilokavijayasya deśanā vajrapāṇinā vyadhīyata  vajracaṇḍacittaguhyatantra bhagavatā tathāgatenendradevasya nivedanena samupadiṣṭam  śrīvajracaṇḍacittaguhyatantrottaratantra bhagavataḥ vajrapāṇeḥ nivedanena bhagavān samupadiṣṭavān   vajrahṛdayavajrajihvānalanāmadhāraṇī bhagavān śītavajramahāśmaśāne bodhisattvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhadevāsuranaraprabhṛtibhyaḥ samupādiśat   śrīguhyavajrapāṇyabhideśatantra bhagavatā tathāgatena akaniṣṭhabhuvane alakāvatīprāsāde vīreśvare pṛṣṭavati sati praśnottararūpeṇa samupādiśyata  āryalohatuṇḍanāmadhāraṇī bhagavatā indrasya nivedanena magadhe āmravanasya videhaguhāyā viharatā deśanā samapādi  āryamekhalānāmadhāraṇī kapilavastuni nyagrodhodyāne kumārarāhulasya nivedanena upādeśi  āryavajrapāṇihṛdaya bhagavān buddhaḥ śrāvastījaitravane ānandādinā vajrapāṇeḥ ki kulamityādi praśne samupādiśat vidyādevītantram  mahāmāyūrīvidyārājñī bhagavatā tathāgatena anāthapiṇḍakodyāne viharatā deśitā  dīkṣāmādāya śārināmakabhikṣoḥ bhikṣusaghe praveśasya kiñcitkāla eva gataḥ akasmācca sarpeṇa saḥ daṣṭraḥ ta mūrcchita vilokya ānandena bhagavān  niveditastadā prāṇimātrasya vibhinnarogebhyo muktaye vidyārājñīmupādiśyata   mahāmantrānudhāraṇīsūtra bhagavān buddhaḥ śrāvastyā jetṛvane indra trāyastriśadevadikpālayakṣādibhirnivedane kṛte sati samupadideśa  āryamahāpratisarāvidyārājñī bhagavān tathāgato vajraparvate samupadiṣṭavān   āryajayavatīmahāvidyārājñī bhagavatā rājagirividehaparvate nivasatā bhikṣusaghabhikṣuṇīsaghaśrāmaṇerasaghopāsakānā śāsana prati  vighna vilokya prārthanayā svayavajradharacaṇḍarūpeṇāvirbhūya pūrvābhimukhasahasravajrajvālāḥ prasāryya bhūtasamūha tarjayatopādeśi   āryatārābhaṭṭārikānāmakāṣṭaśatakamāryāvalokiteśvaraḥ samupādiśat  sarvatathāgatamātṛtārāviśvakarmabhāvatantra tathāgatabuddhena tuṣitaloke mañjuśrīprabhṛtibodhisattvābhyarthanayā samupadiṣṭam  āryatārāṣṭaghoratāraṇīsūtra bhagavān sumeruparvate devasthāne samupādiśat uṣṇīṣatantram  asyāpyaneke granthāḥ prāpyante eteṣu ca āryamahādaṇḍanāmadhāraṇī bhagavāstathāgataḥ rājagireḥ gṛdhrakūṭe āyuṣmato rāhulabhadrasya prārthanayādiśat   āryasarvaāntarāyikaviśodhinīnāmadhāraṇī bhagavatā tadā samupādeśi yadā rājagireḥ pūrvasmin brāhmaṇanivāsāmravanasya dakṣiṇe ca videhaparvatasya  indrākhyakandarāyā bhagavān viharamāṇa āsīt  sasevakaḥ indrastatropadeśagrahaṇāya samupāgatastasya ca nivedanena bhagavatā dhāraṇīya tasmai samupādiśyata  āryasarvaabhayapradānanāmadhāraṇī cāpi magadhe bhagavatā indrasya vinatyā didiśe   āryabāhuputrapratisāranāmadhāraṇī śrāvastyāmanāthapiṇḍakena rājñā prasenajitena ākramaṇe kṛte sati tadrakṣaṇa katha śakyam iti pṛṣṭe sati  bhagavateya dhāriṇī samupādeśi   śrāvastyanāthapiṇḍakodyāne pañcaśatottarasahasradvaya bhikṣubhiḥ saha yadā bhagavān viharati sma tadānīm ānando grīṣmakāle māsatrayamupoṣatha sampādya ayodhyātaḥ buddhadarśanāya śrāvastīmupajagāma bhagavatā ānandaḥ samabhihitaḥ yadadyataḥ pūrva saptasaptatikoṭimitasamyaksambuddhairapi āryamahādhāraṇī samupadiṣṭā aha ca punaḥ āryamahādhāraṇī tubhyamupadiśāmi  āryabhadrarātrināmasūtra bhagavatā rājagiriveṇuvane bhikṣubhyo didiśe  āryaojaḥpratyaṅgiraṇīsūtra śrāvastyāmānandādibhikṣubhyaḥ samupadiṣṭam  āryajvarapraśamanīnāmadhāraṇī ca bhagavatā rājagireḥ śīlākhyaśmaśāne bhikṣusaghāyopādiśyata  sarvatathāgatoṣṇīṣavijayanāmadhāraṇīkalpasya amitāyurbhagavatā sukhāvatīloke avalokiteśvarasya nivedanenopadeśaḥ samapādi  āryadraviṇavidyārājatantra buddhaḥ śrāvastyā veṇunirmite prakoṣṭhāṅgaṇe viharan ānandādibhyaḥ samupādiśat  kriyātantrasya svarūpam kriyātantrasvarūpa tathāgatena jñānasamuccaye eva pratyāpādi  loke avahelanāvidhātṛcaryāyā bhītaḥ kriyātantrasya  sādhakaḥ bāhyaśuddhi prābalyena vidhatte  asmin jñānasattvasyābhāvaḥ svadehe devakāyasya bhāvanābhāvaḥ ativiśiṣṭedhvani praveśayogyatābhāvo bhavati ataḥ sa doṣakṣayahetave vikalpamāśrayate eva sādhakaḥ kriyātantrāvasthitaḥ samabhidhīyate etadvyākhyāyamānaḥ koṅṭula rinapoche vakti  mandabuddhirjanaḥ  sādhakaḥgambhīrārthād rāgotpannānubhūte bibheti svaya samayadevasya bhāvanāyāmasāmarthyena svadehe devakāyasya bhāvanābhāvo bhavati etadabhāve jñānadevamāhūyātmani sa vilīnatvamapi na kartumarhati sandhyābhāṣayā mudritātiviśiṣṭamārghānukaraṇepi tadasāmarthyam doṣāṇā prahāṇāya vikalpānāśritya snānādikamācaradbhiriṣṭadevasya svāminaḥ rūpeṇātmanaśca sevakasya rūpeṇa bhāvanā vidhāyādhiṣṭhātumiṣyateeva sādhakāḥ kriyātantravantaḥ kathyante ebhirmantrājanādyaṣṭalaukikasiddhīnā svātantryeṇācaraṇābhilāṣeṇa tatprāptyartha mantrāvṛtimanuṣṭhāya sādhanānuṣṭhīyate  seratogapācāryeṇa kriyātantrasya svarūpamittha nyarūpi  kriyācaryātantrayoḥ sādhakāḥ sampūrṇamārga sādhanāsthalasvatatvavidyāmantrāvṛttiagnisthadhvanisthadhvanyantaḥstha  samādhimantrasādhanāpraveśavidhiṣu homābhiṣekākhyeṣu daśasu tattveṣu sagṛhya dhyāna kurvanti  etāni daśa tattvāni bodhyaṅgāni manyante  buddhenānuṣṭhitāyāḥ jñānasamuccayavacanavyākhyāyā udāharaṇa dadatācāryacoṅkhāpāmahodayena vyāhriyatekriyātantrasya vineyajanā ye ca devayoge  ekāgratāyā bibhyati  ativiśiṣṭācaraṇasya lokagarhaṇatvād eva cārtha vidhātumasamarthāḥ eva cotpattijarābhaṅgādidoṣāṇā kāraṇena sarvadharmasatyatā sattvā sādhanā eva vikalponmukhasādhakebhyaḥ eva svaya devabhāvanāyāḥ jñānāveśasya cābhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ na tu kriyātantrasya samagrasādhakebhyaḥ eva viśiṣṭasādhakāḥ ye ca svadehadevabhāvanājñānāveśarāgahāsadarśanādimārgeṇacaraṇe kṣamante teṣā  kṛte samanujñā vidyate  itthamatra kriyāyāḥ sāmānyaviśiṣṭasādhakānā starānurūpa svarūpa svīkṛtamasti  niṣkarṣastu kriyātantrasya tadeva svarūpa yasmin snānādibāhyācaraṇādipavitratām ābhyantaramantrādyāvṛtti prābalyena pratipādya rāgasya staracatuṣṭaye  prathamadarśanāvasthāyāḥ mārgīkaraṇavidhiḥ pratyapādyata  kriyātantrasyāvāntarabhedāḥ kriyātantracaryātantrayoḥ kulasya bhedadvaya vidhīyate yathā   lokottarakulam lokakula ca  lokottarakulam tathāgatakulam lokottarakule tathāgatakulapadmakulavajrakulākhyāni trīṇi kulāni samāhitāni kramaśa etānyuttamamadhyamādhamānyucyante  buddhaguhyena kulatrayābhiprāya spaṣṭayatā kīrtyatetathāgatakule sarvadharmān samyag vijñāyātīte yathā anantā buddhā bodhisattvā abhuvan  tasminneva mārge tadvat pragatya bodhilābhakārakaḥ tathāgatakulasyocyate yathā bhagavān śākyamuniḥ  sarvatathāgatatattvasagrahe cāpi svacittaprativedhādibuddhabodhiryathāvidhi sa eva bhagavān sarvatathāgatakula bhavet tathāgatakula saiva saiva vajrakula smṛtam saiva padmakula śuddha saivokta maṇisatkulam sādhakasya svacittamapi tathāgatānā kāyavākcittasadṛśa vidyate tadyathā vadavagamanameva tathāgatakulam tattvasaṅgrahādyanekatantragrantheṣu o vajrātmakohamcittaprativedha karomi iti varṇitam yaśca a u ma iti tryakṣarasampannaḥ trivajrasadṛśosti tatprativedhavidhānameva tathāgatakulamabhidhīyate etena cāpi sidhyatīda cittatattvameva kulamyanmārgabalena sādhakaḥ tatsākṣātkurute tadeva kulasya sādhakaḥ sa manyate  padmakulam kleśarahitaḥ san ahorātra praharaṣaṭke nissahāyaprāṇino vīkṣya karuṇādravībhūtaḥ san prāṇināmuddhārāya prayatnaśīlaḥ sādhakaḥ padmakulika  udyate  atrāvalokiteśvarastadadhiṣṭhātṛtārādayaḥ kulasyāsya devā devyaśca santi vajrakulam bauddhaśāsanarakṣaka śatrupradharṣaka vajrakulakamucyate yathā hi bodhicittasamantabhadraṣaṭpāramitodbhūta jñānakrameṇa cādhiṣṭhitacaṇḍacaṇḍīprabhṛtika vajrakulika vartate punaśca trikulasyābhyantarabhedā naike santi  yathā ca tathāgatakulasyāṣṭau bhedāḥ santipradhānakulaadhipatikulamātṛkuloṣṇīṣakulakrodhakuladūtadūtīkulabodhisattvakulaśuddhāvāsikakulāni pratyeka kulasya granthānā vivaraṇam  pradhānakule trisamayavyūharājatantrādyaneke granthāḥ  tathāgatādhipatikulasya mukhyo granthaḥ āryamañjuśrīkalpaḥ  mātṛkule mahāmāyūrīvidyārājñīprabhṛtayaḥ granthāḥ  uṣṇīṣakule āryasarvatathāgatasitātapatrā nāma aparājitā pratyaṅgirā mahāvidyārājñīprabhṛtayaḥ granthāḥ  tathāgatakrodhakule viṣayakalpaguhyatantrādyaneke granthāḥ  dūtadūtīkule āryabhadrarātrināma sūtra gaṇyate  tathāgatabodhisattvakule āryamaitreyanāmaaṣṭottaraśatakadhāraṇīsahitā prabhṛtao granthāḥ  tathāgataśuddhāvāsikadevakule āṭānāṭīyasūtranāma mahāsūtrādigranthāḥ eteṣu dhāraṇītaḥ ya granthamanukṛtya sādhakaḥ svasādhanāmabhyasyati saḥ tatkulasyaivocyate padmakulasyābhyantarāḥ pañca bhedā vidhīyante pradhānakulaadhipatikulamātṛkulakrodhakulaājñākārikulāni  pradhānakule āryaaparimitāyurjñānanāma mahāyānasūtrādika gaṇyate  adhipatikule āryāvalokiteśvarapadmajālamūlatantrarājanāmādigranthāḥ  mātṛkule sarvatathāgatamātṛtārā viśvakarmabhavatantranāmādidhāraṇyaḥ naikasūtragranthāśca santi  krodhakule āryāvaloketeśvarahṛdayagrīvādhāraṇīprabhṛtayaḥ granthāḥ samāhṛtāḥ  ājñākārikule āryamahālakṣmīsūtrādyaneke mantrāḥ srotāsi dhāraṇyaśca santi vajrakulasyāpipradhānakulaadhipatikulamātṛkulakrodhakrodhitakuladūtadūtīkulaājñākārikulāni cetyetāni pañca upabhedāḥ  pradhānakule āryasarvakarmāvaraṇaviśodhanīnāmadhāraṇīprabhṛtayo granthāḥ āyānti  adhipatikule āryavajrapātālanāmatantrarājādayaḥ granthāḥ  mātṛkule āryavajrājitānalapramohanīnāmadhāraṇīprabhṛtayaḥ granthāḥ āyānti  krodhakrodhinīkule āryajayavatīnāmamahāvidyārājaḥ  dūtadūtīkulethavā ājñākārikule mahābalanāmamahāyānasūtrādyanekasūtradhāraṇīmantrastotratantragranthāḥ samāyānti atreme bhedāḥ bustona jicaturdaśam eva ca khasaḍubaje sāmānyatantram ji navamamādhārīkṛtya samuṭṭaṅkitāḥ dhīḥ patrikāyāḥ pañcameṅke śrībanārasīlālamohodayena vistṛtaḥ paricayaḥ ādāyi lokakulam lokakulasyābhyantarabhedāstrayaḥ maṇikula pañcakakula puṣṭikulamityākhyamapilokakula ca  maṇikule āryamaṇibhadrānāmadhāraṇī eva ca āryajambhalajalendrayathālabdhakalpanāmaprabhṛtayaḥ granthāḥ samāviṣṭāḥ  pañcakakule āryamekhalānāmadhāraṇī prabhṛtayaḥ  lokakule āryamantrarājamahāśvāsādayaḥ granthāścāyānti eteṣā kulānāmantarbhāvaḥ iṣyetatarhi bhāgatraye kartu śakyate maṇikulasya padmakule puṣṭeḥ pañcakulasya vā vajrakule cāntarbhāvaḥ anye sarve laukikāḥ devāḥ lokakule sammilanti subāhuparipṛcchāṭīkāpiṇḍārthavidhau nirūpitaye etattritayakule na sagṛhyante te tathāgatenādhiṣṭhitā āvirbhūtāśca na manyante tatredamapi kathitayadyapīme laukikadevāḥ svalaukikarūpa sandhāryya loke vicarantipara ca tathāgatena damitāḥ santaḥ samaye tiṣṭhanti tatpālayanti ca ata ete tathāgataulāśritā manyante lokakule brahmagaruḍasūryacandraprabhṛtayaḥ naike devāḥ samāyānti prāyaśaḥ kulaparicayastanmantrairapi kartu śakyate yathā tathāgatakulasya mantrāḥ o namo ratnatrayāyanamo buddhāyanamo dharmāyanamaḥ saghāya ityāditaḥ ārabhyate padmakulasya namaḥ āryaavalokiteśvarāya bodhisattvāya mahāsattvāya mahākāruṇikāya ityādita ārabhyante mantrāḥ vajrakulasya namaścaṇḍapāṇaye mahāsenāpataye ityāditaḥ maṇikulasya mantrāḥ o namo maṇibhadrāya mahāyakṣāsenāpataye ityāditaḥ prārabhyate pañcakasya puṣṭikulasya ca mantrāḥ namaḥ pañcakāyanamo mekhalāyai ityādinā samārabhyante lokakulasya mantrāḥ svādhipateḥ namanena sahārabhyante ataḥ kimapi suniścita nirdhāraṇamaśakyam kulabhedasya prayojanam yathā vidyāyāḥ sarasvatī dhanamagalādeśca kuberagaṇeśau devau manyete tathaivātra prādhānyena śāntikarmasiddhyai tathāgatakula puṣṭikarmasiddhyartha padmakula raudrakarmaṇaḥ  tvaritasiddhyai ca vajrakulamabhimanyate  tathāgatakulena puṣṭiraudrakarmābhilāṣiṇā pātrāṇāśca punarābhyantarabhedā vidhīyante yathā ca tathāgatasya mukhyakula śāntikarmasiddhyarthatathāgatādhipatikula puṣṭyartha krodhakula ca raudrakarmasādhanāyai upayuktammanyate tathaiva padmakulavajrakulādīnyapyavagantavyāni kriyātantrasya sādhanāpaddhatiḥ kriyātantrasādhanāyāścatvāryaṅgāni caryānāmnāpyucyante etannāmānipraveśacaryāyogacaryāsādhanacaryāsiddhicaryāḥ praveśacaryā kriyātantre praveśāya jalapaṭākhyābhiṣekayorāvaśyakatvamapekṣyate kalaśābhiṣekaprāptyā sādhakaḥ dharmakāyaprāptibhāg bhavati paṭābhiṣekeṇa ca sambhogakāyasya prāptibhāg jāyate  jalābhiṣeke bāhyamaṇḍalānā praveśārtha kalaśābhiṣekeṇa dvitīyamaṇḍale praveśāya sarvadevakalaśābhiṣekeṇa tṛtīye śrāvakapratyekabuddhakalaśena  caturthebodhisattvakalaśena pañcame buddhakalaśena jinavijayakalasyaica jalābhiṣekonuṣṭhīyate  sādhakaśirasi hastamudrādinā paṭābhiṣeko vidhīyate ittha kriyātantrasya pramukhābhiṣekadvayaprāptyā sāka svasvasamayasavara pālayet  tenaiva saha kriyātantrasya vibhinnāmnāyānusāreṇa vajrācāryatvaprāptyai jalapaṭābhiṣekau vidyāmantrasya ca siddhyai yasmin deve sādhakasya  puṣpa patet taddevasya mantrajapāya mantravyākaraṇamāvaśyakam  sādhakasya sādhanāvasare samāgatavighnebhyo rakṣaṇāya snānābhiṣekaḥ aiśvaryasya cābhivṛddhyartha aṣṭamāṅgalikadravyāṇāmabhiṣekaḥ pradīyateyadyapīda jalapaṭābhiṣakayoḥ nihitamastitathāpi vineyajanārhatā vīkṣya vistārāya eva vidhānamapyapekṣyate kuleṣvapi tathāgatakulābhiṣekaprāptyā sarvapradhānakulādhipatīnā kulābhiṣekopi prāpta iva mantu śakyatetathaiva ca padmakula vajrakula cāpi mantavyam kriyātantre abhiṣekārtha mṛṇmayamaṇḍalasyaiva vyavasthāsti cittamaṇḍaladehamaṇḍalādīnā v yavasthā tatra na vartate yogacaryā etadbheddvayamgauṇaprayogacaryā mukhyaprayogacaryā ca   kriyātantriṇā yaḥ devaḥ sādhyastasya paṭacitra mūrti sahāyakadravya ca prati samarpitabhāvanayā samucitadeśaparvatakandarādisādhanāstāneṣu  vasantartuuṣaḥkālaprabhṛtibhirdaśabhiraṅgaiḥ paripūryya sādhanā prārambhaṇīyā  gauṇeya prayogacaryā  pramukhaprayogacaryāyāḥ catvāryaṅgānisvatattvabhāvanā devatattvabhāvanājapabhāvanā dhyānatattvabhāvanā caitāni santi  svatattvabhāvanā tantre praveśāyābhiṣekāvāptyanantarameva tantrasādhanādhikārī jāyate sādhakaḥ anyathā tantrasādhanā niṣphalā bhavati kriyātantre kalaśābhiṣekaprāptyanantara sādhako dharmakāyasya prāptibhāg bhavati sa dharmakāyasya hetubhūtajñānapuṇyasabhārābhyā ṣaḍdharmairyukta svatattva śūnyatā bhāvayati ṣaḍdharmayuktaśūnyatābhāvanāvadhau pūrva sādhakena snānādika vidhāya śuddhena bhāvyam tataśca svarakṣāyai rakṣācakra bhāvayet tadanu sveṣṭadevamāhūya svasammukha sasthāpitapaṭe citre mūrtau vā tatpratiṣṭhāpya tatpūjā vidheyā tataḥ param iṣṭadevasadṛśamāsana vidhāya dharmakāyaprāptimārge ṣaḍdharmayuktacatuṣṭkoṭiniṣprapañcaprabhāsvare stheyam ṣaḍdharmāśca grāhyagrāhakādīnā vikalpānāmabhāvaḥ nirvikalpasya nirābhāsatā sūkṣmāṇvādirūpābhāvaḥ sarvanimittābhāvaḥ sarvavikalparahitā śūnyatāyā ca aprasajyā satī prabhāsvarā svasvabhāvapratisavedyasamādhiśca ite ṣaḍdharmā eva dharmakāyasya prāptimārgāḥ santi  devatattvabhāvanā devatattva rūpakāyaprāptimārgaḥ ucyate etasya ṣaḍbhedāḥyathāśūnyadevaḥakṣaradevaḥdhvanidevaḥrūpadevaḥmudrādevaḥnimittadevaśca ka śūnyadevaḥ tattvadevaḥsvacitteṣṭaparamārthābhinnabodhicitta svabhāvaśūnyamiti pratipādya tadavasthitireva devatattvabhāvanocyate  kha akṣaradevaḥsādhakena yaḥ iṣṭadevaḥ bhāvanīyastatpūrva svaśarīra śūnyākāśe parivartya svacittacandramaṇḍale pariṇata vicintanīyam  tatsvacittacandramaṇḍale tanmantrabīja nyasya tadekībhūya sthitirevākṣaradevasya bhāvanā vyāhriyate  ga dhvanidevaḥsvacittacandramaṇḍalasya madhye sahasā mantrabījād dhvanirguñjatiiti mattvā tatra samāhitireva dhvanidevabhāvanābhidhīyate  gha rūpadevaḥ nabhomaṇḍale svacitta candramaṇḍalasadṛśa bhāvayitvā tanmadhye yasyeṣṭadevasya mantrabījasya nyāsena akṣaradevadhvanidevayorbhāvanāvidhinā  cittasyaikāgryamabhūt tadbījamantrāt pañcaraśmipujaḥ sphuritaḥ san tanmin ārādhyadevyaḥ daśāśāsu virājitabuddhasya bodhisattvānā ca pūjārcana  kurvanti ityeva cintanīyam  tadanu prakāśapuñjonarakapretatiryagmanuṣyaprabhṛtiṣaḍyoniparyanta prasṛtya nikhilaprāṇinā pāpān kṣiptvā puṇyasabhāreṇa tatparipūrṇatā eva paunaḥ punya gambhīratayā vicāraṇīyam tadanubījamantra sveṣṭadeve pariṇata vicintya ekāgratā kuryāt ṅa mudrādevaḥ hastamudrayā svoṣṇīṣalalāṭakaṇṭhādiṣu spṛṣṭeṣu satsu svaya samayamudrayādhiṣṭhito bhaveteva bhāvanāvidhānameva mudrādevasya bhāvanocyate  ca nimittadevaḥ sādhakaḥ yamiṣṭadeva svacittamaṇḍalabhinna mattvā samāhitavān tata upari pṛṣṭhabhūmau sarvabhājana sattvalokaśca śuddhābhāsaḥ arthāt sveṣṭadevasya sthāna kāyasāmagrī cāsti eva bhāvanā nimittadevasya bhāvanā samabhidhīyate sādhakena bhāvanāyā dakṣatāprāptyai prāṇāyāmaḥ abhyasyate prāṇāyāmaśabdaḥ yadyapyanuttaratantre kriyātantre copalabhyate para ca vidhestu bhinnatvameva yathā guhyasamāje prāṇavāyurastiapāna ca tad yat prāṇebhyaḥ dīrghatva pradadāti ataḥ prāṇāpānabandhanam tadavarodhaśca prāṇāyāmaḥ vartate kālacakre lalanāyā rasanāyā ca caladvāyumavarudhya tanmadhyamāyā praveśasya prayāsa eva prāṇāyāma ucyate atra prāṇāpānayoḥ śvāsapraśvāsayoḥ niyantraṇa sasthāpya tatra vikalpodbhavāvarodho vidhātavyaḥ tadā tadbāhyagatireva rudhyate tadābhyantarabhāgaḥ śuddhyati iṣṭadevābhāsaḥ prakaṭībhavati prāṇāyāmavidhānakālasyāpi tantranaye pārthakyameva  anuttaratantre niṣpannakramasya bhāvanākāle eva prāṇāyāmabhāvanā kriyate nānyasyāmavasthāyām atra nimittadevasya bhāvanāyā prāṇāyāmo vidhīyate prāṇāyāmaprayojanānyapi pṛthak santi anuttaratantre vāyumadhūtyā praveśayitu prāṇāyāmo vidhīyate atra kriyātantre tu kevala vikalpāvarodhāyeda sampādyate vikalpabandhanād devatābhāsaḥ suspaṣṭa prakaṭībhavati prāṇāyāmavidhau cāpi bhedaḥ anuttaratantrevasthitoṣṇīṣacakrasthitasya pitṛlabdhaśukrasya nābhicakrasthitamātṛlabdhaśoṇitasya cordhvādhogatibhyāmutpannamahāsukhasya cānubhūtyā  mahāśūnyatā sākṣātkriyate  atra vikalpānavarodhya devabhāvanām ekāgracittena gṛhītvā ālambane sthitvā devābhāsodbhavāya cittavṛtteraikya vidhīyate  japabhāvanā japasya dvau vidhīkapūrvakarma khapradhānabhāvanā  ka dhyānottaratantrasya vyākhyānusāreṇa snānādinā pavitrībhūya svasamakṣamiṣṭadevamāvāhya
