nirvikalpasvatattve samāhitaḥ syāt viśrāmakālamatiricya svasamakṣam iṣṭadevālambane tāvat ekāgramanāḥ tiṣṭhet yāvacca devātmanorabhinnānubhūtirna bhavet kriyātantresmin svadehe iṣṭadevābhāvammanyamānānā paddhatyanusāra mantrajapavidhirayamasti  yairvidvadbhiḥ kriyātantre svadehe devakāyasya bhāvanāvidhiḥ svīkriyate tairūpari varṇitāṅgatrayayuktairbhūtvā svayamapi iṣṭadeve bhāvayitvā  prāṇāyāmakāle śvāsāvadhau nijahṛdayasthāśrayāśritabījamantrādika sarva prabhāmaya jātam eva vicintya navadvārāṇi pidhāya mantrabīje manaḥ  pravartya japonuṣṭhīyate  śvāsamuktyavadhau praśvāsaḥ svasamakṣa bahiḥ sthiteṣṭadevasya maṇḍale praviṣṭaḥ eva bhāvyate  dhyānatattvasya bhāvanā dhyānatattva bhāvanāyāḥ trayo bhedāḥ  ka agnistham  dhyānam  kha dhvanistham  dhyānam  ga dhvanyantaḥ stham  dhyānam  ka agnisthadhyānam  svasammukha bhāviteṣṭadevasya hṛdayacandramaṇḍalasya madhye caturdik dīpaśikheva atyanta śāntamavacchinna bījākṣaraiti vicārya prāṇāpānau niyamya yathāsādhya śvāsamavarodhya ālambane cittaikāgyrameva agnisthadhyānamucyate etena śāntikarmādisiddhau sāhāyyamupalabhyate   kha  dhvanisthadhyānam iṣṭadeva hṛdayakamalacandramaṇḍale caturdik agnipuñjena sama bījamantramalaṅkṛtameva kiñcitkṣaṇa manaḥ pravartya  paśyet  tataḥ kramaśaḥ bījākṣaralopaḥ tataśca tasmānmantradhvanirūtpadyateeva bhāvayitvā pūrvavat prāṇāyāma kṛtvā ekāgratva kuryāt atra prāṇāyāmābhiprāyaḥ  sarvacchidreṣu praviṣṭo vāyuḥ prāṇākhyastathā tato nirgato vāyurapānākhyorthāt śvāsapraśvāsākhyau vāyūtanniyamya sahasā candramaṇḍalād utpadyamānaghaṇṭādhvani sama mantradhvanisthitireva dhvanistha dhyāna nigadyate   ga  dhvanyantaḥ stha dhyānam  etadadhyānasthityā śabdamantradhvanau vicāryamāṇe sati utpattisthitibhaganirodhavirahite nirvikalpasvatattve  samāhitattve sati adhiprajñākhya jñānamutpadyate yacca mokṣasarvajñatayorūpādāna bhavati  varṇitoya sādhanāvidhiḥ prāmukhyeṇa buddhaguhyaviracitadhyānottaratantraṭīkāmādhārīkṛtya nyarūpi  sādhanācaryā subāhuparipṛcchāsūtre varṇita yad vidhipūrvaka mantrajapānantara yadi mantrasiddhiḥ cikīrṣyeta tarhi tena sādhanāsiddhicaryā  vidheyā  atreda dhyeya mantrasādhako yadi bodhicittotpādābhāve mantrajapasakhyā pūrayet tarhi sa śrāvakayāniprabhṛtīnā fala tu lapsyatepara ca tena vajradharapada nāvāpsyate ato mantrayānine bodhicittotpādanamanivāryya bhavati kriyātantrasādhakaḥ kulānusāra trividhā siddhimāpadyate tathāgatakulāt śāntikarmapadyakulāt śreṣṭhakarma vajrakulācca tena raudrakarma prāpyate punaśca kulānāmāntarikabhedena pradhānakulāt śāntiḥ adhipatikulāt puṣṭiḥ krodhakrodhinīkulāt raudrakarma siddhyati  svarūpagataḥ kriyātantrī trividhasiddhimavāpnotiuttamaḥ kriyātantrī vidyādharapada madhyamaśca abhijñādipañcajñānāni kaniṣṭhaśca kriyātantrī  sarvaśāstrāṇā sūkṣmajñāna laghimādika  rasa rasāyanatvaritagamanavaśīkaraṇamāraṇādikṣudrasiddhi ca prāpnoti  āśrayādisiddhyanusāreṇa kriyātantriṇaḥ kramaśaḥ kāyasiddhidravyasiddhisabhogasiddhīnā bhāgino bhavanti etat siddhi prāptyai mantrajapasakhyāpūrto satyāmeva sādhanācaryā vidhātavyā nānyathā sādhanācaryāyā niyamadvayam sāmānyasādhanāyā kālatraye sveṣṭadevasya savidhi pūjārcanāpāpadeśanābhyarthanāpariṇāmanādika sampādanīyam sūtrānta ca paṭhanīyam eva sādhanāyā svasamakṣa sthāpitayā mūrtyā stūpādinā vā ābhāprakaṭīkaraṇamsādhanāyā kṣutpipāsādīnāmabhāvaḥ śarīrasfūrtiḥ svapne iṣṭadevadarśanamityetat sādhanāsiddhilakṣaṇāni eva lakṣaṇeṣūditeṣu svagurū pṛṣṭvā siddhicaryānuṣṭheyā viśeṣasādhanāyā khaḍgādikamādāya mantrajapahomādika kuryāt khecarādiśuddhakṣetra gatvā ajanādika sasevya caryāḥ ācaryyerantena ca vidyādharapada prāptu prayasanīyam svadehasya sūkṣmatva vidhāya īśvarasya aṣṭau guṇāḥ prāptavyāḥ siddhicaryā kriyātantrasya sādhanāvidheḥ siddhicaryānusāra caryā vidhāya sādhakaḥ yatheccha siddhi labdhumarhati uparyukta yad bodhicittotpādābhāve anayaiva sādhanayā śrāvakapada lokalokottarasarvavidhahīnamadhyamādhamasiddhīśca prāptu pārayati ataḥ uttama paramapada coddeśya bhavet kriyātantrasādhanoddeśya kṣudrasiddhiprāptirna bhavati tattu buddhatvāvāptireva kriyātantrasādhanānusāreṇa buddhatvaprāptyai aṣṭakalpānā kalpatrayasya vā kālo vyatyeti sādhakasya tīvraprayāsena ekasmin janmanyapi paramapadaprāptyuktistu mañjuśrīmūlakalpādikriyātantragrantheṣu vihitāsti  kriyātantre pañca mārgā daśa bhūmayaśca kriyātantrānusāra pañcamārgāṇā daśabhūmīnā ca vyākhyāvyavasthā ittham   kriyātantrābhiṣekaprāptyanantara  sādhakoha kriyātantrasādhanāyāḥ samyaksambodhi prāpsyāmi ityetadakṛtrimābhilāṣotpattimārabhya dhvanyantaḥ sthādhyānabhāvanābalena śūnyatābodhakavipaśyanāyāḥ  sākṣātkārapūrvavartimārgaḥ kriyātantrasya sabhāramārgaḥ ucayate   vipaśyanotpādamārabhya śamathavipaśyanāyugalabhāvanayā śūnyatāsākṣātkārapūrvāvasthā mārgaśca prayogamārgaḥ samabhidhīyate   vipaśyanāsamādhidvārā śūnyatā sākṣātkṛtya bhāvanāmārgeṇa praheyadharmasya mahākleśāvaraṇasya sthūlāśapratipakṣotpattimārgaḥ darśanamārgaḥ   pramuditā bhūmiḥ  udyate    bhāvanāmārgeṇa praheyadharmamahākleśāvaraṇasya sthūlāśapratipakṣotpattimārabhya sūkṣmātisūkṣmāvaraṇākṣayāt buddhatvaprāpakavajrāsanākhyasamādheḥ  pūrvakṣaṇāvasthā bhāvanāmārgaḥ  vimalā prabhākarīprabhṛtayaḥ navabhūmayaḥ santi bhāvanāmārgasya praheya kleśāvaraṇa jñeyāvaraṇa ca  kleśāvaraṇasya sthūlamadhyamasūkṣmabhedāḥ tadvadeva madhyamāvaraṇasya sūkṣmāvaraṇasya ca krameṇa trayastrayo bhedāḥ eva navabhedāḥ bhavanti  ye ca bhūmipraheyadharmāḥ nigadyante  etannavakleśāvaraṇeṣu svabhūmijñeyāvaraṇeṣu ca naṣṭeṣu satsu kramaśaḥ sādhakena uparitanabhūmayo labhyante  kriyātantrasya samyaksambodhyavasthaivāśaikṣamārgaḥ paramapada cāsti upasahāraḥ jñānasamuccaye kriyātantrasādhakāyokta  tatra svadehe devakāyasya bhāvanābhāvosti imāmuktimāśritya vidvatsu matabhedo vartate jonaṅ je cuna prabhṛtayotra svadehe devakāyabhāvanābhāva svīkurvanti ācārya coṅkhāpāprabhṛtividvadbhiḥ kriyātantre svadehe devakāyabhāvanāpaddhatiḥ svīkṛtāsti etasya ca samarthane naikānyāgamavacāsi yuktayaśca prādīyanta  ācāryakarmāṭhinalas prabhṛtibhiḥ kriyātantrasādhakasya pradhānāpradhāneti staradvayamabhimatam bhaṇitañcāpi pradhānasādhakaḥ svadehe devatā  bhāvayati  aparaśca svasammukha devatā bhāvayitvā mantra japati  ayameva caramapakṣaḥ susaṅgataḥ pratīyate yataśca kriyātantrasya naikeṣu prāmāṇikagrantheṣu svadehe devabhāvanāyāḥ sattvam asattva vobhaya  prācuryeṇa labhyate  ata ekasya viśiṣṭamartha kṛtvā vyākhyāna kiyaducitamiti duḥśakam sāmānyavicāreṇāpi pratīyate pāramitānayasya vacanenānena  buddhāśca bodhisatvāśca sarvatrāvyāhatekṣaṇāḥ sarvamevāgratasteṣā teṣāmasmi puraḥ sthitaḥ yaḥ sādhakotyabhilaṣati tatsammukha sadā śāstāvatiṣṭhate etadāśaya yotyantamabhiniveśapūrvaka dhārayatikriyātantravidhau tatpravartanāya iṣṭadeva svasammukhamāhūya pūjārcanābhāvanāyāḥ vyavasthāvidhānamanucita na bhavati anyataśca svadehe devabhāvanātyantābhāvopyasvīkāryaḥ yataśca evamabhimatyā pāramitānayād mantranayasya kimapi vaiśiṣṭya na syāt rūpakāyasyopādānakārakābhāvopi syāt tataśca atra falasya mārgīkaraṇamapi na syāt  ārya asagaracitamaitreyasādhanāyā bhikṣuṇīśrīdevīviracitaikādaśānanasādhanāyā candragomiracitatārāsādhanāyā svadehe devatva bhāvayitu  coktam  etatsarvamapyamānya syāt  ataḥ uparyuktapaddhatyavalokanena pratīyate kriyātantre svadehe devabhāvanākaraṇākaraṇayoḥ vidhidvayameva prāpyate kasyāpyekasya pakṣasya  nyāyasaṅgatipratipādanamapi nocita pratibhāti  vineyajanayogyatānusāreṇa bhedoya jāyate bhoṭadeśe tantraśāstrasya pracāradṛṣṭyā pūrvakālikaśāsane kriyātantracaryātantraprādhānyamavartata vyākhyāsādhanāpaddhatiścāpi mukhyata ācāryabuddhaguhyamevānukaroti uttarakālikaśāsane bāhyābhyantarasādhanāyāmubhayayogatantraprādhānyamāsīt dīpaṅkaraśrījñānenāpi bodhipathapradīpasya svavṛttau pratipādita sarvā dhāraṇyaḥ kriyātantre sagṛhyante atoyamatra praśnaḥ  prāyaḥ dhāraṇīsagraheṣu sādhanāvidhirna bhavati tatsādhanā kena vidhinā kriyeta  etat samādhayatā buddhaguhyena subāhuparipṛcchāsūtravyākhyāyāmucyete nikhilakriyātantrasādhanā praveśacaryāprayogacaryāsādhanāsiddhicaryāsiddhicaryākhyacaturaṅgeṣu  sagṛhya sādhanā karaṇīyā  yeṣu grantheṣu samagravidhirna pratipādi tastatra dhyānottaratantrasusiddhitantrasubāhu paripṛcchāsūtratantrāṇyādhārīkṛtya caryeta prādhānyena guhyasāmānyatantre praveśacaryā dhyānottaratantre prayogacaryāsusiddhitantre ca sādhanācaryā pratipāditācaryālakṣaṇāni bhedāśca subāhuparipṛcchāsūtre nyarūpyanta  guhyasāmānyatantrasusiddhitantrasubāhuparipṛcchāsūtradhyānottaratantreṣu kramaśaḥ pūrvavartiguhyasāmānyatantra bṛhatkāya dhyānottaratantra  ca laghukāyagrantharatnam  guhyasāmānyatantre aparipakvapātrāṇā paripakvatāyai abhiṣekavidhirniradiśyata etasmin tathāgatādikulānā pañcaśatādhikaikasahasramaṇḍalāni nirūpitāni kriyātantrasya sarvakulānā maṇḍalaviṣayepyatra sūcanā labhyate  etadatirikta caryātantrasya yogasyānuttarayogatantrasya ca maṇḍalābhiṣekayoḥ prathamadivase sampatsyamānādhivāsamaṇḍalānā vidhirapyualabhyate asmin eka eva sargaḥ  paricchedaḥ  susiddhitantre aṣṭatriśat vidhikramāḥ sagṛhītāḥ santi yathā    guhyamantralakṣaṇakramaḥ   ācāryalakṣaṇakramaḥ   sādhanālakṣaṇakramaḥ   mantrasevakakramaḥ   sthānalakṣaṇakramaḥ   vidyāmantravineyakramaḥ   puṣpalakṣaṇakramaḥ   gandhalakṣaṇakramaḥ   dhūpalakṣaṇakramaḥ   ālokalakṣaṇakramaḥ   balividhikramaḥ   śāntipuṣṭivaśitācaryāvidhikramaḥ   siddhibhedalakṣaṇakramaḥ   āhvānavidhikramaḥ   pūjāvidhikramaḥ   rakṣāvidhikramaḥ   japavidhikramaḥ    devasantuṣṭividhikramaḥ    devābhiṣekavidhikramaḥ   adhivāsavidhikramaḥ   vidyāmantraparigrahaṇavidhikramaḥ   vidyāmantraparipūrṇavidhikramaḥ   devakānta   aojasvidhikramaḥ   sādhanāṅgasañcayavidhikramaḥ   dravyalakṣaṇavidhikramaḥ   dravyaparigrahaṇavidhikramaḥ   dravyapariśodhanavidhikramaḥ   dravyaparimāṇavidhikramaḥ  dravyādhiṣṭhānavidhikramaḥ   sādhanākālavidhikramaḥ    sādhanāyā prādurbhūtalakṣaṇaparicayavidhikramaḥ   dravyādhivāsavidhikramaḥ   tathāgatakuladravyasādhanāmaṇḍalavidhikramaḥ   padyakuladravyasādhanāmaṇḍalavidhikramaḥ   vajrakuladūtidravyasādhanāmaṇḍalavidhikramaḥ   dravyasādhanāvidhikramaḥ   dravyaharaṇākuśavidhikramaḥ   sādhanopāyasagrahavidhikramaśca ebhireva tantramida sampadyate subāhuparipṛcchā sūtre guhyasāmānyatantrānirdiṣṭābhiṣekavidhiḥsusiddhitantrāpūrṇākriyāmantrasādhanāvidhiḥśāntipuṣṭiraudrakarmāṇyādhārīkṛtya sāmānyāsāmānyasiddhyavāptividhayaśca spaṣṭīkṛtāḥ santi granthoyamekādaśaparicchedeṣu vibhaktaḥ kathyate ca yat subāhuḥ vajrapāṇirastiaya ca ekajīvanānantara bodhipadaprāpako bodhisattvo vartate tasyaiva nāma subāhuḥ dhyānottaratantra hi mahākriyātantroṣṇīṣatantrasyaikaḥ aśaḥ ata evedamuttaratantramucyate etadatra kriyātantrasya daśa tattvāni pratipāditāni atra prāṇāyāmopi vyamarśi granthaśca tripacāśat ślokeṣu nibaddhoyam buddhaguhyabodhiśreṣṭhau kriyātantrasya mahāntāvācāryyau manyete  buddhaguhyena dhyānottaratantrasya subāhuparipṛcchāsūtrasya ca sāragarbhitā vyākhyā vyadhāyi sūtrasya śabdārthayoḥ sāmānyarūparekhā cāpyalekhi bodhiśreṣṭhena susiddhitantre upāyopasagrahākhya grantho vyaracyata kriyātantrasya varṇitasādhanāvidhīnā vistareṇāvagamāya granthoyamatyantamupayogitāmāvahati  tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ caryātantram caryātantrābhyudayaḥ dīpaṅkaraśrījñānena bodhipathapradīpasya svavṛttau caryātantrasya vairocanābhisambodhitantravajrāaṇyabhiṣekatantraprabhṛtīni  aṣṭasahasrāṇi tantrāṇi pratyapādyanta  bustonopi vairocanābhisabodhitantra mūlatantraguhyaśreṣṭhatantramuttaratantravajrapāṇya bhiṣekāditantragranthatrayañca caryātantrāntargatamamanyata anyavidvatsu śākyasampradāyasya ḍodgonachosagyalafagasapāprabhṛtayaḥ kriyātantre svadehe devakāyabhāvanābhāvammanyante ata eva mañjuśrīmūlakalpamapi caryātantrāntargata manyate etanmatena vairocanābhi sambodhitantram acalamahākalpatantrayamāntakakrodhavijayatantramapi caryātantramasti anyavidvadgaṇeṣu mahāpaṇḍitapuṇyakīrtiprabhṛtibhiracalamahākrodharājatantranīlāmbaradharavajrapālaprabhṛtayaḥ sapta granthā agaṇyanta sakṣepeṇa sanidāna paricayotra prastūyate   vairocanābhisambodhitantram sāmānyatastathāgatamahāvairocanaḥ akaniṣṭhabhuvane kālacatuṣṭaye dharmamupadiśati yathāsamaya nirmāṇakāyatvena sumerūparvatajambudvīpādiṣvāvirbhūya dharmamupadiśati  viśeṣataśca caryātantrāsādhāraṇavairocanābhisabodhitantrasya deśanā bhagavataḥ vairocanasya kusumatalagarbhālaṅkāravyūhākhye buddhatattvaprāptisthāne  kṛtā  etatsambandhe vajrapāṇyabhiṣekatantrasya nidānaparivarte kathita yadida kṣetram anantasasāradhātu nirdiśati ekasasāradhātāvanantalokadhātavaḥ sagṛhyante śatakoṭicaturdīpaśatakoṭisumerūparvataśatakoṭimahāsāgarasūryacandrādayaḥ sarvepi trisāhasramahāsāhasralokāḥ kathyante ittha śatakoṭikusumatalagarbhālaṅkāraḥ ucyate eva śatakoṭiekasantatikusumatalagarbhālaṅkāra ucyate  arthāt bhagavadvairocanena buddhatvātpūrva bodhisattvānā caryayā pariśodhita sampūrṇakṣetrameva kusumatalagarbhālaṅkāravyūhakṣetram evocyate yaccācintyavipākasya sampannatayodbhūtamasti  tatkṣetre yathākāśe sūryaprakāśe prasṛte sati ākāśa prakāśābhinnau bhavatastathaivādvayabhāvasthito mahāvairocano buddhaḥ satvebhyaḥ kāyasamatāsthitanāmadharmaparyāya vāksamatāsthitanāmadharmaparyāya cittasamatāsthitanāmadharmaparyāya ca diśati kāyavākcittānāmagādhatvena bhagavato vairocanasya kāyavākcittāni sarvabhūmiṣu praveśārhāṇi  itthamasminneva kṣetre vajrapāṇinā bhagavān vairocanaḥ pṛṣṭastadāsya tantraśāstrasya saptaskandheṣu caturviśatiparivarteṣu ca vibhaṅga kṛtvā  diśyate  tadvivaraṇamittham   bodhicittatadutpādavidhipratipādakaścittavibhaṅgakramaḥ   mahākarūṇayā prerito maṇḍalapraveśaḥ abhiṣekavidhimantralakṣaṇavighnopaśamanavibhaṅgakramaḥ   sāmānyamantrakośavibhaṅgakramaḥ   lokasiddhivibhaṅgakramaḥ   siddhisādhanātattvavibhaṅgakramaḥ   devadhyānapratipādanavibhaṅgakramaḥ   nirlakṣaṇavibhaṅgakramaḥ   lokottaramantrajapavibhaṅgakramaḥ   akṣaracakravibhaṅgakramaḥ   mudrākramavibhaṅgakramaḥ   mantramaṇḍalapraveśavibhaṅgakramaḥ   mantrāṣṭamudrāvibhaṅgakramaḥ   vidyāmantravratavibhaṅgakramaḥ   bodhisatvaśikṣopāyavān vibhaṅgakramaḥ   ācāryatattvajñānavibhaṅgakramaḥ   akṣaranyāsavibhaṅgakramaḥ   śatākṣarīudbhūtavibhaṅgakramaḥ   falayoganirdiṣṭavibhaṅgakramaḥ   svatattvasādhanāvibhaṅgakramaḥ   śatākṣarīvidhivibhaṅgakramaḥ   samyaksambodhisvabhāvanirdeśavibhaṅgakramaḥ   trisamayacaryāvibhaṅgakramaḥ   tathāgatanirdiṣṭavibhaṅgakramaḥ   mantrānusāra bodhisatvacaryāvidhiryathākramavibhaṅgaśca bustonamahodayena ṣaḍviśopi parivartogaṇyata  buddhasya pūrvajanmani bodhisatvarūpeṇodbhavakāle brāhyaṇairagnibhedaviṣaye pṛṣṭe sati vedapratipāditacatuścatvāriśadagnibhedānā buddhatvasyāvāptyā  dvādaśāgniṣu pūrvagamanena homavidhirapi gaṇitaḥ  para parivartoya sampratyupalabdhadegetañjurākhye na vidyate vairocanābhisambodhitantra mūlatantramasti atra maṇḍalatrayam mūlatantreṇānena sāka bhoṭabhāṣāyāmupalabdha guhyaśreṣṭhatantram uttaratantramabhidhīyate atra sapta parivartāḥ yathā    śāntyādicaturthakarmārtha śāntihomaḥ   puṣṭihomavidhiḥ   vaśahomavidhiḥ   raudracaryāsiddhyartha homaḥ   svaravyañjanādyakṣarapratipādanapūrvako bhāvanāvidhiḥ   devabhāvanātaḥ pūrva karmaprāyaścittam   mahākarūṇodbhūtyā saha guhyamaṇḍala praviśya tathāgatādhiṣṭhito vidhiḥ tantrasyāsya viṣaye bustonakathanānusāramidamapūrṇam yatosya nāmnā samuddhṛtānyanekāni vacāsi śāstre pratipādyante yāni samupalabdhaguhyatantre nopalabhyante     acalamahākrodharājatantram etad deśanāviṣaye granthesminneva kathita bhagavatā vāyumaṇḍale vibhinnaratnairalaṅkṛtavimāne anantavyūhaiḥ  paripūrṇe anantapuṇyebhyaḥ samutpannasihāsane sthitvā vajrapāṇibodhisatvāvalokiteśvaramaitreyaśāriputramaudgalyāyanādiśrāvakaiḥ paripūrṇaiḥ  brahyaviṣṇuprabhṛtibhiḥ saha viharatā mahākarūṇayā preritena satā cittena etat tantramupadiśyate      nīlāmbaravajrapātālatantram etaddeśanā bhagavatā saptapātālakramasthitanāgaloke vajrapāṇinā saha viharatā svapādābhyā prakāśapuñja  sasforya nāgaānandaupānandādinṛpān nāgāścāvarjya taddamana vidhāya tadabhiṣicya etattantramadiśyata  sapta paricchedā atra yathā     nidānaparivartaḥ   dhanasādhanavighnanivāraṇaparivartaḥ   niṣpratikāraroganivāraṇaparivartaḥ   maṇḍalaparivartaḥ    yakṣasādhanāparivartaḥ   nāgasādhanāparivartaḥ   kathāparivartaśca     nīlāmbaratrilokavinayatantram tantramida bhagavatā sumerūparvatasya dakṣiṇalakāvatītyākhye prāsāde viharatānantāsurebhyaḥ devebhyaḥ  vajrapāṇiprabhṛtibhyaḥ samupādiśyata  asmiśca catvāraḥ paricchedāḥ   nidānaparicchedaḥ   pātāladamanaparicchedaḥ   manuṣyalokadamanaparicchedaḥ   ākāśalokadamanaparicchedaśca  nidānaparicchedāvalokanāt pratīyate sādhakaḥ śraddhābhaktisādhanānā balena tattva sākṣātkṛtya tathāgatena saha saralasambandha sthāpayitumarhati praśna kṛtvā tadādhārīkṛtya grantha praṇetu śaknoti caryātantrasya deśanā sarvakāleṣu mahāvairocanenākāri kusumatalagarbhālaṅkāravyūhādyavalokanāt sampūrṇa jagadeva tathāgatadeśanākṣetra pratīyate etena suspaṣṭa bhavati yajjagataḥ kasminnapi koṇe kenāpi sādhakena dhyānabhāvanāyā kṛtāyā satyā tathāgataḥ prakaṭībhūya ta diśati caryātantrasvarūpam bāhyasnānādiśuddhyā saheṣṭadeva bhāvayitvābhyantaradhyānasyāpi caryāvidhāyakaḥ sādhakaḥ caryātantravān kathyate  jñānasamuccaye caryātantrasvarūpa suspaṣṭayatā bhagavatābhāṇiṣaḍdevatattvānā bhāvanāvidhinā kāyavākcittaśuddhyartha vibhinnacaryāvidhīnām  anuśīlanam kriyātantre varṇitakarmamudrādevyā saha hāsyādikriyābhiḥ sukhānubhūtipūrvaka dhyāna  caryātantramārgasvarūpamasti caryātantre prādhānyena svakāya buddhakāye dṛṣṭvā kāyādhiṣṭhāna tvarita sādhakaḥ prāpnotimantrarūpeṇa svavacāsi bhāvayitvā vāgadhiṣṭhāna nijacite jñānasvarūpa bhāvayitvā cittādhiṣṭhāna ca labhate svayamapi devarūpeṇa bhāvanayā svadeha prati abhiniveśamohau kṣīyetedivyaguṇāḥ saukaryyeṇopalabhyante arthāt falasya mārgarūpeṇa bhāvanayā puṇyadvaya paripūrtirbhavati paṭacitrādāviṣṭadeva bhāvayitvā ārādhanādyapekṣayā svadeha devakāyarūpeṇa parivartya bhāvanākaraṇād druta sambhāradvaya sacīyate caryātantreṣvayameva vidhirūpādeśi ataḥ sāmānyakriyātantrāpekṣayāya vidhiḥ śreṣṭhobhimanyate caryātantrasyāntarikakulabhedāḥ kriyātantravadeva caryātantrasyāpi trayo bhedāḥ    tathāgatakulam   padyakulam   vajrakula ca koṅṭularinapochemahodayasya matānusārametat kāyavākcittākhye trikulepi vibhājayitu śakyam yathā ca tathāgatakula hi kāyakula vidyatepadyakula vākkula vajrakula caiva cittakulamasti etadeva caryātantradvāramapyucyate sāmānyataḥ sarve tathāgatāḥ kulāni ca tattvataḥ abhinnānyevakevalamupāyavaśena vineyajanāśayānusārametāni vibhinnarūpeṣu āvirbhavanti yathā caikaḥ sādhakaḥ bhagavacchākyamuneḥ rūpākṛtī citte samālambya dhyāyate tathā rūpākāra sākṣātkurūte evameva sihalīyajanāḥ ātmavaddevamūrti nirmānti tathaiva cīnajāpānatibbatadeśīyā ātmarūpākārarūpeṇaiva eva kāyavākcittānyapi tattvataḥ abhinnānyeva vajrapāṇyabhiṣekatantrepi yaḥ kulaputraḥ maṇḍala praviśya mantracaryāṅkaroti tad vāgatiriktammano nāsti manasotiriktā vāgapi na kāyātiriktā vāg nāstivāgatiriktaḥ kāyopi nāsti tena vicāraṇīyā vāgeva manostimana eva devarūpamdevarūpā caiva vāgevāsti evametattrayābhinnatvammatvā dhyānānuṣṭhānena taccharīram iṣṭadevatārūpe mantravācimanasi citte ca pratiṣṭhāsyate etena suspaṣṭa yat kāyavākcittānyapi ekānyeva caryātantreṣvapi kriyātantravacchāntipuṣṭiraudrakarmaṇā sasiddhyai bhāgatraye kula vyabhāji devasvarūpasyātra kriyātantrāpekṣayā bhinnatvam yathā tathāgatakule vairocanācalau akṣobhyo vā vajrakule ca vajrapāṇirnīlāmbaraśca svīkṛtāḥ santi padyakarapo kathayati caryātantramapi prāyaḥ kriyātantrasadṛśameva ataḥ kriyātantramatiricyāsmin kulasya pṛthag bhedā na bhavanti  kriyātantracaryātantrayoryadyapi pañca kulabhedāḥ kartum sambhāvyante para ca tantradvayasya sādhakasiddheḥ kulatraye sagṛhītattvāt kulasya  bhedatrayameva yujyate  ḍogonachosajñala fagasapākhyaḥ ācāryaḥ sāmānyacaryātantre tathāgatakulagrantha vairocanābhisambodhitantravajrakulagrantha ca vajrapāṇyabhiṣekatantratvenābhimanyate etena kathyate padyakulatantra tibbatībhāṣāyā nānūditam paṇḍitapuṇyakīrtimatena hayagrīvatantra padyakulasya granthaḥ yo hi tibbatībhāṣāyām anūditobhūt bustonaḥ kriyātantrasama caryātantramabhimanyate ataścaryātantra pṛthag vyākhyāyina tena caryātantrasādhanāpaddhatiḥ caryātantrasādhanavidhiḥ śrībuddhaguhyena bhāgacatuṣṭaye vibhajyate   praveśacaryā   yogacaryā   sādhanāsiddhiḥ   siddhicaryā ca   praveśacaryā praveśacaryāyāḥ punaḥ dvau bhedau bāhyapraveśaḥ abhiṣekavidhirvāābhyantarapraveśo hi samayasavarāṇā pālanam abhiṣekaviṣaye paścād vakṣyate vistareṇa adhunā caryātantrasādhanāyā keṣāmabhiṣekāṇā prāptiranivāryyā tatsaṅketaḥ kariṣyate  jñānatilakepyuktacaryātantrasādhakena kriyātantrasya sarvābhiṣekeṣu vajraghaṇṭānāmābhiṣekāḥ prāptavyāḥ arthāt jalapaṭavajraghaṇṭānāmābhiṣekāḥ  prāptavyāḥ bhavanti  kalaśābhiṣekato durgatirnaśyati  ayamabhiṣekaḥ bhavacakrabīja prakṣālayati prathamapramuditābhūmita ārabhya dharmameghākhyadaśamabhūmiparyanta sādhaka sampreṣya buddhatva  prāpayati   paṭābhiṣekād dvātriśad lakṣaṇānyaśītyanuvyañjanāni labhyante ghaṇṭābhiṣekāt ṣaṣṭibrahyasvarāṅgānā prāptirbhavati vajrābhiṣekācca yathāvadyāvadjñānaprāptimārgasya  sopānamudghaṭate  caryātantrābhiṣekaprāptyai prapañcaniṣprapañcamaṇḍalayorvyavasthā varīvarti  prapañcamaṇḍale mṛṇmaya niṣprapañce ca cittamaṇḍala svīkṛtamāste abhiṣekāvāptipūrva maṇḍalapraveśakāle abhiṣekāvāptyanantara tāsu tisṛṣvavasthāsu  trividhasamayānā savarāṇāñca pālanamāvaśyakam  samayasavaraviṣaye paścād vistareṇa nirūpayiṣyate atra ca caryātantrasādhakasya sāmānyatonivāryarūpeṇa pālanīyānā samayasavarāṇā saṅketamātra nirdiśyate abhiṣekaprāptyai sādhakaḥ kāyavākcittānīṣṭadevāya samarpayati tataśca sādhakopi iṣṭadevasya kuliko bhavati tadā tena kulaśikṣānusāreṇa kārya kriyeta abhiṣekaprāptyanantara sādhakena caryātantrasya yathārthasādhanāyā salakṣaṇanirlakṣaṇarūpadevayogasya bhāvanā satata karaṇīyā bhavatiarthāt sādhakena kālatraye vajrasatvarūpohamiti vicārya gambhīrodārasalakṣaṇanirlakṣaṇadevayogaḥ bhāvanīyo jāyate sahaiva ca samayasavarāṇā vināśo mā bhūtetadarthamapi sannaddhatayā stheyam  yogacaryā asyā api bhedadvayamsalakṣaṇayogaḥ nirlakṣaṇayogaśca salakṣaṇayogasyāpi bāhyābhyantaracatuścaturaṅgairyuktau dve vidhī pratyapādyetām punaścaturaṅgasādhanāvidheḥ dvau bhedau bhavataḥ    sāmānyasādhanāvidhiḥ   viśeṣasādhanāvidhiśca  ka  bāhyasāmānyasādhanāvidhiḥ kriyātantravadeva śūnyadevaakṣaradevarūpadevādidevatattvānā catvāryaṅgāni āśritam   bodhicittam   dhvanimantrabījam   prāṇāyāmaśca etaccatuṣṭayena bhāvanā kriyate bāhyabhyantarasnānādinā śuddhībhūya rakṣācakra ca bhāvayitvā sveṣṭadevamāvāhayet iṣṭadevasya pūjārcanābhyarthanānantara śūnyatābhāvanameva śūnyadevo bhaṇyate iṣṭadevamantrabījasya bhāvanaiva akṣaradevaḥ mantradhvaninā saha sfuraṇasahārabhāvanā hi dhvanidevaḥiṣṭadevarūpa rūpadevaḥiṣṭadevahṛdayakamale āyudhādīnā bhāvanā mudrādevaḥsvadeha ca mantreṇādhiṣṭhāya devarūpeṇa taddhayāna lakṣaṇadeva ucyate etatṣaḍdevatattvānā bhāvanāvidhiḥ kriyātantravadeva vidyate sāmānyavidhirayamucyate  kha  bāhyaviśeṣasādhanāvidhiḥ vairocanābhisambodhitantre vajrapāṇinā tathāgatavairocanaḥ pṛcchyate he bhagavan yaḥ sādhako devarūpānvitaḥ san devarūpa vāvalambya caryāṅkarotisa tvarita devarūpeṇa pariṇamate ataḥ devarūpa mahya nirdiśyatām pratyuttare sādhu sādhu praśnoya suṣṭhu he vajrapāṇe śṛṇu devasya svarūpatrayamakṣarammudrā rūpa ca akṣarasya punaḥ bhedadvayam  śabdabodhicitte mudrāyā api dvau bhedau rūpyarūpiṇau rūpasyāpi punaḥ  paripūrṇaśuddhamaśuddha ca dvau eva bhāvanāmayadevasya ṣaḍ bhedāḥ iṣṭadeve nijahṛdayakamale ca sasthitacanramaṇdalabodhicittamtadupari iṣṭadevamantrabījasya bhāvanaiva śabdadevabodhicittayorbhāvanāsti cakravajrādika hi rūpimudrādharmodayaśca yā śūnyatābodhikā sā arūpimudrā yannirvikalpa sarvalakṣaṇarahita tat paripūrṇaśuddham yacca lakṣaṇavarṇasasthānairyukta tadaśuddhamasti devasyaitadantimarūpadvayasya prayojanam falasya salakṣaṇarūpatva nirlakṣaṇarūpatva ca     ābhyantarasāmānyasādhanāvidhiḥ vairocanābhisabodhitantre bodhisattvavajrapāṇinā guhyamantrasya sādhanā katha kriyeta eva bhagavati  pṛṣṭe sati bhagavatā etānyeva catvāryaṅgāni pratipādayatā siddhyartha daśalakṣamitamantrajapo nirdiśyate ataḥ pūrvakarmasāmānyavidhi samāpya paramārthabodhicittasvarūpeṇa savṛtyābhāsacandramaṇḍala dhyeyam tadupari bījākṣara nyasetyacca sahasā dhvanirūpeṇa sasfuret bījākṣara candramaṇḍala ca pariṇata sat svadehe devarūpeṇa prakaṭimiti vicāraṇīyam ādarśe rūpapratibimbanamiva ātmavadeva svasamakṣa bhāvanīyamiṣṭadevasya hṛdayakamale sthāpitabījākṣare mano nidhāya prāṇāyāma vidadhyāt prāṇāyāmābhiprāya bodhayitvā vairocanābhisambodhitantre nirūpita prāṇāśca vāyurapāna ca smṛtirasti śarīre vāyupraveśamārga niyantrya mantre manasa ekāgratva hi smṛtiyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ yāvanna devābhāsastāvat prāṇāyāma kurvan mantra japet ābhyantaraviśeṣasādhanāvidhiḥ svacandramaṇḍalabodhicitte  a  ā a ā  iti caturakṣareṣu kimapyeka bhāvanīyam tataśca prakāśasya sfuraṇena saharaṇavidhinā ca svārthaparārthasiddhiḥ dhyātavyā  tadanantara bījākṣaratvena pariṇatasya pītavarṇasya ekamukhasya bhujayugalasya dhyānamudrāyām uṣṇīṣe pāe ca cakrālakṛtadvātriśadlakṣaṇāśītyanuvyañjanaiḥ  paripūrṇacīvarāṇi dhārayamāṇasya śvetakamalacandramaṇḍalayorūpari virājamānasya buddhadevasyaiva mama svarūpam itthamahaṅkāreṇa stheyam tadanu hṛdayakamale punaśca candramaṇḍale bījākṣare vairocanasya bhāvanā karaṇīyā tataśca tadhṛdayakamale candramaṇḍalabījamantre nyasya prāṇāyāmadvārā mantra japet ābhyantaracaturaṅgasamanvitaḥ ayameva mantrajapavidhirūcyate nirlakṣaṇasādhanāvidhiḥ nirlakṣaṇasādhanāyāḥ dvau bhedau  ka sāmānyam  kha  viśeṣaśca  ka  sāmānyam svahṛdayakamale  svayam iṣṭadeva bhāvanāviṣayībhūta kṛtvā āyudhacakravajrabījākṣaradika bhāvayitvā prāṇāyāmakaraṇamtataśca devadavyoḥ parasparam īkṣaṇa hasanātmaka svarūpa dhyātvā rāgamārgīkaraṇavidhānena saha viṣaye  śūnyatāyām sthitireva sāmānyanirlakṣaṇasādhanāvidhirūcyate   kha  viśeṣaḥ skandhādiṣu catuṣkoṭivatyāmādhyamikayuktyā ajātānirūddhādiguṇasahitā catuṣkoṭiniṣprapañcatā buddhvā tattve sthitirapekṣyate  ye ca sattvā etattathyādaparicitā stathānenaiva kāraṇena nānāduḥkhāni anubhavanti tān dṛṣṭvā karūṇayā dravībhūtaḥ san anugrahītumicched arthāt  yuktibhiḥ vastuniḥsvabhāvatā pratipādya pravarteta tadanu ca tattve yathāsabhava sthitiḥ antataḥ samādherūtthitiḥpṛṣṭhalabdhau sattvahitavidhānamtryaṅgayukta bhāvanākaraṇa hi nirlakṣaṇabhāvanā kathyate vairocanābhisambodhau salakṣaṇabhāvanāpekṣayā nirlakṣaṇabhāvanā prabalatayā preritā yataśca salakṣaṇayogāt salakṣaṇasiddhirlabhyate nirlakṣaṇayogācca salakṣaṇanirlakṣaṇobhayasiddhiravāpyate sārāśaḥ kriyācaryātantrayoḥ yogasya catvāri mahattvādhāyakānyaṅgāni devaśūnyatayoryogaḥ prāṇāyāmamantrajapayośca yogaḥ paramārthataḥ śūnyatābhāvanā savṛtito devarūpā ca bhāvanaiva dharmakāyasabhogakāyaprāpteḥ pradhānamupādānam mantrajape ya iṣṭadevo bhāvyetatadāvāhanam ātmanaśca tadrūpeṇa adhiṣṭhāna bhavet prāṇāyāmayogaḥ ubhayayoge dādryaprāpyupāyaḥ ata ida salakṣaṇanirlakṣaṇayogayoḥ samānamanivārya cāṅgamasti  sādhanāsiddhicaryā mantrajapasya pūrṇatāyā satyā sādhakaḥ sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇasiddhīnā prāptyadhikārī bhavati sādhāraṇasiddhiprāptyai sādhakaḥ khaḍgādikamādāya mantra japet tena ca vidyādharādisiddhayaḥ prāpyante asādhāraṇasiddhyavasthāyāmantarnihitakṣitijalapāvakādimaṇḍalānāmāśraye śaktipuṣṭiraudravaśyādikarmasu pūrṇatva labhate prātihāryābhijñādibhiḥ svaparobhayahita karoti siddheraya māpadaṇḍaḥ eva sthityāgamanapūrva sādhanā kriyamāṇā bhavet samānyasādhanākāle svapna iṣṭadevābhāsaḥ iṣṭadevamaṇḍalasya pūjārcana svapnādyavekṣaṇamapi sādhanāyāḥ śubhalakṣaṇa manyate kramaśaḥ pariṣkṛtyā sākṣād iṣṭadevasya darśanena sāmānyāsāmānyasarvavidhasiddhayaḥ prāpyante etatsāmānyāsāmānyasiddhibhyaḥ mantrajapapūrṇatānantara sādhakasya siddhiprāptistadyathecchamālambate  siddhicaryā siddhicaryayā mṛdvindriyo janaḥ aṣṭakalpeṣu nūnameva samyaksambodhi labhate tīkṣṇendriyaḥ kalpatraye paramapadamavāpnoti sādhakaḥ prāptyabhilāṣāyāmekasmin jīvanepi paramapada prāptumarhati upasahāraḥ bustonamahāśayenāvocikriyācaryātantrayoḥ sādhanāpaddhatirekavidyāsamācāsti ataścaryātantrasādhanāpaddhatirna viśada vivecitā tena paṇḍitapuṇyakīrtimahodayenāpi caryātantra samayasavaratantragrantha yāvat kulabhedamātra ca niradhāri tanmatenāpi sādhanāpaddhatiḥ kriyātantrasadṛśī caivāsti ācāryacoṅkhāpāmahodayena sakṣepeṇa caryātantrasādhanāpaddhatirvivecitā atra jñeyakośamādhārīkṛtya kiñcillikhyate kriyātantravadeva caryātantramapi kulānusāreṇa tathāgatakulapadyakulavajrakulākhye bhāgatraye vibhajyate  sādhanāpaddhatau caturañgayuktabhāvanāvidhiḥ yadyapi kriyātantrasamāna eva para ca caryātantrasya bhāvanāvidhiḥ kriyātantrāpekṣayā bhṛśa nānyathā kriyātantrāt pārthakyāvaśyakatva syāt  yathā ca kriyātantre svadehe devakāyasya bhāvanāyā satyāmasatyā matabhedaḥ kintvatra nirvivāda svadehe devakāyasya bhāvanāvidherāvaśyakatva  pratyapādi  svasammukha ca dhyeya iṣṭadeve jñānadevamāhūya vilīnatvasyāpi paddhatiḥ prākāśi sādhaneyameva salakṣaṇadevayoganirlakṣaṇadevayogeti nāmnā vijñāyate yā ca kriyātantrāpekṣayā sūkṣmā salakṣaṇadevayogasya tātparyantu svayam iṣṭadeva bhāvayitvā pūrvoktacaturavayavayukta sat mantrajapavidhānam atraiva vijñeya yat sādhakaḥ svayam iṣṭadevarūpeṇa katha pariṇato bhavetyathā asmāka skandhaḥ yaśca pañcamahābhūtairvinirmitaḥ naikatattvānā saghātamātraḥpūrvakarmafalaiḥ samudbhūtaḥ sa paramārthapratipādakayuktibhiryadāsmābhiḥ viśliṣyate tadā śūnyatva prāpyate para ca tad hetupratyayānāmupalabdhau niḥsvabhāvatayāpi ādarśe pratibimbitatattvamiva prabhavati tathaiva sarvadharmā avagantavyāḥ yathā śūnyatāsvarūpeṇa vastūni āvirbhavanti tathā ātmanā devatvāvirbhāvenagurūpradattābhiṣekeṇa ca iṣṭadevaśaktyadhiṣṭhānādinā pratītyasamutpannavidhinā sādhakaḥ iṣṭadevatvena prakaṭībhavati ataḥ etat sthiteḥ pūrva iṣṭadevaḥ eva bhāvanīyo yadahameveṣṭadevaḥiṣṭadeve ahamasmi evam iṣṭadevabhāvanayā mantrajapakāryameva atra salakṣaṇayogaḥ ucyate nirlakṣaṇayogaḥ sāmānyena dharmakāryaprāptyupādānakārakaḥ salakṣaṇayogāvadhau bhāviteṣṭadevopi viśleṣaṇīyaḥ  viśleṣaṇena yathā rūpādidharmāṇā kāpi sattā na tiṣṭhati tathaiveṣṭadevakāyasattāpi na tathā ca svacitta kālatrayarahita sarvalakṣaṇeṣu  nirvikalpasthiti prāpnoti ayameva nirvikalpabhāvanāvidhirūdyate bhāvanākramepi kamalaśīlenedameva tathya nyarūpi kecid vidvāsaḥ śūnyatābodhānantara kṛtadevabhāvanā nirlakṣaṇabhāvanā tadabhāva tadabhāva ca salakṣaṇabhāvanā manvate yathā śūnyatāsākṣātkaraṇānantara tacchūnyatābodhake citte prabalaprajñotpatyā sahaiva dānasampādanamparikramaṇamvandanamityādi karmāṇi na śūnyatābodhakānipara ca śūnyatābodhapūrṇacittatvāt tatkarmāpi śūnyatāpreritamucyate  yathā bodhicittamutpādya tatkṣaṇameva śūnyatāyā samāhitatve sati samāhitāvasthāyā bodhicittapravāhāstitvamurarīkriyate tathaivātrāpi śūnyatājñānasya  pravāhe devabhāvanā nirlakṣaṇadevabhāvanābhidhīyate eva vidhā vyavasthā pāramitānaye tu sambhāvyate para ca tantreṣu na sabhāvyate  gurūvarācāryachulaṭhimopi prajñopāyasya yuganaddhasvarūpa spaṣṭayan kathayāmāsa yathā kasyāścinmāturekākiputrasya mṛtyau atyanta duḥkhamanubhūyate  tathāpi sā tadanubhavavedanādinā saha sarvāmapi dinacaryā sampādayati tadvadeva śūnyatāpreritadānādisampādanam pāramitānayasya prajñopāyādvayāvasthocyate ataḥ pāramitānayānusāreṇa eva vyākhyā nūnammānyā para ca vajrayānānusāreṇa amānyaiva yataśca tantreṣu devasvarūpasya śūnyatāyāśca yuganaddharūpamapekṣyate sāvṛtikacittābhāsasya devasvarūpatvamtacchūnyatā ca paramārthā yā cādvayaikākārāekarasābhinnā satī ekabuddhiviṣayiṇī cāsti falāvasthāyā kāyasya lakṣaṇānuvyañjanālaṅkṛta āśrayaḥ  devakāyaḥ eva ca tadāśritā nirālambakarūṇā ca advayabhāve tathaiva avatiṣṭhete yathā ca dīpakālokau tathāgatakāyastasya ca niḥ svabhāvatārthāt prajñopāyādvayabhāvanaiva nirlakṣaṇadevabhāvanāsti atra vyākhyātamadvaya yuganaddhadevaśca manomayaḥmanasā nirmāya etad bhāvyate para ca yogatantrānuttaratantrayoḥ pañcābhisambodhibhiḥ prāṇāyāmena caitat sūkṣmaprāṇacittopāyena samutpādya bhāvyate etadbhāvanādvaye mahadantara yaccāgre vakṣyate taditi  caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ yogatantram yogatantrasyābhyudayaḥ tattvasagrahaḥ padyavajratathāgatena tattvasagrahasya tantrārthāvatārākhyaṭīkāyā  yogatantradeśanāvidhi spaṣṭayatā samullikhyate  sāmānyato bhagavān svaparārthahetubodhicittotpādadvārā āvaraṇānā kṣayāt puṇyasabhārajñānasabhārābhyā  paripūrṇatayā vajrakāya prāpyākāśavat sarvatattveṣu vyāpto nirālambanirvikalpasvarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate   īdṛśasthitāvapi bodhicaryāsapādanakālikasaskārāṇāmarthātprāṇinā hitāya kṛtāyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ vaśībhūtaḥ san sambhoganirmāṇakāyatvenāvirbhūya  satvahita vidadhāti  tena sattvānāmadhyādeśānusāra kramaśaḥ yugapadubhayarūpeṇa dharmaḥ diśyate śāstustrīṇi rūpāṇi  dharmakāyasabhogakāyanirmāṇakāyākhyāni dharmopi trividhaḥ hetuyānabāhyayānamābhyantarayāna ca pārṣadopi trividhaḥ pratītyasamutpannaḥ praṇidhānotpanno jñānotpannaśca dharmadeśanāsthānānyapi trīṇinagaravimānamaṇḍalaprāsādākhyāni lokopi trividhaḥpātālalokaḥ sattvalokaḥ devalokaśca mahāyogatantratattvasagrahasya deśanā tathāgataḥ sabhogakāyadvārā devaloke cakre tataśca kramaśo jambudvīpe cakāra etacca tantrasagrahakarturadhiṣṭhānena puṣpita vikasita cābhūt tattvasagrahārambhe etaddeśanāviṣaye īdagvivaraṇamupalabhyate buddhaguhyena tattvasagrahasya prathamabhāgamāśritya  vajradhātuḥ ekaḥ śobhanaḥ vṛhattantrārthāvatārākhyo granthaḥ praṇanāyi etadādau tattvārtha spaṣṭayatānena tattvasagrahasya tāni saptatriśat tattvāṅgāni gaṇitāni yathā    hṛdayam   mudrā  mantraḥ  vidyā   adhiṣṭhānam   abhiṣekaḥ   dhyānam   pūjā   svatattvam   devatattvam  maṇḍalam   prajñā pratyavekṣaṇajñānam  kṛtyānuṣṭhānajñānam   dharmadhātuviśuddhajñānam   ākarṣaṇam  sthāpanam   bandhana   vaśīkaraṇa ca ete saptatriśatsādhanāvidhayaḥ susagṛhītāḥ ataḥ tantrasyāsya tattvasagrahanāma sārthaka vidyate buddhaguhyakathana yat  etāni saptatriśat tattvāni punaḥ hṛdayamudrāmantreṣu vidyātattveṣu ca sagrahītu śakyante granthasyāsya catvāro bhāgāḥ   vajradhātubhāgaḥ  trilokavijayabhāgaḥ  sakalajagadvinayabhāgaḥ  sarvārthasiddhibhāgaśca pratyeka bhāge ṣaḍ maṇḍalapaṭalāni yathā    vajradhātubhāgaḥ   ka vajradhātumaṇḍalam  kha vajraguhyavajramaṇḍalam  ga vajrajñānadharmamaṇḍalam  gha vajrakāyakarmamaṇḍalam  ṅa caturthamudrāmaṇḍala  ca ekamudrāmaṇḍala ca  trilokavijayamaṇḍale  ka trilokavijayamahāmaṇḍalam  kha krodhaguhyamudrāmaṇḍalam  ga vajrakuladharmajñānasamayamaṇḍalam  gha trilokavijayakramamaṇḍalam  ṅa trilokavijayacaturthamaṇḍalam  ca ekamudrāmaṇḍala ca   sakalajagadvinayabhāgaḥ   ka sakalajagadvinayamahāmudrāmaṇḍalam  kha padyaguhyamudrāmaṇḍalam  ga jñānamaṇḍalam  gha karmamaṇḍalam  ṅa caturthamudrāmaṇḍalam  ca sakalajagadekamudrāmaṇḍalam  sarvārthasiddhibhāgaḥ   ka sarvārthasiddhimahāmaṇḍalam  kha ratnaguhyamaṇḍalam  ga jñānamaṇḍalam  gha karmamaṇḍalam  ṅa caturthamudrāmaṇḍalam  ca sarvārthasiddhiekamudrāmaṇḍalam uparyuktānā ṣaṇṇā maṇḍalānā vyavasthānandagarbhaviracitatattvasagrahaṭīkānusāreṇa pradattāsti tattvasagrahasya atibṛhatī sundarī ca ṭīkeyammanyate tattvasagrahe sarvaprathama nidānavastuni  parivarte svārthaparārthobhayaprayojanānvita vairocanapada carcitamāste yena sādhakaḥ tatpadaprāptyai utkaṭecchā kuryāt tadanu viśeṣeṇa tatpadaprāptyupāyena sāka laukikalokottarasiddhīnā prāptimārgopi samavarṇyata yadyapi tathāgataśabdaprayogaḥ sarvapañcatathāgatakuleṣu bhavati yadā tathāgatakulamātra prayujyate tadānī vairocanakulikabodhisattvebhya eva bhavati na tu catuḥ kulabodhisattvebhyaḥ  tantrasyāsya prathamāṅge tathāgatakulānā sambaddhamārgaḥ pratipāditaḥ tathaiva dvitīyeṅge vajrakulamarthāt akṣobhyakula tṛtīye ca padyakula  caturthe ca sarvaprāṇihetusiddhida ratnakula pratyapādyata  atra kulāni catvāryeva varṇitāni prāṇināmarthasampattikartṛ ratnakula kāryasampādaka karmakula arthāt amoghasiddhiḥ ekenaiva rūpeṇa sagṛhītā tasmād bhāgacatuṣṭaye eva pañcakulāni samāhriyante mūlatantratattvasagrahena sahaiva uttaratantram uttarottaratantramapi samupalabhyate yasmin caturaṅgeṣu pratipāditaparamapadaprāptyupāyā vistareṇa vyākhyātāḥ uttarottaratantre vistareṇa spaṣṭīkṛtamyat yogatantrasya ye sādhakāḥ ābhyantarayogasya sādhanāyāmasāmarthya budhyante tebhyaḥ japapūjādibāhyacaryā vihitāḥ mūlatantrasya caturaṅgeṣu yallaukikasiddhiprāptimārgasya vyavasthāspaṣṭāpūrṇā ca tadapi spaṣṭīkṛtyātra pūritam atra yogatantrasyopavibhāga uttaratantrasambandhe praśnoya samudbhavati ki yogatantrasya ekaḥ pakṣaḥ kriyātantra kathayiṣyate yataścāya bāhyapavitratā dhyāyati japādikamapi karoti etaduttaramapyasti yat sāmānyacatustantrāṇā sthūlaprasthānātmako bhedosti para caitad mithaḥ virodhābhāsośakyaḥ  yathā guhyasamājasya vineyajana spaṣṭayatā candrakīrtimahodayenocyate yaḥ sādhakaḥ utpattikramapūrṇatāprāptyanantara sādhāraṇasiddhi labdhu  na prayasati niṣpannakrama bhāvayan paramapadāvāptyai caiva prayatate īdṛśaḥ sādhakaḥ ratnasadṛśa yogyatāpātramucyate  yena sādhakena utpattikrame dākṣyam upalabhya sādhāraṇasiddhiprāptyai prayasyate sa adhamapuṇḍarīkaḥ ākhyāyyate yathā cātra pradhānagaṇasādhakau samupalabdhau stastathaiva yogatantre cāpi sthitiḥ punaratra praśnaḥ samudeti tantrasya bhāgacatuṣṭaye ekasmā eva sādhakāya vairocanādeḥ paramapadaprāptimārgo varṇitosti vibhinnacaturvidhasādhakānā sādhyamārgo vā varṇitosti etasya suspaṣṭamuttara paramādyatantre ittha varṇita  pañcatathāgatasādhanā vidhāyakeṣu yasmin trividha  kāmamohakrodhākhya samānarūpeṇa vidyate tebhyo mahārāgibhyaśca prathamabhāgorthāt dharmadhātumaṇḍalammahādveṣibhyaḥ dvitīyabhāgorthāt trilokavijayamaṇḍalammahāmohibhyaḥ tṛtīyabhāgaḥ sakalajagadvinayamaṇḍalākhyamahākṛpaṇebhyaḥ sarvārthasiddhimaṇḍala ca samupādeśi buddhaguhyācāryeṇāpīdameva prasthānamurarīkriyate  ācāryakunagā ñiṅapo mahodayopi sāmānyalaghutantre prāyastādṛśīmeva vārtām acakathatsādhakaḥ svaya kimapi nirṇayaṅkartumasamarthaḥ san yathā  yathā gurūnupalabhya teṣāmupadeśānanusaran kadācidrāgayuktamadhvāna kvaciddveṣayuktamapi bāhyaśuddhiprabhṛtimapi dharma matvā caryāḥ sampādayati  tadyathāvanmārge praveśayitu buddhena yogatantramupadidiśe   yathā ca    yogatantrasya prathamabhāge rāgiṇāmanugrahāya devānā varṇābharaṇaparidhānāni lohitavarṇatvena darśayatā prādhānyena rāgibhyaḥ  sādhanāvidhiḥ pratyapādi     dvitīyabhāge dveṣapradhānasādhakānanugrahītu bhayānakaraudrakṛṣṇavarṇedevarūpe sādhanāpaddhatiścāvarṇayata    sakalajagadvineyabhāge mohapradhānasādhakānugrahāya devānā śvetaśāntasvabhāvaparidhānābhūṣaṇādīnā śvetatva pradarśitam     caturthabhāge samānarūpeṇa doṣatrayayuktasādhakāya devānā varṇopi citravicitravarṇasvabhāve ābharaṇaparidhānānyapi naikaprakārakāṇyadarśyanta bustonopi evameva pratyapādīt ānandagarbheṇa yogatantrasya etadbhāgacatuṣṭaya svabhāvavipākasabhoganirmāṇakāyeṣu ādarśajñānasamatāyānapratyavekṣaṇajñānakṛtyānuṣṭhānajñāneṣu ca bodhicittadānapāramitāprajñāpāramitāvīryapāramitānā prādhānya kramaśaḥ bhāgacatuṣṭaye  sahaiva sayojya vyākhyāyi  kulānusāreṇa   prathamabhāgīyā devāstathāgatasya candramaṇḍalahṛdayādutpannāḥ  dvitīyabhāgasya devāḥ vajrakulikāḥ tṛtīyabhāgasya padyakulikāḥ bhāgasyāsya sarvadevāḥ avalokiteśvarasya cittavajreṇa nirmīyante sarvadevānāñcāyudhāni padyavajramālāpadyavajrapaṭaprabhṛtīni bhavanti  caturthabhāgasya sarve devāḥ ākāśagarbhacittavajra vyākurvāṇāḥata eva ratnakulikāḥ kathyante yadyapi devāḥ svaya krodharūpā bhinnarūpā vā na bhavanti yataśca paramapadāvasthā paramaśāntasyaiva bhavatikevala vineyajanāḥ prayojanavaśād vibhinnarūpeṇāvirbhavanti yathā ca tattvasagrahe aho mahopāyamaha buddhānā karūṇātmanām yatsatvārthatayā śāntā raudratvamapi kurvate  nāyametadabhiprāyaḥ yad ekena kenacitsādhakena bhāgacatuṣṭayasya sādhanānuṣṭhānenaiva viśuddhapadamavāpsyate para ca pratyeka bhāge kvacidekasādhanāpaddhatyanuśīlanenāpi  paramapada prāptu śakyate  yogatantrasya sādhanā dhyānatrayeṇāpi  adhiyogadhyānamaṇḍalarājāgradhyānakarmarājadhyānaiḥ  kriyate  tattvasagrahasya pratyeka bhāge uttamamadhyamamandaprakṛtikasādhakebhyastathaiva vistṛtā madhyamā sakṣiptā ca sādhanāpaddhatirūpadiṣṭā ānandagarbhaḥ tattvāloke avarṇayatyaḥ sādhakaḥ padyakulasya vistareṇa sādhanā cikīrṣati tasmai padyakulasvabhāvamahāmaṇḍalamdhāraṇīmaṇḍalamdharmamaṇḍalamkarmamaṇḍala ca vidyate yo hi madhyamā paddhatimabhipraititasmai mudrācatuṣṭayasya vyavasthāyaścātisakṣepeṇa bhāvanāmicchati tasmai ekamudrāmaṇḍala deśitam tattvasagrahe karmamudrādicaturvidhamudrāḥ caturbhiḥ kulaiḥ saha sayojya vyākhyātāḥ kāyamahāmudrāvairocanakulamcittasamayamudrāakṣobhyakulamvāg dharmamudrā amitābhakula cāste kṛtya  karma jñānamudrāsti yacca ratnakulasabhavam vibhājanādhāroya prādhānyamāśritya vartateanyathā tu buddho guhyatantrārthāvatāre kathayatikāya binā cittamasambhavam citta ca binā vāgapi na sambhavā ataḥ sarvakuleṣu catasro mudrāḥ sannihitāḥ santi sāratastu kathayitu yujyate tattvasagrahasyaikasya bhāgasya tadekasya vāṅgasya bhāgacatuṣṭayasya sādhanāmanuṣṭhāya bodhiḥ prāptu śakyā tenaiva vidvadbhistattvasagrahasya bhāgacatuṣṭaya pṛthak kṛtvā svātantryeṇa ṭīkā akriyanta
