vyākhyātantramatra ca mūlataḥ catvāro mukhyāḥ paricchedāḥ santi yathā     sarvatathāgataguhyasūtreśvaranāmapaṭalam   sarvatathāgataguhyatathāgatakulapaṭalam   trilokavijayavyākhyāpaṭalam   tathāgatavajrakulatattvavyākhyāpaṭala ca ṣoḍaśa tattvāni vyākhyātattvaviśatiḥ homaguhyavyākhyāprabhṛtayoneke avāntaraparicchedāḥ santi vajraśekharatantra hi vyākhyātantra na pratīyateyataśca etat sarvatathāgataguhyasūtreśvarākhyārambhika paṭalamuttaratantrasya vyākhyānaśailyanusāra praśnottararūpeṇopalabhyate nirvikalpo dharmārthaḥ kaḥ punaratra vikalpapratipādanābhiprāyaḥ kaḥ sādhanārthaḥ kaḥ kathamuttaratantramidam kimuttaram tantra kimucyate vajradharakrodhaśca kaḥ vajracaṇḍaḥ katha katividha ca tat ityādipraśnāḥ ekadaiva sakṣepeṇa pṛṣṭāḥ punaśca vistareṇa pṛṣṭāḥ tataśca praśnottararūpeṇa yathā katividhaḥ vajradharaḥ etaduttare kathita sarvadikṣu vyāptatvāt dharmadhātoranantatvād vajradharasyāpyānantyam asminneva granthe idamuttara katham tantra katha eva vākyāvekṣaṇāt prathamapaṭalamuttaratantram uttaratantrasya deśanāśailyāmupadiṣṭa vyākhyātantra vā pratīyate uttaratantrasya deśanā nidānaparivartopi pṛthaktvena nāsti atrāpi atha rājā vajradharaḥ  ityataḥ granthaḥ samārabhyata etenedamapi siddha  tattvasagrahasya deśanānantara tanmaṇḍale idamapyupadiṣṭam pārṣadapraśne taduttararūpeṇa uttaratantra diśyate bhagavatāyathā ca guhyasamājauttaratantram eva pratīyate vajraśekharasya prathamapaṭalamuttaratantrarūpeṇa avaśiṣṭaśca bhāgaḥ vyākhyātantratvenopādeśi   trilokavijayamahākalpaḥ vajrapāṇirākāśamārgādavatīrya sāṣṭāṅga bhagavanta vandate lokasthitakrūradurātmanā samayasavarayoḥ sthāpanavidhimupadeṣṭa  yadā nivedayate tadā bhagavān sumerūgirimaṇiratnāgrākhye prāsāde trilokavijayamahākalpasya deśanāvadhau anantadevanāgayakṣagandharvakinnarabhūtapiśācādibhiḥ  saha viharan kathayatiasmin trilokavijayamahākalpe vajrahuṅkāranāmakalpatathāgatakalpavajramahācakravidhivistārakarmamaṇḍalavidhivajrapāṇikalpaavalokiteśvarakalpagaganagarbhakalpagaganakośakalpakarmaprasarakalpa  vidyāmantramahākalpakarmasamūhakalpakarmadūtīkalpasevakakalpakarmavajrasamūhamātṛkalpakarmavajrīdūtīkalpakarmasevakakalpākhyāḥ vibhāgāḥ  santi  etāvanmūlatantram tadanu granthesmin vajrapāṇinā bhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ tathāgataḥ kathamutpadyatevajra kasmādutpadyate taduttareṇa bhagavatā yatkimapyabhihita taduttaratantramucyate  sarvadurgatipariśodhanakalpaḥ tantrasyāsya deśanā tathāgatena devasthānake nandanāmakavane cakre   paramādyatantram paramādyatantra kāmadhātoḥ paranimittavaśavartini devarājaprāsāde bodhisattvaavalokiteśvaravajrapāṇimañjuśrīākāśagarbhaprabhṛtibhyaḥ  samupadiṣṭam   asmin tathāgatakalpatrilokavijayakalpamuṣṭikalpavajracakrakalpaākāśagarbhakalpavajrayakṣakalpakulasagrahakalpavajrakulamaṇḍalakalpamahāsukhavajraamoghasamayakalpākhyāḥ  nava paricchedā vartante    vajragarbhālaṅkāratantram tantrasyāsya deśanā sarvatathāgatairadhiṣṭhitānantabuddhānā prādurbhāvasthāne vairocanahṛdayaprabhāsvaravimānatathāgatasthāne  vajragarbhālaṅkāre anantabodhisattvamahāsattvapariṣadi kṛtā   mahāmaṇḍalavidhijaladevamaṇḍalavidhiagnidevamaṇḍalavidhivāyudevamaṇḍalavidhijātattvavidhisrotovidhitathāgatakāyasiddhopāyikāprabhṛtayosya  prathamabhāgīyā viṣayāḥ   dravyasādhanopāyikāvāksādhanopāyikāmantrasādhanopāyikāsarvābhāsauṣṇīṣasādhanopāyikākleśavajrasādhanopāyikāsarvatathāgatamuṣṭisādhanopāyikāsarvatathāgatoṣṇīṣasādhanopāyikāśvetacchatrasādhanopāyikāsarvoṣṇīṣasādhanopāyikāmañjuśrīsādhanopāyikājagadīśvarasādhanopāyikāvajradharasādhanopāyikāmaitreyasādhanopāyikāākāśagarbhasādhanopāyikāsamantabhadrasādhanopāyikāsāgaramatisādhanopāyikāratnasabhavasādhanopāyikāprabhṛtayaḥ  imā buddhasya bodhisatvānā ca sādhanopāyikāḥ santi  yamāntakasādhanopāyikākrodhakaṇasādhanopāyikāhayagrīvasādhanopāyikābhiḥ krodhamaṇḍala sampadyate  anena sāka buddhalocanamudrāsādhanopāyikā  pāṇḍurāsādhanopāyikābhṛkuṭisādhanopāyikāmāmakīsādhanopāyikāvajramālāmayī sādhanopāyikācundāsādhanopāyikādibhirmantratattvaiśca  guhyamaṇḍala sampadyate   etadagre vajraratnamaṇḍalanābhicakradharmacakramaṇḍalagaganakośamaṇḍalavajrajinamaṇḍalasuvajramaṇḍalaprabhṛtayo naike maṇḍalavidhayopi  pratipāditāḥ  atrānte dvātriśallakṣaṇānāmaśītyanuvyañjanānā nāmāvalī tadvyākhyāna cāpyakāri  kāyavākcittaguhyabhūtālaṅkāratantram yogatantrasūcyā tantramidamapi bustonaḥ agaṇayat asya jñānaśreṣṭhamaṇḍalaguhyālaṅkāramahāmaṇḍalakāyavākcittaguhyākhya ca bhāgatrayamāste   āryaguhyamaṇitilakatantram etattantra bhagavatā akaniṣṭhabhuvane devarājagṛhe nivasatā bodhisattvavajrapāṇiavalokiteśvaraākāśagarbhavajramuṣṭiprabhṛtibhiḥ  navanavati    bodhisatvairguhyatilakopadeśāya nivedane kṛte sati samupādiśyata etasmin vajratilakapratyavekṣaṇadevītantravidhisarvatattvarahasyavidhivistāraparamatattvarahasyatilakākhyāścatvāro bhāgāḥ vidyante   pañcaviśatiprajñāpāramitāmukham etaddeśanā bhagavān sumerūparvate devadevaputrāsuravāyudevagarūḍanāgayakṣakinnararākṣasavidyādharabhūtavināyakapiśācaprabhṛtibhistathānantamātṛsamūhena  ca sāka viharan vyadadhāt  vajrapāṇirākāśādavatīrya bhagavanta parikramyopaviśatitadānī vajrapāṇi guhyādhipatināmnā sambodhayan  om bodhicittavajraprajñāpāramitāmukha hū om samantabhadracaryāprajñāpāramitāmukha hū aomakṣareṇa prārabhamāṇaḥ prajñāpāramitā pañcaviśativiśeṣaṇairalaṅkṛtya tanmukhamarthād muktidvāra  pratipādyādiśat  ittha yogatantrasya naike granthāḥ ye ca mūlatantravyākhyātantrauttaratantra sabhāgīyatantranāmabhiḥ jñāyante ḍogonachosajñalafagasapāmahodayena khasamatantra supratiṣṭhitantra cāpi yogatantrāntargatamabhimatam  yogatantrasya svarūpam gambhīrārthaparamārthasatye udārārthasavṛtisatyerthāt gabhīrodārābhāsaśūnyādvayasvarūpe pratiṣṭhāpanena yogatantramidamucyate yogatantre kāyamudrayā dehadharmamudrayā vāca samayamudrayā cittaiṣṭadevasya karmamudrayā kṛtyāni ca mudrayitvā dhyānabhāvanayā tathatā paramapā ca sādhakaḥ prāpnoti bustonasya kathanānusāreṇa yogatantre bodhiprāptividhermārgīkaraṇa bhavatiyataḥ pañcābhisambodhibhirdevabhāvanā kriyate parañcātrānuttaratantravad janmamṛtyuviṣaye samutpattikramaniṣpannakramabhāvanāvidhirna bhavati jñānasamuccaye yogatantrasvarūpa spaṣṭayatā bhagavatāvoci vidyādevībhiḥ saha maṇḍalasthaḥ san maṇḍalatattvādidaśatattvānuśīlakaḥ ubhayatantrī yogatantrī vā nigadyate trinayapradīpepi kathita yadanyebhyaḥ  yogatantribhyaḥ advayatattvabhāvanātyanta rocate te bāhyavibhinnacaryāḥ cittavikṣepakāraṇammanyanteadhyātmaviṣaya ca prerayanti tenaiva te caryātantriṇaḥ kathyante atra caryātantrī iti śabdābhiprāyaḥ yogatantrī śabdena grāhyaḥ yogatantrasyābhyantarabhedāḥ yogatantra kulānusāra pañcabhāgeṣu vibhajyate yathā    tathāgatakula   vajrakula    ratnakulam   dharmakulam    karmakula ca vistareṇa tu śata bhedāḥ pratyeka kulasya tathāgatakulatathāgatavajrakulatathāgataratnakulatathāgatadharmakula tathāgatakarmakula ca eva pañca bhavanti pratyeka pañcānā pañcaviśatikulānā punaḥ hṛdayamudrāmantravidyāmantrakulabhedena vibhāge kṛte sati śata kulāni jāyante hṛdayamudrāmantrādika spaṣṭayatā tattvasagrahe nigadita  manīṣitavidhānaistu sidhyate tu manīṣitam samādhisādhano hṛtsthaḥhṛdayastu tena cocyate duratikramo yathābhedyo rājamudrāgraśāsanaḥ mahātmacihnaviśvastutathā mudreti kīrtitā   anatikrama  ṇīyo  hi durbhedyo guhya eva ca mantryate guhyasiddhatva mantrastena nirūcyate   avidyāvipraṇāśāya vāgvidyo  ttama  siddhaye vidyate vedanāsiddhistena vidyā prakīrtitā   vajraśekharatantrepi kathita viṣamayaprāṇibhyaḥ pāpibhyaśca rakṣaṇatvāt mudreyamucyate mantroccāraṇād duṣṭaprāṇināmuccāṭana kleśakṣayaśca bhavati mantrabalena sādhakaḥ buddhabodhisatvaiścādhiṣṭhito bhavatiatoyammantraḥ vidyārāgādidoṣān prahāya tattva sākṣātkārayati ata eva vidyā kathyate dhāraṇī sarvadharmāśrayākuśalān nāśayati kuślāśca gṛhṇātiato dhāraṇīyamucyate padyakarapo kathayāmāsa hṛdaya hi kāyamudrā kāyasya kendra hṛdaya vidyate mahāmudrāyāmekāgratva dhyānam hṛdayasthaḥ san siddhi prāpnoti ato hṛdayamidam iṣṭadevasya hṛdayarūpi bījākṣarameva hṛdayamucyate tathāgatacaryāṇāmanukṛtiḥ sādhakena vidheyā bhavatitadatikramaṇamasambhavam ataḥ mudreyamasti mantro manaso doṣa nivārayati ata eva mantroyam vidyayā avidyānāśo bhavatijñānodayaḥ ata eva vidyeyamucyate  hṛdaya mahāmudrāpradhānasya kāyamaṇḍalatva mudrāsamayamudrāpradhānasya dhāraṇīmaṇḍala guhyamantradharmamudrāpradhānasya dharmamaṇḍalatva  vidyākarmamudrāpradhānasya ca karmamaṇḍalatvamucyate  dhāraṇīmaṇḍalasyābhiprāyo hi devīdhāraṇīnāmāyudharūpeṇa maṇḍalanyāsaḥ karmamaṇḍalatathāgatātiriktamanucaradevīnā nyāsaśca vidhīyate ete bhedāḥ sakṣepeṇa prajñopāyayoḥ samāviśanti bustonamahodayenābhihita  mantrakulābhiprāyaḥ upāyabhūtapitṛpradhāna vidyāmantrasya  prajñāyāḥ mātṛpradhānakula cāsti etaddvayamarthāt prajñopāyau akṣaratattve vilīya smṛtisaprajanyābhyā yuktena citta dūṣaṇatayā rakṣitu śakyate ataḥ ekasmin mantrakula eva sarvakulāni sammilanti ajñānasya pratipakṣijñānotpannatayā sarvadoṣakṣayaḥ guṇāvāptiśca bhavati ato vidyākulamapyucyate jñānaśrīviracite dvayāntanivāraṇe cāpi kathita  purūṣadevo guhyamantraḥ strīdevaśca vidyāmantrosti yanmantraḥ pitari mātari cobhayoḥ prayujyate sa dhāraṇīmantro nigadyate bustonamahāśayena tathāgatakula suspaṣṭayatābhāṇi sarvatathāgataprakṛtivajradhātuadhigamajñāna bodhicittasvarūpaprakṛtipariśuddhadharmadhātujñānameva ca vairocanakulamarthāt tathāgatakulamāste sarvatathāgatānujñānurūpopāyasvarūpa prāṇināmicchānusāra prakaṭitamādarśajñānamakṣobhyasvabhāvavajrakulamasti tathāgatānā dānapāramitāsvarūpa sattvānā manobhilāṣapūraka samatājñāna ratnasambhava ratnakula vidyate tathāgatānā prajñāsvarūpapratyavekṣaṇajñāna padyakulamastitathāgatānā vīryasvarūpasarvasiddhiḥ kṛtyānuṣṭhānajñānasvabhāvakarmakulamasti yogatantrepi prajñā mātṛtantramupāyo hi pitṛtantra cāsti ittha kāyavākcittaguhyālaṅkāravyūhatantre carcitam bustonopi laghusāmānyatantre vakti tattvasagraho hyupāyatantram daśatattvāni nirūpayati prādhānyeneda ata ida pitṛtantram paramādyatantram pañcaviśatiprajñāpāramitāmukhādigranthāḥ prajñāpradhānamātṛtantrāntargatāḥ ittha yogatantrepi mātṛpitṛtantrākhyeti bhāgadvaya kartu śakyate etat tantradvayasvarūpam anuttaratantrād bhinnam atrābhāsaḥ śūnyamātram yatra cānuttaratantre mahāsukhaśūnyattvam ābhāsaśūnyatāpi atra manonirmitamātram anuttaratantre vāyoḥ avadhūtyā praveśānantaram utthāpanavidhinā yuganaddhakāye prakaṭanameva ābhāsaśūnyatā cāsti  sārāśastu yogatantre kriyācaryātantrayorapekṣayā vistareṇa suspaṣṭarūpeṇa ca pañcābhisambodhibhāvanayā tathāgatakula krodhakulavajrakulapadyakulādīnā  svātantryeṇa sādhanāvidhirūpādiśyata  yogatantrasya sādhanāpaddhatiḥ yogatantrasādhanāyai sarvaprathama pañcakuleṣu kasyāpyekakulasya maṇḍala praviśya abhiṣeko labhyeta abhiṣekasamaye yasmin deve puṣpa patet sa eva sveṣṭadevo niścetavyaḥ abhiṣekasamaye sarvaprathama karmakalaśasya jalena snānīyam tadanu iṣṭadevakalaśenābhiṣeko labhyeta  tadā dvitīyacaraṇe tathāgatapañcakulānā paṭābhiṣeka tṛtīyacaraṇe vajrābhiṣeka caturthacaraṇe ca ghaṇṭābhiṣaka dattvā sādhakena puṣpa  pātita yadupari patet tadiṣṭadevakulānusāra nāmābhiṣeko dīyate  ye ca śiṣyābhiṣekanāmnā jñāyante tataśca vajrācāryābhiṣeke anāgāmiabhiṣekaguhyābhiṣekānujñāvyākaraṇāśvāsapraśasānāmakāḥ ṣaḍabhiṣekāḥ pradīyante eva yogatantre sādhakena ekādaśābhiṣekāḥ prāptavyā bhavanti jñānatilakatantre etad vistareṇa samupabṛhitam yaḥ sādhakaḥ tathāgatakulasavara na grahītu pārayatibodhisatvasavaramātra ca grahītu pārayati tasmai pañcaśiṣyābhiṣeka eva dīyate ye sādhakā bodhisatvasavara tathāgatakulasagraha ca grahītu samarthāstebhyaḥ vajrācāryābhiṣekopi pradeyaḥ etadabhiṣekaprāptyanantarameva sādhakena yogatantrasya nimnaḥ sādhanāvidhiranuśīlanīyaḥ yogatantrasya tridhyānacaturyogānā vā sādhanā caturmudrābhiḥ mudrayate atotra pūrva tridhyānasya mudrācatuṣṭayasya svarūpaparicayaḥ sāmānyena prastūyate tridhyānam sāmānyato yogatantrasyottamaḥ sādhakaḥ tridhyānena yogatantrapratipāditasādhanāpaddhatimanuśīlayati  tridhyānavidhi spaṣṭayatā bhāratīyaupādhyāyakumārakalaśena vajradhātumaṇḍalārthabhāvanāpiṇḍārthākhyagranthetisakṣepeṇa tridhyānabhāvanāyāstattva  svarūpa ca vivecitam  atra    ādiyogaḥ  maṇḍalarājāgraḥ   karmarājāgrākhyaśceti trividhadhyānābhāsaḥ kriyate atra kramaśaḥ sakṣepeṇa varṇayāmaḥ  ādiyogaḥ ādau nairātmya bhāvayitvā kramaśaḥ kṛkāṭikā  kāṣṭham  pariśodhanavighnotsāraṇasthānarakṣāmaṇḍalanirmāṇapuṣpādisamarpaṇavandanā pāpaprāyaścittapuṇyānumodanaabhyarthanācodanāpūjāviśatisvārpaṇapariṇāmanā  praṇidhānabodhicittotpādaviśatisavaragrahaṇabodhicittotkṛṣṭarūpotpādana svabhāvamaṇḍalanirmāṇamaṇḍalabhāvitamaṇḍalapratibimbitabhāvanāmudrābandhanaparyanta  kriyā sakṣepeṇa pūryyate  tadā vajrājalilakṣaṇa tadadhiṣṭhānamantraḥ vajrāveśotpattiḥ vajradṛdīkaraṇasarvadurgatyākarṣaṇapāpanivāraṇa mudrāmocana tattvaniratiśayatāsvahṛdayavajre hṛdayanyāsaḥcandradvayabhāvanā vajrabhāvanā ca vidhīyate sādhako yadā parahitāya sādhanāmācarati tadā tenānyamudrābhāvanamhṛdayanyāsaḥmudrāhaṅkāraḥpūrvakathitamaṇḍale praveśaḥvajrasattvabhāvanāsamayavajrasattvasya ahaṅkāraḥ jñānamudrayā mudritāhaṅkārastena cānyacaturṇāmadhiṣṭhānam mahāmudrāhṛdayammantrajapaḥ svahṛdaye maṇḍalabhāvanāmālā gṛhītvā japakaraṇam maṇḍalapraveśaḥmālā gṛhītvā uṣṇīṣabandhana mukhapaṭavimocanamaṇḍalanidarśanadarśanaprāptamaṇḍale dārdyāptiḥ  pañcābhiṣekaḥ pratyekamaṇḍalaśuddhyadhiṣṭhāna pratyekamaṇḍaladvārā ātmādhiṣṭhāna ceti dvinavatyuttarapañcaśata yogānā sādhanā karaṇīyā hṛdayamaṇḍale ekīkaraṇa svakāye candramaṇḍalānā nyāsastadanu ākāśe candramaṇḍalanyāsaḥhṛdayanyāsaḥ vajrāyudhādīnā nyāsaścetyebhistathā tadahaṅkāramaṇḍalotpannajñānatattvākarṣaṇālokanādibhirātmani vilīnatvamvarṇākārādihṛdayamantreṇa dṛdīkaraṇamtathāgatapraveśaḥ vajradhātu dhyātvā pañcatathāgatairadhiṣṭhāna caturdikṣu vajranyāsaḥmudrācatuṣṭayena mudraṇamsāmānyamantraṇena sarvamudrābandhanamśatākṣarīdhāraṇyā taddṛdīkaraṇapunarabhiṣekaprāptiḥsaharṣa nṛtyalāsyādinā pūjāvajraghaṇṭādikamādāya tattvamantroccāraṇamtriśabdagītigānaniḥsvabhāvātmakamantroccāraṇena saha nairātmyabhāvanāacalapraveśaḥ bhājanalokaviśuddhikaraṇamsāmānyapīṭhaviśeṣapīṭhasarvārthasiddhidhyānamarūpiṇī bhāvanāacalapraveśaḥ tathāgatairūtthāpanamtaddarśana  tadvandana tadupadeśaḥ pañcābhisambodhiśca    pratyavekṣā akṣobhyasvarūpa   bodhicittamutpādya dānapāramitāratnasambhavaḥ   vajrāviddhāmitābhaḥ    prajñāpāramitāsarvatathāgatakāyādiparamāṇuvadavasthitiḥ   vīryapāramitārthāt amoghapāśaḥ   rūpasya pariniṣpannatā  tathāgatasvabhāvavairocanosti vajraratnābhiṣekaḥ anujñādāna sumerūparvate vimānamaṇḍalabhāvanātathāgatacatuṣṭayadvārā sarvataḥ āvṛtya avasthitiyogādiyogadhyāna cāsti  uparilikhitatattvānīmāni ābhyantarasādhanayā saha sambaddhānīti tatraivoktam ābhyantaraātmasnānamkāyasmṛtyupasthānamjihvādhiṣṭhānavedanāsmṛtyupasthānam hastādhiṣṭhānacittasmṛtyupasthānavighnotsāraṇadharmasmṛtyupasthāna cāsti vighnanāśacittaṛddhipādaḥ vighnabandhanamīmāsāṛddhipādaḥvandanāsamutpannākuśaladharmatyāgaḥpūrvādivandanāanutpannasyotpādābhāvaḥ maṇḍalanirmāṇena pañcamaṇḍaladvāravandanāanutpannakuśaladharmotpādanam pāpaprāyaścittaprabhṛti viśatividhapūjā savaraprāptyavadhividhiḥ utpannakuśaladharmarakṣāete sarve sabhāramārgāḥ santi pratibimbabhāvanāyogādārabhya mahāyogaparyantamārgaḥ prayogamārgo vidyate yasmin vajrāñjalivajravandanāvajrāveśaḥ vajradṛdatā durgatipariśodhana śraddhendriya cāsti nairātmyabhāvanā vīryendriyācandradvayasya bhāvanā smṛtīndriyājñānasatvapraveśaśca prajñendriyosti hṛdayamaṇḍale maṇḍalanyāsaḥ śraddhābalamasti maṇḍalapraveśaḥ vīryabalamasti mālābhiṣekaḥ smṛtibalatrisamayagītiḥ samādhibalaśūnyatābhāvanā ca prajñābalamāste prayogamārgoyamasti akaniṣṭhabhuvane sūkṣmamanomayasthitiḥ dhyānabodhipakṣāṅgamasti sumerūbhāvanā vīryabodhipakṣāṅgam pīṭhabhāvanā prītibodhapakṣāṅgam sarvatathāgatagamana prasrabdhibodhipakṣāṅgamasti taddarśana dharmapravicayabodhipakṣāṅgam tadupadeśaḥ samyaksmṛtibodhipakṣāṅgamsvavāgacaladhyānasya tyāgaḥ upekṣābodhipakṣāṅgam darśanamārgoya yaddhi prathamapramuditābhūmiḥ ucyate pratyavekṣaṇā ca samyagdṛṣṭiḥ yā dvitīyavimalābhūmirūcyate cittotpādaḥ samyaksakalpaḥ yaśca prabhākarībhūmirastivajrātmaka bhāvanā hi samyakpariśuddhavāk arciṣmatībhūmiḥsarvatathāgatapraveśaḥ samyagvṛttirdurjayābhūmiḥrūpasiddhiśca samyagvyāyāmaḥ abhimukhībhūmiḥadhiṣṭhāna samyakkarmānta dūraṅgamābhūmiścāstiabhiṣekaghoṣavandane samyaksmṛtiracalābhūmiḥśatākṣarīdhāraṇī dvārā dṛdatāsamyaksamādhiśca sādhumatī bhūmiḥpañcānujñāprāptiśca dharmameghocyate etadbhūmayaḥ bhāvanāmārgāntargatāḥ  maṇḍalarājāgradhyānam vajrasadṛśadhyānasya pūrvāṅga sampūrayitu hetufalaprajñaptyā maṇḍalarājāgradhyānāvasthā bhavati arthāt hetoḥ falatvena parivartanāvastheyam   karmarājāgradhyānam atra prāṇinā karmaprādhānya vartate arthāt ekādaśabhūmisamantaprabhāyā buddhabhūmau vā buddhakṛtyameva karmarājāgradhyānamasti upādhyāyakumārakalaśena ānandagarbhaviracitatattvasagrahaṭīkāviṣayasya sakṣiptatva vihitamiti pratīyate  yataśca tattvasagrahasya prathamabhāgevajradhātumaṇḍalaṭīkāyā tridhyāna vyākhyāyamānena tena kṛkāṭikāpariśodhanāya kṛkāṭikāmadhye sravyamāṇa  hrīḥ  akṣarasya vivecanam aṣṭadalapāde vistareṇa paprathamataḥ ṣoḍaśaparyanta yogadhyānāntargata ṣoḍaśataḥ ūnaviśaparyanta    maṇḍalarājāgravyākhyā sfuraṇasaharaṇavidhiḥūnaviśatito dvāviśatiparyanta karmarājāgravidhirvivecitosti etadvyākhyāvalokanena pratīyate buddhatvāptiprakriyā ādiyogadhyāna vidyate yataḥ cātra bāhyamaṇḍalanirmāṇapūjāvidhiabhiṣekabodhicittotpādaprabhṛtīni varṇitāni  tatraivābhyantararūpeṇa saptatriśadbodhipakṣānanuśīlya daśabhūmiprāptirādiyogatvena buddhatvāvāptirvajrāsanākhyasamādhyavasthā maṇḍalarājāgratvena  buddhatvaprāptyagrimakṛtyāni ca karmarājāgratvena varṇitāni  vajraśekharākhyagranthānusāra tridhyānasyādiyoge svaya sādhakaḥ akaniṣṭhabhuvane pañcābhisambodhidvārā bodhi labheta eva dhyāyet tadanu bodhisatvasabhāsadān vyākṛtya maṇḍale nyaset dvitīyadhyāna pārṣadasya ātmānaścābhinnatā matvā prāṇinā hitasādhana karmarājāgradhyānamucyate  jñeyakośepi kathita  yogatantrasyottamena sādhakena akaniṣṭhabhuvane buddhatvamavāptu madhye sumerūparvatādi samupagamya anucarebhyo  yogatantropadeśaḥ ante ca vineyajanapātratānurūpa tān vibhinnakuleṣu praveśya tadanugrahavidhiḥ yā kriyate  sa tridhyānavidhiśca kīrtyate tattvālokepi sakṣepeṇaikatra tridhyāna vivecitam yathāsādhakaḥ padyakula dhyāyet devabhāvanāmahāmudrādhyānakūṭāgārapīṭhādīnā bhāvanā ādiyogī vidyate tadanantaramanyasamānadeva vyākṛtya nyāsakaraṇa dvitīya dhyānam sahārādhiṣṭhādīni tṛtīyadhyāne samāviṣṭāni caturyogaḥ ye ca sādhakā īdṛg bhāvanāmanuṣṭhātumasamarthāste caturyogadvārā yogatantra sādhayanti etannāmāni yogānuyogasarvayogātiyogākhyāni yatkule sādhakobhiṣeka prāpnot tatkulasya devabhāvanā yogosti tatra jñānadevamāvāhya vilīnatvamanuyogaḥ ucyate iṣṭadevasya bhājanalokasya sampūrṇasattvalokasya ca svabhāve bhāvanāvidhāna sarvayogaḥtriyogena caikāgratāprāptiratiyoga ucyate caturmudrāḥ tridhyānena caturyogena vā kayācitpaddhatyā vā yogatantra sādhayet taccaturmudrābhiḥ samudraya bhāvayet mudrābhirmudritakaraṇābhiprāyabodhanaviṣaye paramādyatantre kathitayo yayā mudrayā mudrayiṣyate saḥ tatsvabhāva eva syāt samayamudrayā mudrite samayadeve jñānamudrayāvāhito vilīnaśca deva eva jñānadeva ucyate caturmudrābhiḥ mudritasādhanānuṣṭhānena vibhinnajñānāni prāpyante yathā ca sūtrālaṅkāre rāgapañcendriyaparāvṛttyā paramavibhūtiprāptiḥ pratyapādyata tathaivātrāpi bodhyam    kāyamudrāyogenālayavijñāne āgantukabhrānti  mala vināśastathā darśanajñānamāvirbhavati   cittasamayamudrāyogena kliṣṭamanasaḥ bhrāntinirākaraṇa tathā samatājñāna mutpadyate    vāgdharmamudrāyogena manovijñānāgantukamala kṣīyate pratyavekṣaṇajñāna ca prādurbhavati    kāyavākcittaiḥ karmamudrāyogena pañcendriyāgantukamalakṣayaḥ kṛtyānuṣṭhāna codeti    dharmadhātujñāna sarvaprakṛtiṣu samānatayāvatiṣṭhate yogatantrasādhakaḥ caturmudrābhiḥ mudrito bhūtvā iṣṭadeva sādhayati atra mudrācatuṣṭayasya sāmānyaparicayapariśodhana pariśodhya falaprāptividhi ca pratipādayatā yogatantravarṇitamudrācatuṣṭayasvarūpa nirūpayiṣyate mudrābhiprāyastu anatikramaṇameva mudrā tathāgatopi  yathā rājñā svamurābhirmudryate rājaśāsanam mahātmanā svamudrabhirāmudryante tathā janāḥ kāyavākcittavajrāṇā pratibimbaprayogataḥ mahātmanā mahāmudrā iti vijñāya sidhyati mudrābhedāḥ mudrāyāḥ svarūpagatāścatvāro bhedāḥ yathā mahāmudrā dharmamudrā samayamudrā karmamudrāśca mudrāpariśodhyā dharmā api catvāraḥ yathā ca pṛthakjanakāyaḥ vākcitta karmamohakrodhau mātsarya kṣitiagnijaladhātavaśca mahāmudrayā kāyaḥ dharmamudrayā vāksamayamudrayā ca citta karmamudrayā ca karma pariśodhyate mārgānusāra mudrācatuṣṭayasya punaḥ lakṣyārthamudrālakṣitabāhyamudrā lakṣitābhyantaramudrāprabhṛtayastrayastrayo bhāvātmakā bhedā jāyante mahāmudrā vairocanādidevānā kāyaḥ eva rūpākṛtiḥ lākṣaṇikamudrāsti tatkāyasadṛśahastakriyā bāhyalakṣitamudrocyate tatkāle svaya vairocanādidevānā rūpabhāvanāvasthitiḥ ābhyantaradharmamudrā vartate dharmamudrā vairocanavācaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ brahyasvarā lākṣaṇikadharmamudrātvenābhidhīyante  svaya vairocana bhāvayitvā jihvākṛkāṭikādau hrīḥ ityakṣaranyāsena lakṣitā bāhyadharmamudrāsti tatprakāśyamānavacanānāmakṣararūpeṇodayaḥ  ābhyantaradharmamudrā kathyate  samayamudrā vairocanacittasya nirvikalpajñānameva vastutaḥ samayamudrā tatsadṛśakriyādirhi bāhyasamayamudrātenaiva ca sāka svaya vairocane bhāvitacittasya jñānarūpeṇodayaḥ samayamudrābhidhīyate karmamudrā vairocanasya kṛtya vastutaḥ karmamudrocyate svayam iṣṭadevavairocanasya bhāvanānantara prabhāsfuraṇasahārādividhīnāmanuśīlana bāhyakarmamudrāsti kṛtyasyānābhogarūpeṇa vicaraṇa ābhyantarakarmamudrā nigadyate pariśodhyā mahāmudrāpi caturvidhādharmakāyasabhogakāyanirmāṇakāyasvabhāvakāyākhyā mudritavidhiḥ mudrāhetuḥmudritavidhiḥsiddhihetuḥādhipatyaprāptiśceti catvāro mudritavidhayo bhavanti mahāmudrāhetuḥ vajramuṣṭiḥ kāyavākcittavajrasagraharūpā eva vajramuṣṭiḥ svabhāvasthitirmahāmudrāyā mudrito vidhiḥ devahṛdayakamale pañcāṅgavajrabhāvanā hi siddhihetuḥ gambhīrodārādvayayogasya bhāvanādhipatyaheturūcyate śabdoccāro dharmamudrāsti devakṛkāṭikāyā hrī ityakṣareṇa padyajihvayoḥ pañcāgravajra bhāvayitvā mantroccāraṇa dharmamudrāyā mudritavidhiḥ kīrtyate dharmākṣaravajra nābhi parito niviṣṭam eva bhāvana siddhihetuḥ  gambhīrodārādvayatattvastho bhūtvā jihvā tālau pravartya nāsāgre sūkṣmavajra bhāvayitvā tadekāgratva dharmamudrādhipatyaprāptividhiḥ kathyate vajrajapaśca samayamudrāhetuḥ  vairocanarūpeṇātmana parivartya śvāsapraśvāsābhyā saha kumbhakedvayatattvadhyānamātmanaḥ iṣṭadevāhaṅkāreṇa saha tattvasamāhitireva samayamudrāyāḥ  mudritattvamucyate  samādhyanantara tattvajñāna pañcāgrabhāvanāviṣayībhūta vidhāya triḥ mantroccāraṇa samayamudrāsiddhiheturabhidhīyate tadanu svaskandhādiśūnyatāpratipādanāya yuktibhirviśleṣaṇamādhipatyaprāptiheturūcyate tattvārthāvatāre pratipādyānusāra kāya binā vākvākya binā kāyaścittañca binā kāyopi na sambhāvyate ato yathā mudrācatuṣṭasya svasvamudritā vidhayastathaiva ekaikā mudrāpi caturmudrābhirmudraṇīyā kulānusāra tathāgatakulammahāmudrāvajrakula ca samayamudrāpadyakula dharmamudrāmaṇikula cārthāt karmakula karmamudrā vartate akṣayakāyanirmitistathāgatakulād bhavati cittavajrakulena yāvad yathāvacca jñānamanuṣṭhīyate vācā dharmapravacanādika padyakulamāste vibhinnakṛtyānā karmamudrātva maṇikulatva cāstiyataḥ etena sattvānā mahaddhita jāyate  yogatantrasya sādhanāvidhiviśeṣaḥ yogatantrasya sādhanāviṣaye ānandagarbheṇācāryeṇa sādhakasya samīpe anivāryarūpeṇa yogyatāsādhyanirdhāraṇasādhyopādānakārakasādhanopāyādiṣu  ki kimapekṣyate etadvarṇayatā sādhanāpaddhatiḥ spaṣṭīkriyate   sādhakayogyatā sa eva sādhakoyasmin praṇidhānaprasthānākhyobhayabodhicittamutpadyete etadubhayavidhacittasya spaṣṭīkaraṇa bodhicaryāvatāre ittha pratyapādiprāṇimātre bodhilābhecchā praṇidhānacittatadartha ca pāramitācaraṇa prasthānacittamucyate  etadubhayavidhicittasamanvitasādhakasya tantraśāstra pratyanavacchinnā śraddhā tathāgatapadaprāptyai pratipāditaśikṣāmanuṣṭhātu lālasā  mārgadarśakagurū śāstāra ca prati dradiṣṭho viśvāsaścāpekṣyate  vajreśvareṇāpyavoci gṛhasthenāpi tatsarvaśīlāni pālanīyāni yāni pravrajitebhyoparihāryāṇi santi   sādhyanirdhāraṇam sarvāvaraṇarahitaḥ guṇapūrṇaḥ kāyacatuṣṭasampanno vairocana eva yogatantrasya sādhyosti  ānandagarbheṇa tattvasagrahasya koṣālaṅkārākhyaṭīkāyā samabhāṇi tathāgatavajraskandhātmakavairocano laghuvairocano dharmadhātumayamādyantarahita  nirāvaraṇatattva mahāvairocanosti    upādānam ādyantarahitabodhicittasamantabhadraprakṛtiprabhāsvarapratyavekṣaṇālakṣaṇadevamantrādhāraviśuddhatattvāni vairocanaprāptyupādānakārakāṇi  sādhanā sevā sādhaneti bhedadvaya sādhanāyāḥ sevāyāḥ punaḥ upāyaprajñetha vā salakṣaṇanirlakṣaṇākhyau bheau kriyete  upāyotha vā salakṣaṇayogaḥ tridhyāna caturvidhayogo vā caturmudrābhirmudritaḥ kulamaṇḍalabhāvanā sthūlasalakṣaṇayogabhāvanocyate sthūlayoge dārdyaprāptyanantara sādhakaḥsūkṣmasalakṣaṇayoga bhāvayati sūkṣmasalakṣaṇayogasya bhāvanāyā tridhyāne caturyogeṣu vā kenāpyekena vidhineṣṭadevo bhāvyate jihvā tālau pravartya iṣṭadevavarṇasadṛśa tilopamasūkṣmasvarūpa nābhimadhye dhyāyyate  praśvāsena saha sūkṣmavajra śanaiḥ nābhikṣetrādutthāpya ghrāṇachidrād bahirniṣkāsanakāle upariśvāsa nirodhya smṛtisaprajanyasamanvitāḥ sādhakāścitta  tadvajrasvarūpastha vidhāya yathāsabhava dhyāyanti  tattvasagrahepi  jihvā tālugatā kṛtvānāsikāgrantu cintayet sūkṣmavajrasukhasparśādbhaveccitta samāhitam cittasya ghrāṇāgrabhāgasthitatvād vāyucitte śāmyataḥ nikhilakāye sukhamanubhūyate kāyaprasrabdhiriyamevocyate kāye vāyusacārapravāheṇa samarasatāgamanena vāyvāśritacittepi sahasā sthairyyamāyāti yā ca cittaprasrabdhirūcyate  tatpaścād yatheccha cittānukūlyārhatāyai sādhakaḥ pratidivasamabhyāsena viśiṣṭadhyānotpādanāya praśvāsakāle nāsikāgre anantasūkṣmavajrāṇi  sasfārya triloka vyāpnoti  śvāsāvadhau ca punaḥ nābhikṣetre sahṛtya sthairyya vidhātu śaknoti dhyānesmin viṣaye tattvasagrahepi  sūkṣmavajrasukhasparśanimitta jāyate yadā sfārayet tannimittantutaccitta sarvataḥ sfaret yatheccha sfaraṇāccitta traidhātukamapi sfaret punastu saharet tattu yāvannāsāgramāgatam tataḥ prabhṛti yatkicid bhāvayet susamāhitaḥ sarva caiva dṛdīkuryāt samādhijñānakalpitam tattvaloke salakṣaṇayogasya ādimadhyāntasādhanābhedena daśatattvairyuktaḥ sādhakaḥ syāt yathā  rūpārūpimaṇḍalam   bāhyabhyantaramantraḥ  caturmudrābhirmudritattvam  sthānayogarakṣe  jñānasatvānā sahāra āvāhana ca   vajraśabdena manasā ca mantrajapaḥ tridhyānādibhāvanā maṇḍalapūjādibāhyābhyantarahomaḥ  mudrāmocanamupasahāraśca  pūjānantara visarjana ca salakṣaṇayogasya daśa tattvānīmāni santi prajñā  nirlakṣaṇayoga bhāvanā sāmānyaprajñāyāḥ cittatattvasya sākṣātkārāya svasavedyajñānasthitireva nirlakṣaṇayogo vyāhriyate viśeṣayogatantrapaddhatyanusāra tattvasagrahe cāpi  aakṣarapraveśenasarvākṣaravijānanā svavaktra paravaktra tu bhāvayan siddhimāpnuyād salakṣaṇayoge pūrṇadakṣatayāpi yathāvadyāvajjñānayorbodhodhiprajñā nirlakṣaṇayoga vā binā na sambhāvyate nirlakṣaṇayoge hṛdayamudrāguhyamantradhāraṇīprabhṛtika prajñayā viśliṣya niṣprapañcatā pratipādyate nāmasaṅgīternimnavacanepi vārteya spaṣṭīkṛtā a ityasyārthonutpannosti ata eva  a  ityādi svarād vyañjanāccotpanna sarvabījākṣaram ādhāradeśavirahita nairātmya śūnya cāsti akṣareṣu sarvaśreṣṭhasya prathamasya akāra ityasyotpattiḥ kiñcidaṅgasahayoga binā jāyate yathā  mahāprāṇo hyanutpādo vāgudāhāravarjitaḥ akāraḥ sarvavarṇāgrayo mahārthaḥ paramākṣaraḥ akāro mahāprāṇānnirgacchati yaśca śūnyatāvabodhakaḥ tadeva sarvabījākṣarāṇi atra vaktramukhābhiprāyastu praveśadvāramataḥ sādhakaḥ svayamapi trivimokṣamukhācchūnyatāyā praviṣṭa ucyate svasammukha bhāviteṣṭadevasyāpi maṇḍale tadvatpraveśa svaya dhyāyettattvasagrahasyottaratantre cāpi  prajñā nairvedhikī nāma samādhiriti kīrtitā tayā tu mudrāḥ sidhyantebhāvayan sidhyati kṣaṇāt arthāt prajñānairvedhikī asti idamanutpanna nairātmyadarśanamniḥsvabhātābodhāābhāsaśūnyasthitireva nirlakṣaṇayogaḥ nigadyate nirlakṣaṇayogabhāvanayaiva druta siddhirlabhyate yathā tatraivoktam  vidyāmantra viśeṣāṇā viśeṣo na hi vidyate prajñayā bhāvayannevamāśu siddhirdhuvā bhavet  nikhilakathanasārastu  ubhayayogavidhau sanimittayogenaikāgratādhyāna sidhyati nirlakṣaṇānimittadhyānena nairvaidhikaprajñayā pratyavekṣaṇātmakadhyānena  vipaśyanayā ubhayayuganaddhadhyānena ca yuganaddhafala labhyate   sāmānyajapavidhiḥ viśeṣasiddhisādhanākramasca japavidhiḥ tridhyāne caturyogeṣu vā kiñcidekapaddhatyā iṣṭadevabhāvanānantara siddhyartha japonuṣṭhīyate sāmānyataḥ japasya bhedadvayam  vajrajapaḥ śabdajapaśca siddhabārāvāmahodayena japasya ṣaḍbhedāḥ pratyapādyanta  śvāsapraśvāsayordhyānāvadhāna binā cittasya aakṣare kendrīkaraṇa nirodhajaposti śvāse ao praśvāse hū  āḥ  ityakṣarasahitavāyoḥ pūrakarecakakumbhakādividhāna vajrajapobhidhīyate    hṛdayakamale iṣṭaevamantrasya bījākṣara bhāvayitvā tadraśmipujasya sfuraṇa saharaṇa ca kṛtvā tathāgatānā pūjā prāṇihita ca vidadhat  yaḥ sādhakastasya bhāvanāvidhāna sfuraṇasaharaṇajapaḥ ucyate   manasi eva japakaraṇam dhvani binā tālujihvauṣṭhabalena japānuṣṭhānam  sāmānyadhvaninā sāka śabdamātrāḥ dhyātvā japavidhānam japasyaitat ṣaḍrūpāṇi tattvasagrahe japabhedā nimnāḥ nātisyanditajihvāgradantoṣṭhadvayasayutā sādhayet sarvakalpān tu vajravāksvaravarjitā meghadhūlitahūkārakrodhagambhīravāk sthirā krodhasfuṭā mahāvajra vajrakrodhavāksādhanam anucchvāsa sūkṣmaśvāsa sūkṣmavācā susasfuṭam sidhyante sarvajāpānisamādhijñānagarbhayā vajrajapaḥ svayamiṣṭadevabhāvanānantara svopameṣṭadeva svasamakṣa bhāvayet prāṇāyāma ca vidadhyāt vāyupraśvāse sammukheṣṭadeve citta sthāpayet śvāse svadehakāyabhāvitadevakāyayorabhinnatva bhāvayet antarvāyunirodhakāle manasi mantrajapaḥ kriyateayameva savṛtisalakṣaṇayuktaḥ vajrajapobhidhīyate svaya sādhako devamantraprabhṛtayaḥ sarvepi dharmaśūnyagaganavat pariśuddhāḥeva matvā yathāsādhya śūnyatāyā vāyu nirodhya tiṣṭhet vāyumuktikāle iṣṭadevalakṣaṇamātra smaret punaḥ śvāsāvadhau paramārthasthito bhūtvā vajrajapānuṣṭhāna paramārthavajrajapaḥ kathyate japavidhiraya tīvrendriyasādhakasya lokottarasiddhiretenāvāpyate śabdajapaḥ mṛdvindriyaḥ sādhakaḥ śabdajapamanukaroti  yathā sādhakaḥ sveṣṭadevāsana vidhāya vāmahaste sveṣṭadevāyudha dhārayitvā dakṣiṇahastena kulānusāra mālā dhṛtvā kulamantrajapavidhimanusṛtya  suspaṣṭa japati sa ca śabdajapo vyāhriyate etasmin laghudīrghādimātrā pūrṇataḥ dhyātvā japonuṣṭhayo bhavati etena dravyakhecaravidyādīni sidhyanti viśeṣasiddhicaryā samādhijapavidhihometividhitrayeṇa siddhiścaryyate sevāyā viśeṣasūkṣmavajradhyāne ca dārdyaprāptyanantarameva lokalokottarasiddhīnā lābhāya caryā vidhīyate lokasiddhisādhanāvidhimāśritya tattvasaṅgrahe cāpi  vajrabimba nidhistha tu hṛdaye paribhāvayet bhāvayan bhūmisasthāninidhānāni sa paśyati vajrabimba samālikhya gagane paribhāvayet patedyatra tu paśyeta nidhi tatra vinirdiśet svahṛdayakamale nidhikalaśa tadupari candramaṇḍalatadupari ca pañcāṅgavajra bhāvayitvā vajranidhistāvad japanīyo yāvacca sparśadarśanādilakṣaṇa prakaṭita na syāt athavātmani viśvavajram ākāśe cāpi vajra bhāvayitvā japānuṣṭhānena vajrapatanābhāsaḥ yatra syāttatraiva nidhirlapsyateeva vijñeyam  tathaiva jalopari pracalanasiddhyai jalasrotasi kiñcicchāntasthāne vā mahatpātre jala prapūrya tatparipaśyatā vajrajalasya japo vidheyaḥ jala  ca vajratvena paravartitamiti cintanīyam  śanaiḥ śanaiḥ jala vajrasadṛśamābhāsiṣyate tadanu yogī yadaiva jala jigamiṣet tāvat samādhau samāhitya gatyavāptisāmarthya labdhumarhati sarvatathāgatatattvasaṅgrahepi  vajrāveśe samutpanne vajrabimbamaya jalam bhāvayed yastu yogīndrojalasyopari caṅkramet lokottarasiddhyai svaya pañcatathāgateṣu kimapyeka bhāvayitvā vajradhātu hū  ityuccārayan ākāśaḥ tathāgatakāyairvyāptaḥ ittha vicintya vāyuśvāsakāle yathā sikatāyā jala śuṣyatitathaiva sarvatathāgatāḥ svahṛdayakamale vilīnāḥ praśvāse ca punarākāśamaṇḍale vyātāḥeva dhyāyet eva dhyānena sādhako buddharūpadhārako bodhisattvo vidyāmantradharaśca bhaviṣyati  mṛdvindriyo madhyendriyaḥ vā sādhakaḥ kramaśaḥ janmatraye ṣoḍaśajanmasu vā mahāmudrāsiddhimavāpya pañcābhisambodhibhirakaniṣṭhabhuvane pañcajñāna  sākṣātkṛtya bodhi labhate  tīvrendriyajanaḥ ekajanmatryapi yogatantrasādhanayā paramapadamavāptumarhati upasahāraḥ sāmānyato mudrā śabdaḥ sūtratantrayorūbhayatropalabhyate  bauddhaparamparāyā tvekedṛśī mudrā svīkriyate yadīya svarūpamittham    saskṛtadharmonityaḥ kṣaṇikaśca  āsravadharmaḥ duḥkham   sarvadharmāṇāmātmaśūnyatva  nairātmya ca    nirvāṇa paramaśāntam ime anatikramaṇīyāścatvāraḥ ato mudrā nāmnālaṅkṛtā ime yaḥ etaccaturmudrāḥ mattvā calatisa bauddha itare cābauddhāḥ agre sūtreṣu śūnyatādīnā mudrātvenābhidhānam  yathā ca sāgaramatiparipṛcchāsūtre kathita  he sāgaramate sarvadharmastu vimuktimudrāmudritaḥ advayaḥ pariśuddhaśca sarvadharmo gaganavadabhinnaḥ  ataḥ sarvadharmaḥ samatayā mudritosti agre ahaṅkārasya pariśuddhatvena vimalamudrāsti ittha viśatirmudrāḥ gaṇitāḥ  maitreyaparipṛcchāsūtrepi he kulaputra sarvadharmeṣu śūnyatāsvarūpamurāsti ratnadārikaparipṛcchāyā kathita sarvadharmasvabhāvo gaganopamaḥ etallakṣaṇameva mudrāyāḥ kadācit prajñāpāramitā cāpi mudrātvenābhihitā mañjuśrīmūlakalpe madhyamāṅgulisaśliṣṭau bhavedekaśikhā dhruvam eṣā mudrā mahāmudrāsabuddhaistu prakāśitā hastamudrāścāpi mudrārūpeṇa pratipāditāḥ vairocanābhisambodhitantre devāyudhāyāpi mudrāśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ yogatantre sveṣṭadevakāyasadṛśa svaya bhāvanameva mahāmudrāprabhṛtyaścatasraḥ mudrā abhihitāḥ yadupari savarṇitam anuttaratantrepi yogatantravadeva mahāmudrādiścaturmudrāścarcitāḥ para ca svarūpato bhinnatvam yathā ca hevajratantre vajram abhedya jñānam tenānena mudryate mud harṣaḥ mahāsukha janyate tena hetunā mudretyucyate mudrārthastat tattva yena mud harṣaḥ athavā mahāsukhamutpādyate etasya catvāro bhedāḥ tathā ca nāgārjunaḥ caturmudropadeśe  karmajñānamahāmudrāsamayākhyaḥ prabhāsvaraḥ heturbhāvyāstathā prāpyaścaturdhā cāvinaśvaraḥ etasyānuttaratantre naikavidhā vyākhyāssanti tatra ca prāyaḥ karmotpannā strīkarmamudrā manomayakālpanikamudrā ca jñānamudrā sarvākāravaropetaśūnyatā hi mahāmurocyate akṣarasukhātmakaprakṛtyābhisambodhilakṣaṇaprabhāsvaratattva ca samayamudrā hetoḥ karmamudrātvasādhanasya jñānamudrātvasādhyasya mahāmudrātvamanābhogāvasthāyāśca samayamudrātva vocyate eva mudrāśabda ekasminnapi tatsvarūpabhinnatva dṛśyate tridhyānaśabdasya yogānuttaratantrayoḥ prācuryeṇa prayogovalokyate ubhayatrādiyogaḥ svārthāya maṇḍalarājāgra karmarājāgra ca parārthāya bhāvyate tathaiva caturyogaprayogopi pitṛtantragrantheṣu lakṣyate śabdasya sāmye satyapi bhāvadṛṣṭyānuttaratantrasyotkṛṣṭatvam yato hyanuttarayogatantra utpattikramabhāvaneṣṭadevabhāvanā vā prajñopāyayuganaddharūpeṇotthāpyate candrabījākṣarāyudhāni tu pañcābhisambodhinā bhāvyante yāvadāliṅgana sīmita yogatantre rāgamārgīkaraṇam para cānuttarayogatantre samāpattidvayānta prādarśi mārgīkaraṇavidhiḥ anuttarayogatantrasādhanāvidhiragre vakṣyate etadubhayatantrasya sādhanāṅgābhidhānasāmyāt tadubhayamekatraivābhimanyate naikairvidvadbhiḥ anuttaratantreṣvapi tridhyānaśabdaḥ prayujyate yogatantrāddhi tadbhinnatvameva abhidhānasāmyāt bhārate paramparādvaya prāvartata ekā baṅgaprānte jagaddalamahāvihārasyāparā hi madhyadeśasya  śākyasampradāyasya jamagona amas jabsa ityasyābhimate jagaddadalanṛpaḥ prakāśacandro yo hi vajrasattva  nirmāṇakāya ucyate tacchiṣya ānandagarbhastārādvārā  vyākṛta āsīt   nṛpaprakāśacandrānusāreṇa guhyasamājamūlatantra vairocanamāyājāla ca tattvasaṅgrahanyāyadiśā rakṣācakrādidaśatattvairmudrācatuṣṭayena ca  sammudrya vyākhyāyyate  ānandagarbhamatānusāreṇa bodhi prāpya saptadinānantara tathāgatena tattvasaṅgrahodiśyata tadanūpadiṣṭamātṛtantre buddhakapālasya pitṛtantre guhyasamājasya māyājālādīnā ca vyākhyā tantratvena vihitā pūrvabhāratīyairbudhaistantrasya kriyācaryāyogākhyo bhedo manyate caryātantrātparavartitantrāṇi yogatantra eva sagṛhyante yogānuttaratantrayorekatvam nāmasaṅgītyādivyākhyā mañjuśrīprabhṛtibhiretaddiśaiva kriyate  tatraiva jamagona amas jabsābhimatenottarabhāratīyavidvāso nṛpāśca tantreṣu kālacakratantrasya śreṣṭhatvamaṅgīkurvanti hevajracakrasavaraguhyasamājādīni  vyākhyānti kālacakrapaddhatyā ceti   pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ anuttaratantram anuttaratantrasyābhyudayaḥ pitṛtantramātṛtantraadvayatantrarūpeṇa anuttaratantrasya bhedatrayamasti atra kramaśaḥ pitṛtantrasyābhyudaya vicārayāmaḥ pitṛtantrasyābhyudayaḥ tatra pitṛtantra vineyajanānāmanugrahārtha rāgadveṣamohādīnā prādhānyāt bhedatraye vibhajyate rāgiṇā kṛte guhyasamājaḥdveṣapradhānasya kṛte yamāritantra tathā mohapradhānāya ca nāmasagītiścopādeśi guhyasamājoya pitṛtantrasya pradhānagranthaḥ mūlatantrasya ślokasakhyā  sahasra tathā sagrahamūlatantrasya  ślokasakhyā svīkṛtā yā ca  paricchedeṣu prāyojitā sagrahatantrasya yadā kadā mūlatantratvenābhihita yato hi  tame paricchede uttaratantre sagrahatantrasya praśnānutthāpya tadvyākhyā kṛtāsti prāyaḥ kriyate cāpi ācāryaseratogapādasya kathanamasti yad guhyasamājaḥ sāmānyataḥ sarvatantrāṇā mūlamastītiyato hyatra kriyātantrādinimnāṅkitatantratraye samāgatasanimittasadasadyogadvārā prāptavyasiddhermārgopi samupalabhyate atoya samājatvenābhihitaḥ  tamaparicchedasyottaratantratvābhiprāya spaṣṭīkurvatā tatraivokta yadaya guhyasamājopyastītiyato hi tantrasyāsya deśanā tasminneva vimānamaṇḍale tathānucaradevānā madhye tadeva krameṇa kṛtā vidyate tathyato guhyasamājasyāvagatistadaiva bhavet yadā tad vyākhyātantrāṇā samyagrūpeṇādhyayana syāt asya vyākhyātantraṣaṭkamastiyathāguhyasamājasyāṣṭādaśaparicchedaḥ caturdevī paripṛcchā sandhivyākaraṇanirdeśaḥ vajramālājñānavajrasamuccayastathā bhoṭabhāṣāyāmanupalabdho devendra paricchedaśca aṣṭādaśaparicchede uttaratantra guhyasamājasya pratipariccheda praśnottararūpeṇa samādadhad vyākhyāti caturdevīparipṛcchātantra prāṇāyāmavidhīn prakāśayat rahasya spaṣṭa nirdiśati sandhivyākaraṇanirdeśatantra guhyasamāje samāgatayorvajrajāpotannakramayornihitārthābhiprāya spaṣṭayati vajramālātantra mṛtyujanmaantarābhavanāḍīvāyutilakaabhiṣekavidheḥ  prabandhānām utpattikramasya tridhyānacaturyoga tattvānā devānā niyatārtha a ādi  akṣarāṇā vyākhyādvārā nidānaparivartadvārā ca tantrasya sampūrṇāṅgāni sagṛhya spaṣṭavyākhyā karoti jñānasamuccayatantra guhyasamājasyābhidheyasālaṅkārāṇā tathā  māyākāyasādhanā vidhīnā ca spaṣṭanirdeśa karoti dagapoṭaśīnamagyalasya kathanamasti yad guhyasamāje  devānām aspaṣṭavyākhyā vidyatevajramālā tā vyākhyā spaṣṭayatīti utpannakramasambaddhe mūlatantre  vidhayopyapūrṇāstānapi prapūrayati jñānasamuccayaḥ guhyasamājamūlatantrasya śabdān saptālaṅkārairalaṅkṛtya tadvyākhyā karoti sandhivyākaraṇa ca mūlasya rahasyābhiprāya spaṣṭīkṛtya vyākhyāti eṣā granthānā sakṣiptaparicayotra prastūyate guhyasamājaḥ asya tantrasya deśanāsambandhe pūrvamuktam atra  paṭalāni santi aṣṭāśa paṭalamuttaratantratvena svīkṛtamasti  bustonamahodayobhidheyena saha sayojya eṣā paṭalānā gaṇanā kṛtavān yathā    nidānapratipādanapūrvakotpattiniṣpannakramayornirdeśaḥ  utpannakramabodhicittanirdeśaḥ  pariśuddhadevayogaḥ  cittamaṇḍalebhiṣekavidhernideśaḥ   yogacaryā  kāyavākcittādhiṣṭhānam  yogacaryāyāvistāraḥ   guhyābhiṣekaḥ  adbhutavyākaraṇanirdeśaḥ  siddhyabhimukhabāhyābhyantaradevahṛdayacodanā mantradevajñānadevayorūtpattiḥ mahāmudrāpariśīlanam ābhyantarapravṛttakarmasamūhaḥ māyāsadṛśadhyānam  kāyavajramaṇḍalātirikto mṛṇmayamaṇḍalavistāravidhiḥ samayasavarayoḥ pradhānanirdeśaśceti  aṣṭādaśa paṭalamuttaratantramasti etanmaitreyādibodhisattvaiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ tathāgataḥ sādhu sādhviti bruvan uttararūpeṇopadiṣṭavān  siddhathaganapādamatānusāramatra  praśnānā bhavyakīrtimatānusāra  praśnānā tathā viśvamitraracitaśrīguhyasamājatantropadeśasāgarakaṇamatānusāra   praśnānāmuttare bodhisattvānā sandehasya nirākaraṇa jātam  viśvamitrānandagarbhau tattvasagrahamanu samastatantraśāstrāṇi uttaratantrattvenopadiṣṭānīti svīkurūtaḥ vajramālādivyākhyātantrāṇā deśanā ācāryaalakalaśamatānusāra vibhinnasthaleṣu jātā  auḍiyānottaraparvate vajrasattvaḥ daśakrodharūpeṇa prakaṭībhūya daśa dikpālān vineyān kartu  sahasraślokātmikāyābṛhadvajramālāyāstathā  laghuvajramālāyā upadeśa kṛtavān   sandhivyākaraṇatantrasya himālaye devībhiḥ kṛtāyā prārthanāyā caturdevīparipṛcchātantrasya vaipulyaparvate jñānavajrasamuccayasya ca gaṅgātaṭe  upadeśo jātaḥ   atra vyākhyātantrāṇā sakṣiptaparicayo nirūpyate vajramālā vajramālākhyo niṣpannakramāṅgaprakāśakaḥ sarvato mahatvapūrṇo bṛhad granthaśca  svīkriyate  cakrapāṇinā pṛṣṭena bhagavatā uttararūpeṇa  paricchedeṣu vibhaktasyāsya tantrasya deśanā kṛtā  nidānaparivartaḥ   ācāryaśiṣyayoḥ parīkṣādvārā abhiṣekavidhiḥ   vajramālānāmnorthaḥ  vāyūnā nāmānisthitiḥ sacāravidhistathā vajramālāśabdasya bhedaḥ  samājaśabdasya vyākhyā  śūnyatāśabdasyārthaḥ  vāyutilakabhedaḥ  vajrajāpayogastathaitaddvārā paramapadasya prāptividhiḥ nādaśabdasya vyākhyā  guhyārthabhagaśabdasya dharmadhātutvena vyākhyā  savaraḥ samayaśca bhakṣyapeyādisamayānā nītārthe vyākhyā mantratattvasya vyākhyā vāyutattvavāyugaṇanādvārā japavidhiḥvāyukṛtyānivāyutattvānā nirdeśana ca  caturabhiṣekāṇām arthastathā mahāmudrāśabdasya vyākhyā nāḍīśūnyatāpadyavāyuhṛdayavajrapadyayogaḥ guhyamantratattvam  vāyorāśrayeṇa kṣaṇe kṣaṇe prāṇānā vilayodayadarśanādamita vāyūnā prāptyupāyaḥ caturnāḍīcakrāṇā samūhe nāḍīnā sakhyā tathā tannāmāni pramukhanāḍīṣu samastanāḍīnā sagrahaḥ vipākādicaturdharmāṇā nirdeśaḥ caturānandānā lakṣaṇa bhedaśca  mantratilakavāyutilakadravyatilakānā bhāvanāvidhireva bhedaḥ  ao āḥhū iti akṣaratraye nāḍīvāyuvikalpānā bhāvanāvidhirarthāt kāyavākcittānā hṛdayarūpeṇa vyākhyā  guhyanāsāgranābhināsāgramukhanāsāgrādīnā tathā pañcavāyūnā varṇana teṣā sacāravidhireva dravyamantratilakānā bhāvanāvidhiśca  śūnyatāśabdasya vyākhyā kāyaskandhaāyatanānā dhātūnā ca devatātvena nirdeśaḥ lakṣaṇa ca  caturnāḍīcakreṣu sthitānā devīnā nāmāni kramaśca nāḍīnā devīrūpatvena pratipādanatāsāmudayāstayoryogikavidhiḥ  ṣaḍnāḍīcakrasamūhadvārā mahāsukhasya kalpitavidhistathānandānā lakṣaṇam  nāḍīṣu śukraśoṇitavāyūnāmāveśavidhistāsā lakṣaṇa ca pramukhanāḍitrayasya kṛtyam daśavāyubhiḥ viṣṇordaśāvatāravaccharīrasyotpattividhiḥ vāyunotpattimanu kramaśo vāyuvyayena saha prāṇakṣayaḥ  cāṇḍālyāgnidvārā samastaḍākinīnā sagrahaḥ  utpattiniṣpannakramābhyā vikalpasya nirodhavidhiḥ arthāt vikalpavāyośchedasya lakṣaṇam  nirvikalpavāyoḥ svādhiṣṭhāne nirdeśo nirvikalpalakṣaṇamvāyorbhāvanayā nāḍīcakrasyāstanirūpaṇam caturnāḍīcakraagnicakravāyucakraiśca saha ṣaṭcakrāṇā bhāvanā caturthābhiṣekasyārthasfuṭīkaraṇam guhyapadasya nirdeśaḥ dharmadhātorvyākhyā vajrasyārthaḥ ekakulāt  kulānāmutpattistathā teṣāmekasmin kule vilayaḥ  caturmudrākarmamudrāyāḥ ṣaḍbhedastathā teṣāmekasmin kule vilayaḥ mahāmudrāyā bhedaḥ skandhāyatanayorlakṣaṇam mahāmudrāyā bhedāḥ nāḍīṣu vāyorāśritatvād utpadyamānānāmaṣṭānubhūtīnā spaṣṭīkaraṇam ahaśabdasya vyākhyā aṣṭādaśaśūnyatāyāḥ lakṣaṇam vāyutattvasya śūnyatāyā bhāvanākaraṇāt vajramālotpattiḥrātrindinasya vistṛtavyākhyā ālokālokabhāsayorjātikālanirdeśastathā tadvistṛtavyākhyā sīmāntarodayalakṣaṇavyākhyā viśatividhiḥ viśatividheḥ kāryakaraṇasya pratipādanam bāhyapūjāyāḥ parityāga vidhāyādhyātmapūjāvidheḥ pratipādanam nāḍyā devyā nirdeśastathā devīnā lakṣaṇam eva śabdasya vyākhyā nidānaparivarte samāgatānā akṣarāṇāmekaikaśo vyākhyā adhyātmahomavidhiḥ amṛtaguṭikāsadhanāvidhistathā pañcāmṛtabhakṣaṇavidhiśca gaṇacakravidhisaketaḥsaketapratyuttaravidhiśca vāṇīsaketaḥ guhyaśabdasya pratipādana ca ācāryakāyena sampūrṇakāyavākcittamaṇḍalanirdeśaḥ buddhadharmasaghalakṣaṇam śiṣyacaryā śāntyādīnā karmaṇā ca falanirdeśaḥ catuḥkrodha  devamālānā sevanena karmaṇaḥ sādhnāvidhiḥ pañcābhijñāsādhanāvidhiḥ  prabhāsvarayuganaddhasya sādhanayā kāyamaṇḍaladevānā pariśuddhividhiḥ  ante bodhisattvasyānuttarādibhagavataḥ stutiḥ atraiva vajramālātantrasya samāptirjāyate caturdevīparipṛcchātantram asya prārambhe eva mayā śrutam  iti nāsti yato hi mūlatantrasya deśanayā sahaiva vyākhyātantratvenopadiṣṭam  atra locanādvārā bhagavataḥ kāyotpattividhau pṛṣṭe sati uttare sūkṣmamantratattvayogadvārā  kāyaniṣpattividhirabhihitaḥ  aya locanāparipṛcchāparicchedosti   māmakīdevīdvārā tilakabodhicittasya gamanāgamanavidhau pṛṣṭe sati tatspaṣṭīkṛtaḥ māmakīparipṛcchāparicchedobhihitaḥ   śukraśoṇitābhinnatilakasagrahe arthāt dhātusagrahe pañcaskandhasya niṣpannavidhi spaṣṭīkurvatā yatra pañcatathāgatānā pratipādana yo hi pāṇḍarīparipṛcchāparicchedobhidhīyate  tārādevīdvārā bodhicittataḥ kāyotpattividhau pṛṣṭe sati bodhicittasādhanākāyādimaṇḍalānā bhedatrayamābhyantarahomaḥ ābhyantarapūjādīnā kāyādimaṇḍalānā bhedatrayamābhyantarahomaḥ ābhyantarapūjādiścopādeśi yadupaśrutya casro devyaḥ prābhasvarapadamāpnuvanti tāsā samastasandehā nivartante itthamaya caturthaparicchedaḥ tārāparipṛcchāparicchedobhidhīyate jñānavajrasamuccayatantram atrāpi nidānasyollekho na kṛtaḥ  maitreyādibodhisattvadvārā kṛtāyā prārthanāyā tricittarahasyasāmānyārthaparyantārthaṣaṭkoṭivyākhyātantranāmakṛtaāvartanavidhisādhyasādhanāsaptālaṅkārāṇā  deśanā kṛtā vidyate  bustonamahodayasya kathanamasti yadida bṛhadjñānavajrasamuccayasyāṅgamātramasti pūrṇantvaprāpyamasti śrīvajragarbhālaṅkāraḥ atra  paricchedāḥ santi yathā bodhicittaprakṛteḥ sarvadharmiṣu vyāptistathā vajraḍākinyadhiṣṭhānam mantraḥ  mṛṇmayamaṇḍala nirmāya pūjāarpaṇā dvārā śiṣyasya maṇḍalapraveśavidhistathā rekhācitramaṇḍalaparicchedaḥ  caturabhiṣekavidhistathābhiṣekaguṇāḥ   maṇḍalābhisamayanirdeśaḥ  yogasādhanātriyogabhedastathā bodhicittabhāvanādvārā jñānasampādanavidhiḥ  kāyavākcittasamayānā nirdeśaḥ uṣṇīṣābhisamayaḥ vajragarbhālaṅkāratantranāmavyākhyādvārā trijñānanirdeśaḥkrodhadevayogāt śatrunāśavidhiḥ tantrāṇā sakhyā  tantraśāstrāṇā bhedāḥ pañcatathāgatakulānā samayaḥādikarmikasamayaḥ catasro mūlāpattayaḥsthūlapattayaścabhakṣyasamayaḥ prayojanavaśādupadiṣṭānyasamayaḥ uccastarīyayogīnā kṛte nirdiṣṭasamayastathā samvaraśca  mahāvetālīsādhanā gurorbhedastasya sevanavidhistathā guṇasahitasya prajñālakṣaṇasya parīkṣā prabhāsvaraprakaṭīkaraṇavidhiḥ sarvacaryāparicchedaḥ  utpattikrameṇa sambaddha tridhyānapañcābhisambodhiḥniṣpannakramaḥ triśūnyatāālokaḥ ālokābhāsastathābhāsalabdhasya viṣayaḥbāhyābhyantarāṇi daśatattvānitathā ca yogasādhanāvidheḥ pratipādanam ante kṛṣṇayamāritantram manīṣiṇaḥ kṛṣṇamāritantra vairocanakulasya deva ityāmananti mahākṛṣṇapādā akaniṣṭhabhuvane asya deśanā svīkurvanti  ācāryaśrīdharasya kathanamasti yad dharmadhātuvimānamaṇḍale sthirībhūya nirvāṇāvāptisamaye mārādibhirvighna utpādite mahāmāravijayasamādhisthaḥ  kṛṣṇayamārirūpeṇa prakaṭībhūya vajrapāṇyesya tantrasya deśanā kṛtavānakathayacca tvamapi evameva kṛṣṇayamārirūpeṇa prakaṭībhūya vighna vināśayetyuktvā  sa bṛhad kṛṣṇayamāritantramupadiṣṭavān punaśca vajrapāṇirapi  devasamūhamaṇḍaladevatādiyutasya kṛṣṇayamārisagrahatantrasya deśanā kṛtavān atra  paṭalāni santi yatra śrīdharasya pañjikāsahalokaḥratnākaraśāntipādasya pañjikāratnapradīpaḥ ratnāvalipadyapāṇyośca pañjikāḥ pramukhāḥ santi yamāritantrasya sādhanā bauddhetarepi prāpyate nāmasaṅgītiḥ nāmasaṅgītau mantravinyāsa parihāya pūrṇāḥ  ślokāḥ santi tibbatībhāṣāyāmanuśasāpi padye kṛtākintu saskṛte gadya eva prāptā bhavati nāmasaṅgītiḥ  bhāgeṣu vibhaktā yathā adhyeṣaṇā  ślokeṣuprativacana ṣaṭkulāvalokanam māyājālābhisambodhiḥ vajradhātumaṇḍalam suviśuddhadharmadhātumaṇḍalam ādarśajñānam pratyavekṣaṇajñānam suviśuddhadharmadhātumaṇḍalam ādarśajñānam pratyavekṣaṇajñānam samatājñānam kṛtyānuṣṭhānajñānam pañcatathāgatajñānastutiśca tathā cānte mantravinyāsaḥ anuśasāanumodanādīni  ślokeṣu pratibaddhāni santi koṅṭula rinapoche mahodayasya matamasti yad māyājālābhisambodheḥ ślokatrayam eva mūlatantramasti anye śeṣāḥ ślokāḥ tadvyākhyārūpeṇa pratipāditāḥ santi nāmasaṅgītitantrasya vidvadbhirvibhinnaparamparāsu vyākhyā kṛtā bodhisattvena kālacakraparamparāyālīlāvajreṇa anuttarapitṛtantraparamparāyāmañjuśrīkīrtimañjuśrī mitrābhyā yogatantraparamparāyāmasya vyākhyā kṛtā tibbate sarvaprathamamasya mahānanuvādo ratnabhadreṇa kṛtaḥ tadanantara mahānuvādonekaśo jātaḥ tibbate smṛtijñānata ārabhya ṅoga dharmavajraparyantamasya yogatantre vyākhyāyāḥ paramparā samāgatā āsīt maitrīpādato marapādharmamati yāvad anuttaratantre prāptā vyākhyāparamparā tibbatedyāpi vidyamānāsti asyānekaṭīkopaṭīkāḥ pariṣkarāgranthāḥ santi yatra raviśrīmahodayasya amṛtakaṇikānāma āryanāmasaṅgītiṭippaṇī vidyate anupamarakṣitasyāmṛtabindupratyālokavṛttiḥrājñaḥ puṇḍarīkasya hastabandhaḥ gītigānavidhiśca herūkakurūkullādyoḥ sādhanopāyikānidānavyavasthāmunimañjuśrīcaturdhārā jambhalatārācundāmahākālādīnā sādhanāabhiṣekaḥmūlāpattibhedaḥ samayanirdeśastathānte pārṣadadvārā bhagavataḥ stutiśca śrīmahāmudrātilakam atrāpi eva mayā śrutam  iti nāsti  yato hyasya deśanā mūlatantrasya pañcalakṣaślokātmakamadhyamamūlatantrasyānantara tasminneva maṇḍale guhyavajrayoginītantrasya mahāmudrātilakadvārā  mudraṇārtha kṛtāsīt  atra  paricchedāḥ santi yathā   tāntrikahetūnā paricchedāḥ ācāraśiṣyayoḥparīkṣā ābhiṣekaśca ṣaḍyogānā lakṣaṇa ṣaṭcakrāṇā svarūpa ca  ṣaṭcakreṣu sthitānā nāḍīnā sakhyānāmasthitayaścaprāṇarātridivāmadhyāntaraastaudayādīnā vidhiḥ ālikālyorūdbhavaḥ kālalakṣaṇatricittaprabhāsvaradharmadhātūnā vidhiḥālikālyorūdbhavaḥ kālalakṣaṇatricittaprabhāsvaradharmadhātūnā nirdeśaśca aha śabdasya vyutpattiḥ mātṛtantrasya nidānaguhyacaturānandāḥpañcakulānā lakṣaṇa ca  ṣaḍlaṅkārāḥ mudrāsaṅketaḥ mudrāpūjāvidhiśca  maṇḍaladevībāhyābhyantarapīṭhaśmaśānāni tatpūjāvidhiśca ābhyantaraparamārthahomaḥ pañcāmṛtarasapānamyoginīmelāpakasthāne prayogārhaguhyaśabdaḥ vāksaṅketaśca hastamudrā varṇagandhalakṣaṇādibhirdūtīkulaparīkṣā  devamaṇḍalānāmutpattikramaḥniṣpannakramaḥcaṇḍālībhāvanayā caturānandānām utpattividhiḥ tilakalakṣaṇamkramadvayasya bhāvanāvidhiḥ tilakajñānayoḥ sthānammūlacaryādiḥ bodhicittasya sthiratāyai dhyānanirdeśaḥ abhiṣekajñānam ālikālikāryakāraṇa nāḍītilakānandānā pratipādana ca  yogeśvaracaryā ghaṭacakrabījamantrayoḥ samuccayaḥ  pañcāmṛtabhakṣaṇacaryā balividhiścagaṇacakravidhiśca prāṇāyāmaḥmanomayajapaḥ prakṛtijapaścacaturyogānā  nāḍīgranthīnā ca nirdeśaḥ rahasyamantrasya prakaṭīkaraṇam mahāmudrāsaptajanmasevanadvārā sādhanāvidhiśca prāṇāyāmaḥ manomayajapaḥ prakṛtijapaśca mahāmudrāvabodhasyopāyaḥ catuṣpīṭhārthasya spaṣṭanirūpaṇa ca śrījñānagarbhamahāyogatantram devībhiḥ kṛte praśne śāstā tantrasyāsyopadeśa sumerūparvate cakre atra catuḥ paricchedāḥ santi prathameānandaparamānandaviramānandasahajānandānāmartha spaṣṭīkṛtavān dvitīyaparicchedemahāmudrātilake samāgatāyā mahāmudrāyāḥ prāptiupāyaprasaṅgataḥ caturabhiṣekāṇā prāptiḥālokaālokābhāsatathyajñānaprabhāsvarāṇāmarthāt mahāmudrāprāptividhirabhihitaḥtṛtīyaparicchedecaturabhiṣekeṣu maṇḍalabhedasya prāptividhirahitaḥ caturabhiṣekāṇā maṇḍalabhedaḥācāryalakṣaṇamśiṣyapraveśaḥ abhiṣekamaṇḍalayorarthaḥ prakaṭīṛtosti caturthaparicchedemaṇḍalābhisamaya tanmantrasamuccayopāya tathā sadguṇān spaṣṭīkṛtya śāstāntarhito jātaḥ  jñānatilakamahāyoginītantram  śāstā vajrayoṣidbhaga praviśya bodhisatvadevendra sambodhyāśrayanāḍīm āśritavāyorvastusthiratva tathā   ardhayāmānāmudayāstayoḥ sthiti vyaktavān   tritattvātmaka paramacandrasukhasya mahāmudrāpakṣasya ca nirdeśaḥ  nāḍīnā nāmānitantrakramānusāramabhiṣekavidhibhedaḥdakṣiṇārpaṇam rakṣācakrabhāvanāvidhiḥ mantrasamuccayaḥ bāhyābhyantarayajñavidhiḥ pūjāgītyorarthanirdeśaḥ catuḥ karmānusāra caturdhā homavidhiḥ gaṇacakravidhiḥ mahābaliyogalakṣaṇamguhyaśabdahastamudrāparicchedaśca aṣṭānanasya  bhujayuktasya herūkasya maṇḍalamabhisamayādiśca mantrajāpakramaḥ yajñaḥmaṇḍalam utpattikramaḥ pīṭhārthaḥ nāḍīcakramtatvārthaparicchedaśca  arthayāmeṣu tilakasya vilayopabhogauadhikṛtakramaḥ vāksaketaśca abhiṣekabhedaḥ caturānandānā bhedaḥabhiṣekanirūktiḥ abhiṣekavidhiśca homasya nītārthaḥvibhinnapūjāābhyantarahomavidhiśca balinītārthaḥ ālokābhāsāditrisattvānā savistaranirdeśaḥ  aṣṭānā śmaśānānā nītārthaḥ ābhyantaradhyānopagamaḥ jñānatilakasya parimāṇapīṭham  bhūmīnā nirdeśaśca gurūśiṣyayoḥ parīkṣā mūlatantrādīnā kramaḥ tantrasya nirūktiśca bhagavatīmahāmudrāyāḥ svarūpanirdeśaḥ  guhyārthasahajajñānasya nirdeśaḥ āyudhamaṇḍalalekhanavidhyādiḥ caturabhiṣekamaṇḍalasya bhedaḥcaturabhiṣekāṇā vidhiḥ āyudhamaṇḍalalekhanavidhiśca caturānandānā svarūpam tadutpattividhau vistṛtaprakāśaśca tattvasagrahaḥ herūkanirdeśaḥ cakrapāṇivyākaraṇamtaddvārātantravyākhyā tantrasagrahakartuḥ rūpe āgantu bhaviṣyavāṇīvajrapāṇeḥ svarūpasya vistaraśca pārṣadasya śāstuḥ praśasā ca ābhyantara ṣaḍvijñānapraśasā ceti viṣayān pradarśya granthaḥ sampadyate  siddhinirdeśatilakanāmatantra hṛdayatantramabhidhīyateyacca tibbatībhāṣāyāmanupalabdham  śrītattvapradīpaḥ śāstā prajñāpāramitānāmabhage sthirībhūya vajradhāraṇīśvara nidānaśabdasyārthāt eva mayā śrutam  ityasya nītārthavyākhyāmuktvā  kramaśaḥ jñānatilake samāgatānā  tattvānā bhūmīśvaracaryākālaabhiṣekabhedaacintyajñānaabhiṣekārthaābhāsādi caturjñānānā prakṛtyādeśca  varṇana karoti  buddhakapālaḥ buddhakapālasya deśanā cakrapāṇinā niveditā prajñāpāramitā karoti atra  paricchedāḥ santi  tantranāmasiddhisagrahaḥjñānāveśaḥnidānacaitadviṣayaiḥ prathamaparicchedaḥ samāpti bhajate  śravaṇārthopadeśaḥ bhasmasevanena vibhinnakarmayogasya pratipādanam  herūkasya navadevamaṇḍalānāmutpattiḥ abhiṣekavidhiśca sārikāyogaḥmaṇḍalānā lekhanaśiṣyāvatāraṇāabhiṣekaḥ sārikāyogavistāravidhiśca  dravyarasāyanavāksaṅketaḥ  chomā bhadrauṣadhyādiḥ prajñādharmodayamaṇḍale śiṣyasyābhiṣekamaṇḍalavisarjanam  herūkena saha  devamaṇḍalānā lekhana tadutpattividhiśca catuḥkarmaṇā homavidhiḥ caryāparicchedaḥ pārasavidhiḥ bandhyātaḥ santānotpattyādiḥ garūḍamaṇḍalalekhanaśiṣyābhiṣekadvārā vidyādharapadasya prajñaptividhiḥ ajanakhaḍgādibhirvibhinnakarmasādhana mudrānandābhyā cittaśuddhiḥ  vajrapāṇipārṣadānā mātuḥ stutiritiviṣayanirūpaṇena mantrajāpavajrajāpaprajñāmātṛdevyabhyarthanādividhinā ca saha tantramida samāpti  gacchati  mahāmāyatantram asya prārambhe  eva mayā śrutamiti nāstiyato hi anuttaramahāyānaparamparānusāra bhagavato mahāparinirvāṇasya prāpteramānyatvāt bhagavān loke satata sthitosti ataḥ sagrahakartrā granthoya sagṛhīto nāsti ittha keṣācid viduṣā mānyatā vidyate tibbatīyāḥ kecana vidvāsaḥ mahāmāyāyāḥ prathama maṅgalācaraṇīya ślokadvaya gurūkukurīpādena racitamityāmananti atra paricchedatrayamasti prathamaparicchede mahāmāyāyāstattvanirdeśapūrvaka tat prakṛtipārthivafalaparyantafalānā viśeṣamārgasya ca nirūpaṇamālikāli ityādi mantraḥ dharmayogaḥ guṭikāsādhanaśukrākṛṣṭiḥ piṇḍākṛṣṭiḥ candrapānāderguṇaḥ siddhilakṣaṇādīnā nirdeśaḥ kṛtosti dvitīya paricchede vyākhyāyāḥ pratijñākaraṇānantara vajrajāpaḥ triyogaguṇaḥadhikāraprāptiḥ śukrākṛṣṭiḥ hayagrīvadvārā raktākṛṣṭiḥsūryacandrasampuṭasasthānayogasyābhyāsaḥamṛtadvārā guhyābhiṣeka nirdeśapaṭala ca vartate tṛtīyāricchede amṛtaguṭikāsādhanopāyikā ca devīdvārā gīticodana samāpattibhāvanāyā guṇaśceti viṣayāṇā tathā guhyopacaryādīnā nirūpaṇena saha tṛtīyaparicchedo viramati  rigiāralitantram śāstā rigirūpe sthito bhūtvā āralinā pīṭhopapīṭhādīnā viṣaye kṛte praśne pīṭhamaṇḍaladevanyāsavidhyādīnā deśanā karoti yaśca prathamāraliyogaparicchedosti dvitīyaparicchedemaṇḍalaparisare narakalokasya lekhana nyāsakaraṇasya prayojanavṛṣṭividhiḥ kṛṣṭāvṛṣṭividhiḥ svarakṣā ceti viṣayāṇām abhiṣekakramādyutpattikramikāvayavānā nirdeśena saha sarvakarmasagrahanidānaparivartanāmako dvitīyaparicchedaḥ pūrṇo  bhavati  tṛtīyaparicchedepīṭhādīnā svaśarīre nyāsakaraṇasya saketita eva mayā śrtam ityasya vyākhyā caturbhūtapratipādanateṣā saketādiparicchedaḥ devanyāsaḥ svadehasya buddharūpatvena pratipāana ca  pavitrakhādyādīnā nirmāṇa ceti hṛdayopahṛdayasamayābhiṣekayorlakṣaṇanirdeśādinā granthasamāptirbhavati vajrāralināmatantram  śāstā pāramitānāmake bhage pratiṣṭhāya vajrapāṇaye devābhisamaya deśayate yaśca prathamaparicchedasyābhidheyosti atra  paricchedāḥ santi   pārṣadaiḥ balimadhikṛtya praśne kṛte balividhiparicchedaḥ  samayaḥsavaraḥ abhiṣekahomaḥ maṇḍalalekhanavidhiparicchedaḥ  abhijñāsādhanopāyikāparicchedaḥ   vajrapūjāparicchedaḥ  samayagurūśiṣyalakṣaṇaparicchedaḥ  caryāvetālasādhanopāyikāparicchedaḥ  pārṣadadvārā paramapada prāpya līlācaryāparicchedaḥ   tantraguṇaśceti viṣayeṇa praśasāyogavidhinirdeśena ca saha granthaḥ sampanno bhavati  kecana vidvāsa etad hevajrasya sabhāgīyatantramurarīkurvate vairocanakulam catuṣpīṭhatantra vairocanakulasya mūlatantramasti atra pīṭhacatuṣṭaya  paricchedāśca santi asya deśanā sarvajñena sumerūparvate kṛtā atra  eva mayā śruta  iti nāyāti yato hyaya mūladvādaśasāhasrikāyāḥ sagrahatantragranthosti svapīṭhaḥ parapīṭhaḥ yogapīṭhaguhyapīṭhādiśca granthasyāsyābhidheyosti pratyeka pīṭhe catvāraḥ paricchedāḥ santi  vajrapāṇinā tantradeśanārtha vinayaḥśāstrā śravaṇārtha cāpramādena vāyutattvavāyuparīkṣayā lagna kālayoganiṣkramaṇārtha jyotiṣaśāstramkālayogenalagnena falitajyotiṣaśāstramlagnotpattiparīkṣāvidhiḥ lagnena siddhiparīkṣālagnasajñāahorātraghaṭikāsakhyā ceti viṣayāṇā śubhāśubhanirṇayādiviṣayāṇā ca pratipādana svapīṭhasya prathamaparicchede vartate  mṛtyuvacanārakṣācakramnāgaviṣacikitsāvṛṣṭyutpādanadūtīlakṣaṇādiviṣayāṇā vivecana dvitīyaparicchede vartate  utpattikramasya prārambhiko dharmaḥ sarvadharmāṇā śūnyatābhāvanāsiddhilakṣaṇaparīkṣādevabhāvanāvidhyādīnā nirūpaṇa tṛtīyaparicchede vartate devayogaḥ devabījanyāsaḥ jñānḍākinībhāvanāsūkṣmayogaḥmantrajāpaścetaiḥ mudrādābhiśca prathamapīṭhaḥ sampadyate dvitīyapīṭhe  śiṣyaparīkṣā japahomavidhiḥ mudrāsahitā jñānaḍākinī devasādhanopāyikābalilakṣaṇa pūjā viśatyāḥ kṣetrapālapūjāvidhiḥguhyapūjāanuttarapūjāmagalagītiḥpraṇidhāna devavisarjana ca  pañcamāsapañcāmṛtādhiṣṭhānamālikāliprajñopāyayogaḥpañcākuśaadhiṣṭhānabaliḥ yoginīsādhanāyā vāṅmudrayoḥ saketaśca tṛtīyapāṭhe vidyate  vajraḥ ghaṇṭāmālā jñānatattva pañca jagattattvāni ca yogapīṭhasya prathamaparicchede vartante  tārācakrasādhanopāyikācaturdhārāvistāraḥjñānaḍākinīprajñāvṛttiḥ vairocanasādhanopāyikā jñānāveśaḥ uccāṭanamākarṣaṇambandhanādiḥ śāntikarmayogaśca  vajraghaṇṭātattvamprajñopāyaprayogaḥkarmānusāra mudrābhedaḥprayopāyasya pārthakyāt siddhiprāpteḥ abhāvanirdeśaḥviṣayacaryāpraśasāḍākinīkrodhādīnā karmasamūhaśca caturthapāṭhe gurūgaṇaḥ tallakṣaṇakriyayoḥ kramaḥ śiṣyamaṇḍalāvataraṇābhiṣekaḥsamayanirdeśaśca prathamaparicchedasya viṣayaḥ  nirlakṣaṇadhyāna tatsādhanopāyikākumbhakayogadvārā amṛtapānaguhyahomādiśca dvitīyaparicchede vartate  kāyabhūtalakṣaṇa teṣā vijñāne layavidhiḥvāyuyogasakramaṇopadeśaḥ ābhyantarakarmayoganāmakastṛtīyaḥ pariccheosti  caṇḍālīyogaḥ anubhūtilakṣaṇaviśuddhadevaḥ sādhanāsthalarasāyanādyupāyānām anukaraṇārtha kṛtāyā preraṇāyā pārṣadena jñānamupalabhya gītighoṣakaraṇamante tantraśāstragrahaṇaguṇa  prakaṭayan granthoya samāpti bhajate  vajrasūryakulam vajrāmṛtatantramida vajrasūryakulasya mukhyo granthosti atra  paricchedāḥ santi  vajrāmṛtadhyānamaṇḍalalekhanavidhiḥ bhāvanāvidhiḥ guhyamaṇḍalanirdeśaśca prathamaparicchede nirdiṣṭaḥ  tattvajñānayogavistāravidhiśca dvitīyaparicchede nirūpitaḥ  mantrasamuccayastṛtīyaparicchede  vartate   homavidhiścaturthaparicchede nirdiṣṭaḥ ajānādiyogavidhiḥ pañcamaparicchede nirūpitaḥ hūkāramaṇḍalopāyaḥ gītinṛtyaabhiṣekatattvāni ca saptamaparicchede niradiśyanta  herūkamaṇḍalasya nirūpaṇamaṣṭamaparicchede kṛtam  amṛtakuṇḍalīmaṇḍalasya nirdeśaḥ navamaparicchede vihitaḥ  vetālasādhanopāyikā daśamaparicchede pradarśitā  pañcāmṛtasādhanayā saha mahātantropatantrasagrahādernirdeśaḥ kṛtosti ekādaśaparicchede padyanarteśvarakulam kulalokanātha pañcadaśaka nāma āmnāye tantrasya mahattvammantrasamuccayopāyaḥjapopāyaḥmantratattvasya vyākhyātilakayogaḥ sūkṣmayogaḥ guṇasya vyākhyāsahajānandasvarūpalokeśvarapadaprāptiḥ catussādhanāṅgānā saguṇatatvavyākhyāśāntiākarṣaṇauccāṭanādivibhinnakarmasādhanopāyikāvajrajāpaḥtilakayogaḥ māraṇayogaḥ caṇḍālīyogastathā devatattvayogavyākhyādayosya granthasyābhidheyāḥ santi paramāśvakulam namastāre saguṇaikaviśatistotrasya raviguptādibhirvidvadbhiḥ anuttaratantrasya sādhanāpaddhatyanusāra vyākhyā kṛtā maṇḍale mṛṇmayakāyamaṇḍalayorvyavasthā kṛtā vajrakālamahākālāditantrāṇi bustonosminneva kule sthāpitavān vajradharakulam yathālabdhakhasamatantre pañca paricchedāḥ santi  vajradharasya svarūpamdevatattvasamayaśca cittotpattidvārā cittamaṇḍalam vāgdvārā vāṅmaṇḍalam kāyotpattidvārā kāyamaṇḍalam anyatantraiḥ sahoktābhidheyasya sāmānyataḥ spaṣṭīkaraṇa kṛtamasti advayatantrasyābhyudayaḥ kālacakratantramkālacakrasya deśanā śāstā svaya kālacakrarūpe prakaṭībhūya dhānyakaṭake ākarṣīt kālacakrasya mūlatantramanupalabdham kecanāśā uddharaṇeṣūpalabhyante tantrasagrahoya pañcapaṭaleṣu vibhajyate yathā dhātupaṭalamadhyātmapaṭalamabhiṣekapaṭalamsādhanāpaṭalamjñānapaṭala ceti eṣu pañcapaṭaleṣu aneke viṣayāḥ santi sagṛhītāḥ ye  śīrṣakeṣu vibhaktāḥ  dhātupaṭalam dhātupaṭale  ślokāḥ santi prathamaśloke tantranidānasya nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ dvitīyaśloke kālacakravyākhyānārtha pratijñā svīkāroktiśca vidyate tṛtīyaśloke tantrarahasyārthamahāśūnyapañcākṣaraṣaḍakṣarādīnā saketo vihitaḥ ebhiḥ padyaiḥ kālatantrābhidheyasya sārāśaḥ sagṛhītaḥ anyaiḥ ślokaiḥ paṭalaiśca eteṣā ślokānāmeva vistṛtavyākhyā kṛtā lokadhātupaṭale sagrahacatuṣṭayamasti  lokadhātusagraheṇa lokadhātornītārthaḥ  jagadbhavasagraheṇa jagatparimāṇam  jyotiṣasagraheṇa nakṣatra jyautiṣa graha nakṣatrāṇām ākāśe gamanavidhiḥ  svarodayena yantrasagraheṇa ca falitajyotiṣakuśalākuśalaparīkṣāśatrunāśavidhiḥ   cakravartinā mlecchadharmotsādanametaiḥ  pañcakadvīpasya dvādaśabhāgeṣu cakravartirāja āgamanādinirdeśena ca saha prathamapaṭalasya samāptirjāyate adhyātmapaṭalam prathamaślokaḥ abhyarthanāvyākhyayoḥ svīkārokteḥ vartate   paṭalesmin  ślokāḥ saptasagrahasamūhaścāsti  kāyavākcittodbhavaduḥkhasamudayanirodhamārganirdeśasagrahādibhiḥ garbhāvasthāyā śukraśoṇitayormelanādārabhya buddhiprāpti yāvat kāyasya  sampannatāvidhiḥ  samudayasatyasagraheṇa sampannakāye nāḍīvāyutilakānā yathāsthitividhiḥ  cakravartimlecchakālacakrakulasantatyādayaḥ udbhūtasagraheṇa kāye bāhyābhyantaraparadharmāṇām abhinnatāyāḥ pūrṇanirdeśaḥ  nāḍīuccheda  kṣaya  mṛtyulakṣaṇasagraheṇa sampannakāyasya mṛtyusūcanā nirdeśaḥ  jagadutpādanirodhahetubhūtam ekakṣaṇalakṣaṇa  kālacakranirdeśasagraheṇa  mṛtyunirdeśaḥ rasāyanādiḥ  niyatabālasantatisagraheṇa mṛtyulakṣaṇa mṛtyuhetu ca jñātvā mṛtyorūparyutthānasya vidhiḥ  svaparadarśanayormīmāsayā samyaṅmārge praveśavidhiśceti dvitīyādhyātmapaṭale nyarūpyanta abhiṣekapaṭalam prathamaḥ ślokaḥ pūrvapaṭalānusāreṇa abhyarthanāyā vyākhyānokteśca vartate atra sapta sagrahāḥ
